93:                <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 1.B.6.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span>   Except for the minimum two aircraft wet leasing referred to above, during the bid periods described in this paragraph, the Company shall not wet lease more than the net gain of trunk aircraft scheduled to be added and brought into service in any calendar year. Should, at the end of the calendar year, the Company actually bring into service fewer trunk aircraft than were scheduled and based on the schedule, the Company wet leased more aircraft than would have been permitted if the scheduled additions were the same as the actual deliveries, then the Company shall pay to the Association the same monies it would have paid the Association as calculated under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_1B6a">Section 1.B.6.a.</a></p>
108:              <p>Should the parent of the Company (FedEx Corp.) or any subsidiary or Affiliate directly or indirectly controlled by the parent of the Company acquire with the intention of retaining and operating a U.S. certificated air carrier or air operation operating aircraft of over 60,000 lbs. MTOGW, then the acquired carrier’s routes and operation of aircraft above the MTOGW of 60,000 lbs. shall be assumed by the pilots on the FedEx Master Seniority List. If the acquired airline is to be sold in the normal course of business, these seniority-merger provisions do not apply. If FedEx Corp., its subsidiaries or Affiliates retain and operate the acquired airline, the assumption of the acquired flying by Federal Express Master Seniority List pilots shall take place as soon as reasonably practical after either the merger of the acquired carrier’s appropriate pilots (those flying aircraft over 60,000 lbs.) into the Federal Express Master Seniority List in the manner set forth in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_1D3">Section 1.D.3.</a>, or in the event the pilots from the acquired carrier are not intended to be retained, then upon the final regulatory confirmation and transfer of the operating certificates to Federal Express and/or FedEx Corp.</p>
113:              <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 1.D.2." rel="tooltip">2.</span> This agreement shall be binding upon any successor, including without limitation, any assignee, purchaser, transferee, administrator, receiver, executor, and/or trustee of the Company (hereinafter referred to as a “Successor” to the Company). Neither the Company nor its Affiliates shall consummate a Successor transaction unless the Successor agrees in writing, in advance of executing an agreement to consummate such transaction and as an irrevocable condition of the Successorship transaction, to assume and be bound by the Agreement, to recognize the Association as the representative of the Federal Express pilots and to guarantee that the pilots on the Federal Express Pilots’ Master Seniority List will be employed by the Successor in accordance with the provisions of this Agreement. The Successor shall continue to recognize the Association in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_1A">Section 1.A.</a> unless and until the National Mediation Board transfers or extinguishes the Association’s certification following an operational merger. The Successor shall continue to be bound by the Agreement until the terms of the Agreement are modified in accordance with applicable law.</p>

1732:      <p id="link_4A2cv" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.A.2.c.v." rel="tooltip">v.</span> In any bid period when the average BLG is less than 64 CHs (81 in a 5 week bid period, or 96 in a 6 week bid period) in a crew position, the Company shall construct reserve lines in that crew position with a minimum of 1 less reserve day than allowed per <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25D3">Section 25.D.3.</a> In any bid period when the average BLG is less than 59 CHs (76 in a 5 week bid period, or 92 in a 6 week bid period) in a crew position, the Company shall construct reserve lines in that crew position with a minimum of 2 less reserve days than allowed per <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25D3">Section 25.D.3.</a> For purposes of this paragraph, the calculation of BLG for a crew position shall not include lines that are more than 16 CH (20 CH in a 5 week bid period, or 25 CH in a 6 week bid period) greater than the lowest paid regular line, system wide;</p>

1742:    <p id="link_4A4" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.A.4." rel="tooltip">4.</span>   When a pilot returns to active pay status during a bid period for which he was not awarded a bid line (e.g., <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25I1a">Section 25.I.1.a.</a>, Custom lines), his minimum bid period guarantee shall be prorated based on the number of days in which the pilot is in active pay status during that bid period.</p>
1743:    <p id="link_4A5" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.A.5." rel="tooltip">5.</span>   A new hire pilot covered by <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_3A">Section 3.A.</a> shall not have a minimum bid period guarantee. When he is activated into his first crew position following initial new hire training, his minimum bid period guarantee shall be prorated based upon the number of days in the bid period following his activation.</p>

1752:        <p id="link_4A6cii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.A.6.c.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>  Carry-in CH and activities removed due to vacation, count toward MLV. Recurrent training pay does not count towards MLV, except where designated in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25E4biv">Section 25.E.4.b.iv.</a> for secondary line awardees.</p>
1761:          <p id="link_4A6ciiib" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.A.6.c.iii.(b)." rel="tooltip">(b)</span>    If the application of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4A6ciiia">Section 4.A.6.c.iii.(a)</a> does not result in an MLV-compliant line (e.g., not enough CH dropped, submission for dropping activities over holiday, no combination of activities that meet the MLV drop range), the Company shall drop activities, as necessary, to bring his line within the MLV drop range. If it is not possible to drop activities that bring a pilot’s line within the MLV drop range, then activities shall be dropped to bring the pilot’s line below MLV by the least amount possible. If the only means of bringing a pilot’s line below MLV is to drop a trip or activity scheduled in whole or in part on the following days: New Year’s Eve, New Year’s Day, Thanksgiving Day, Christmas Eve or Christmas Day; whether to drop that activity shall be at the Company’s discretion.</p>
1763:            carry-in conflicts and shall be eligible for phase-in make up, subject to the limitation contained in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4A6ciiid">Section 4.A.6.c.iii.(d).</a> The pilot shall be notified of all trips dropped due to MLV.</p>
1773:  <p>A pilot who is awarded a regular line shall have a BLG equal to the total of the trip guarantees for all trips on the line, excluding that portion of the CH of a carryover trip allocated to the next bid period as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4G">Section 4.G.</a> Prior to any adjustments, however, a BLG shall not be less than the minimum bid period guarantee as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4A1">Section 4.A.1.</a> If the sum of trip guarantees for trips on a pilot’s regular line is less than the minimum bid period guarantee, such pilot’s BLG shall be increased to the minimum bid period guarantee.</p>
1777:  <p>A pilot who is awarded a reserve line shall have an RLG equal to the value of an R-day multiplied by the number of R-days scheduled on a reserve line for the bid period package (i.e., up to a maximum of 15, 19, or 23 days). The value of an R-day shall be determined by dividing 96% of the average BLG for regular lines published in the bid period package by the number of R-days scheduled on a reserve line for the bid period package and then rounding that amount to the nearest minute. Prior to any adjustments, however, an RLG shall not be less than the minimum bid period guarantee as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4A1">Section 4.A.1.</a></p>
1785:    <p id="link_4D3" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.D.3." rel="tooltip">3.</span>   CH earned in reserve status in excess of a pilot’s mini-RLG shall be paid in addition to his BLG as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4H7">Section 4.H.7.</a> (100% up to RLG, 150% for CH over RLG).</p>
1793:    <p id="link_4E1a" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.E.1.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   A secondary line comprised entirely of trips shall have a BLG computed as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4B">Section 4.B.</a></p>
1794:    <p id="link_4E1b" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.E.1.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span>   A secondary line comprised of trips and R-days shall have a BLG equal to the sum of the trip guarantees (for trips scheduled on the line) and R-day values (for R-days scheduled on the line). Prior to any adjustments, however, the BLG shall not be less than the minimum bid period guarantee (as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4A1">Section 4.A.1.</a>). The CH of a carryover trip shall be allocated between bid periods as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4G">Section 4.G.</a> The CH of a carryover R-day(s) shall be allocated to the subsequent bid period.</p>
1795:    <p id="link_4E1c" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.E.1.c." rel="tooltip">c.</span>   A secondary line comprised entirely of R-days shall have an RLG computed as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4C">Section 4.C.</a></p>
1801:    <p id="link_4E3a" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.E.3.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   If a pilot is assigned a custom line (as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25I">Section 25.I.</a>), and he does not otherwise have a BLG/RLG for the bid period, he shall have a BLG/RLG for his custom line computed as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4B">Section 4.B.</a>, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4C">C.</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4E1b">E.1.b.</a>, as applicable. Prior to any adjustments, however, the minimum bid period guarantee shall not be less than the minimum BLG/RLG prorated as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4A4">Section 4.A.4.</a></p>
1802:    <p id="link_4E3b" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.E.3.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span>   If a pilot is assigned a custom line (as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25I">Section 25.I.</a>), and he has a BLG/RLG for the bid period (e.g., pay only line), his BLG/RLG for the bid period shall be the greater of his original BLG/RLG or the BLG/RLG for his assigned custom line computed as provided in Section 4.E.3.a.</p>
1868:  <p>A secondary line holder with carryover R-days may designate the amount of his carryover R-day CH to be applied toward the new bid period’s BLG or RLG, as applicable. The default setting shall be 0 (zero) CH applied toward the new bid period’s BLG/RLG. Such designation shall be made during the monthly View/Add window, as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25E4biii">Section 25.E.4.b.iii.</a></p>
1871:    <p id="link_4G3a" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.G.3.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   The total credit hour value of a carryover trip shall be computed as a single trip as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4F">Section 4.F.</a> (Trip Guarantee).</p>
1886:      <p>If the carryover trip was not a reserve trip, then a secondary line holder may designate the amount of his carryover CH to be applied toward the new bid period’s BLG or RLG, as applicable. If the secondary or custom line holder has a mini-RLG, his designated carryover CH shall not be credited toward mini-RLG or leveling. The default setting shall be 0 (zero) CH applied toward the new bid period’s BLG/RLG. Such designation shall be made during the monthly View/Add window, as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25E4biii">Section 25.E.4.b.iii.</a></p>
1894:      <p>If the carryover trip was a reserve trip, a secondary line holder shall be afforded the same designation opportunity and default as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4G3biii">Section 4.G.3.b.iii.</a> above. If the secondary line holder has a BLG with mini-RLG in the second bid period, his carryover R-days shall be added to the mini-RLG for the second bid period. His designated carryover CH, if any, shall be credited toward mini-RLG and leveling.</p>
1909:      <p id="link_4H1biv" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.H.1.b.iv." rel="tooltip">iv.</span>    is removed from the reserve assignment for sick leave in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_14B5b">Section 14.B.5.b.</a> (Sick Leave).</p>

1939:  <p id="link_4H9" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.H.9." rel="tooltip">9.</span> A reserve pilot who voluntarily accepted a reserve assignment that was scheduled to extend beyond the end of his block of R-days shall have that portion of that trip that extended beyond his scheduled block of R-days compensated at 150% in addition to RLG. The calculation of the portion of his trip to be compensated at 150% shall be done in the same manner as a carryover trip, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4G3bia">Section 4.G.3.b.i.(a).</a></p>

1962:    <p id="link_4I4a" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.I.4.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   If a pilot’s recurrent training is scheduled other than as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25C12diiib">Section 25.C.12.d.iii.(b)</a>, the following shall apply:</p>
1965:      <p id="link_4I4aii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.I.4.a.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    If a pilot is awarded/assigned recurrent training in conflict with a trip or block of R-days, his pay shall be handled as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4I1a">Section 4.I.1.a.</a> (phase-in conflicts). If the pilot’s recurrent training conflicts with a block of R-days, the entire block shall be dropped as a phase-in conflict and the pilot shall not be responsible for any of the R-days in that block.</p>
1966:      <p id="link_4I4aiii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.I.4.a.iii." rel="tooltip">iii.</span>   If a pilot receiving recurrent training is removed from a trip(s) to protect minimum scheduled days off, his pay shall be handled as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4I1b">Section 4.I.1.b.</a></p>
1968:    <p id="link_4I4b" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.I.4.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span> If a secondary line holder is scheduled for recurrent training other than as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25C12diiib">Section 25.C.12.d.iii.(b)</a>, he shall designate whether or not his recurrent training credit hours (4:30 CH for each such day) are to be counted toward his BLG/RLG. The default setting shall be for those credit hours not to count toward his BLG/RLG. Such designation shall be made during the View/Add window.</p>

1971:      <p id="link_4I4ci" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.I.4.c.i." rel="tooltip">i.</span> If a pilot is removed from a trip(s) for which he has trip guarantee, due to a conflict with recurrent training, he shall earn the trip guarantee for that trip(s). 1975:        <p id="link_4I4ciiia" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.I.4.c.iii.(a)." rel="tooltip">(a)</span>  if no trip was removed due to recurrent training or minimum days off, the pilot shall be compensated 4:30 CH per day, in addition to BLG/RLG, except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4I7">Section 4.I.7.</a></p>

1989:    <p id="link_4I5a" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.I.5.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   A pilot in ITU training for an upgrade award or as a result of a crew position assignment shall earn a minimum of his BLG/RLG, adjusted as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4I1">Section 4.I.1.</a> (Phase-In Conflict), excluding carryover CH. If he does not have a BLG/RLG (e.g., returning from a leave of absence), he shall be assigned a prorated RLG (4 days of work for every 7 days available) for his crew position based on the number of days he is in active pay status during the remainder of the bid period.</p>
2001:    <p id="link_4I6a" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.I.6.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   If a pilot receiving requalification training does not hold a pay only line, pay for requalification training shall be as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4I4">Section 4.I.4.</a> (recurrent training pay), or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4I5">I.5.</a> (ITU training pay), whichever is applicable based on the extent of the training necessary to accomplish requalification.</p>

2013:    <p id="link_4I7a" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.I.7.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   If a pilot incurs a training failure, he shall continue to receive compensation as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4I4">Section 4.I.4.</a>, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4I5">I.5.</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4I6">I.6.</a> (recurrent, ITU or requalification training) as applicable, except that he shall not be compensated for any subsequent training on a scheduled day off.</p>
2018:    <p>A pilot removed from a trip(s) or R-day(s), as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25Z">Section 25.Z</a>. (Bereavement Absence), shall be compensated for the portion of such activities in actual conflict with the bereavement absence as follows:</p>
2061:  <p id="link_4L1" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.L.1." rel="tooltip">1.</span> A pilot’s substitution guarantee shall be the sum of all CH earned in substitution status (i.e., availability credits, airport hold credits, substitution base standby credits and pay for a substitution trip). A pilot shall earn trip guarantee for a substitution trip only if he blocks out on such trip. As provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H3bii">Section 25.H.3.b.ii.</a>, if a pilot’s substitution window is greater than 72 hours, and the pilot chooses not to remain eligible for substitution at 4 hours after showtime of the trip that caused substitution eligibility, he shall be paid 18 CH toward trip guarantee and is eligible for OTP for the balance of trip guarantee.</p>
2064:    <p id="link_4L2s" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.L.2.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   If the pilot accepts all substitution assignments and fulfills all availability requirements (as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H3">Section 25.H.3.</a>), he shall earn the greater of the trip guarantee for the original trip or substitution guarantee, provided, however, that a pilot shall not earn more than the trip guarantee for his original trip unless the value of the substitution assignments he performs (i.e., trips, standbys and airport holds) is greater than original trip guarantee; or</p>
2066:    <p id="link_4L2c" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.L.2.c." rel="tooltip">c.</span>   If the pilot accepts a reassignment trip, he shall earn reassignment trip pay as determined by <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H10">Section 25 H.10.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4M">Section 4.M.</a>; or</p>
2067:    <p id="link_4L2d" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.L.2.d." rel="tooltip">d.</span>   If the pilot enters OTP, he shall earn compensation as determined by <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4N">Section 4.N.</a>; and</p>
2070:  <p id="link_4L3" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.L.3." rel="tooltip">3.</span> If a pilot initially eligible for substitution remains available as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H3b">Section 25.H.3.b.</a> through H.3.e., (availability periods), he shall receive 6 CH toward his substitution guarantee for each availability period if:</p>
2074:    <p id="link_4L3c" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.L.3.c." rel="tooltip">c.</span>   the availability period was not entirely contained within the 72 hours in which no substitution assignment can begin as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H3bii">Section 25.H.3.b.ii.</a></p>
2078:  <p id="link_4L6" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.L.6." rel="tooltip">6.</span> If a pilot is eligible for substitution due to recurrent training, the recurrent training pay provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4I4ciii">Section 4.I.4.c.iii.</a> shall be credited toward his substitution guarantee.</p>
2103:  <p id="link_4O1" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.O.1." rel="tooltip">1.</span> A pilot on base airport or base hotel standby shall be guaranteed an R-day value, except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4O2">Section 4.O.2.</a> below.</p>
2104:  <p id="link_4O2" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.O.2." rel="tooltip">2.</span> If a pilot eligible for substitution is assigned a base standby (as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H5d">Section 25.H.5.d.</a>), and does not block-out on a trip, he shall be credited with 6 CH towards his substitution guarantee. If he blocks out on a trip, he shall be compensated the greater of trip guarantee for such trip or substitution availability credit.</p>
2128:  <p id="link_4Q1" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.Q.1." rel="tooltip">1.</span> Except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C2ciii">Section 12.C.2.c.iii.</a> (taxi/air turn back to base), and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_8C1fiii">Section 8.C.1.f.iii.</a> (deviation trip schedule change), if a pilot blocks out on a VLT/DRF trip, he shall earn trip guarantee at 150% of his normal pay rate and overage, if any, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4BB">Section 4.BB.</a> Such compensation shall be in addition to BLG/RLG.</p>
2138:  <p id="link_4Q5" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.Q.5." rel="tooltip">5.</span> A pilot who is removed from a VLT or DRF trip after block-out due to sick leave shall be compensated at 150% of his normal pay rate for such trip. The CH charged to sick leave (as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_14B5">Section 14.B.5.</a>) shall be charged at 150%.</p>
2139:  <p id="link_4Q6" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.Q.6." rel="tooltip">6.</span> For purposes of this Section, the provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4Q1">Section 4.Q.1.</a> through 4.Q.5. apply for a pilot assigned a CMU trip.</p>
2144:  <p id="link_4R1" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.R.1." rel="tooltip">1.</span> If a pilot in field emergency pay status departs his location to position for the trip, or blocks out on the revenue portion of a trip, he shall earn trip guarantee at 150% of his normal pay rate. He shall be reimbursed for expenses incurred in positioning, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_5A7">Section 5.A.7.</a> (authorized expenses), by submission of an expense report (a field emergency pilot’s trip shall be constructed as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25R">Section 25.R.</a> in order to establish a credit hour value for the trip).</p>

2171:      <p>1:30 CH for each duty period in which one or more of the disruptions described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25S2b">Section 25.S.2.b.</a> occurs.</p>
2175:      <p>1:30 CH per trip for disruptions described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25S2c">Section 25.S.2.c.</a></p>
2179:      <p>1:30 CH for each flight in which a pilot who was awarded/assigned a crew designation as a Standard Crew member, and is assigned and operates as a Relief Pilot, or vice versa, as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25S2d">Section 25.S.2.d.</a></p>

2191:  <p id="link_4W3" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.W.3." rel="tooltip">3.</span> Except for the disruption due to a deadhead at the end of a trip being revised to operate, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25S2bii">Section 25.S.2.b.ii.</a>, a disruption(s) is not payable based on events that occurred during a duty period that qualifies for extra duty period pay, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4Y">Section 4.Y.</a></p>

2200:  <p id="link_4Y2" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.Y.2." rel="tooltip">2.</span> If a duty period qualifies for extra duty period pay, no disruptions (except for the disruption due to a deadhead at the end of a trip being revised to operate, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25S2bii">Section 25.S.2.b.ii.</a>), are payable based on events that occurred during that duty period.</p>

2241:      <p id="link_4BB3cii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.BB.3.c.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    If the pilot does not elect the option in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4BB3ci">Section 4.BB.3.c.i.</a>, the subsequent trip shall be removed with pay and the pilot shall be eligible for substitution.</p>
2248:    <p id="link_4BB4c" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.BB.4.c." rel="tooltip">c.</span>   If the pilot does not elect the option in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4BB4b">Section 4.BB.4.b.</a>, the subsequent trip shall be removed with pay (as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4L">Section 4.L.</a>), and the pilot shall be eligible for substitution. If the removed trip was a substitution trip, that trip shall not be credited towards the pilot’s substitution guarantee and the pilot shall remain eligible for substitution. His entitlement to trip guarantee for his original trip shall not be affected.</p>
2283:  <p>This paragraph applies to all international trips except for international trips constructed under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1b">Section 12.D.1.b.</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1c">c.</a></p>

2288:    <p id="link_4EE1c" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 4.EE.1.c." rel="tooltip">c.</span>   A pilot received more than 4 “not adjusted” rests in a row. Each rest after 3 non-adjusted rests shall be a separate GPE event. An initial GPE occurs when the pilot’s fifth duty period begins without the pilot having received at least 18 hours free from duty preceding the beginning of that duty period. For purposes of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4EE1c">Section 4.EE.1.c.</a>, only, an unassigned hotel standby period shall be counted as part of the rest periods preceding and/or following it (e.g., an unassigned 11:30 hotel standby period, followed by a 12:30 rest period will be counted as an adjusted rest).</p>
2291:    <p>If a pilot’s trip did not conform to 30-in-120 (as set forth in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D2g">Section 12.D.2.g.</a>, except using 30 instead of 32 hours), he shall be paid 3 CH in addition to all other compensation regardless of the 48-hour period as stated in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4EE3">Section 4.EE.3.</a>, and the event shall be additive to the total count of GPEs for the trip.</p>
2293:    <p>If a pilot’s trip did not conform to 34-in-168 (as set forth in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D2g">Section 12.D.2.g.</a>, except using 34 instead of 36 hours), he shall be paid 3 CH in addition to all other compensation regardless of the 48-hour period as stated in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4EE3">Section 4.EE.3.</a>, and the event shall be additive to the total count of GPEs for the trip.</p>

2335:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 5.A.6." rel="tooltip">6.</span> Except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_8C3e">Section 8.C.3.e.</a>, per diem shall be paid to a pilot who deviates as if he had flown the trip as scheduled.</p>
2336:  <p id="link_5A7" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 5.A.7." rel="tooltip">7.</span> The Company shall reimburse a pilot for authorized reasonable expenses not covered by <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_5A3">Section 5.A.3.</a> through A.6. (e.g., authorized transportation, non-contract hotels, reasonable baggage charges) incurred while on a trip or on Company business away from his base. 2364:    <p id="link_5B1h" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 5.B.1.h." rel="tooltip">h.</span> For hotel rooms required under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_5B1a">Section 5.B.1.a.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_5B1b">5.B.1.b.</a> only, if an intermediate stop, measured from block-in to block-out, is less than 5 hours and the stop occurs during the night or critical duty period (or during a domestic duty period at the Memphis hub sort facility), the Company may substitute a sleep room in the hub sort facility for a hotel room; provided, however, that the Company has sleep rooms available in the hub sort facility for all pilots transiting the hub sort facility with an intermediate stop of 2:30 hours or more (from block-in to block-out).</p>
2397:  <p id="link_5B7" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 5.B.7." rel="tooltip">7.</span> A pilot shall cancel any scheduled hotel rooms he does not intend to use. Credit for the cancelation shall be as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_8C2h">Section 8.C.2.h.</a> If, having canceled his hotel room, a pilot’s personal plans change and he needs a hotel room as originally scheduled, he may either re-book his original hotel room, or if unavailable, obtain a hotel room in the same city and be reimbursed for such room up to the contract hotel rate. CRS shall re-book the pilot’s room, (subject to availability), at that city’s contract hotels only, when Company schedule changes or operational delays are the reason for the pilot’s change of plans. If the pilot stays in a hotel room, as provided in this paragraph, other than after a revenue trip, he shall notify CRS of his contact numbers. This hotel room shall be paid for using the Company issued Travel Card, unless CRS advises the pilot of a direct billing arrangement at a contract hotel. This hotel room shall not be charged to the pilot’s deviation bank, and shall be documented by the submission of an expense report.</p>
2406:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 5.D.1." rel="tooltip">1.</span> If crew accommodations (as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_5B">Section 5.B.</a>), have not previously been made, a pilot shall contact CRS to obtain accommodations. If reservations have not been made, at the pilot’s option, he may obtain comparable accommodations at the lowest rate available at the time the reservation is made. If these accommodations cannot be direct billed, pilots are authorized to charge these expenses as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_5A7">Section 5.A.7.</a></p>
2407:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 5.D.2." rel="tooltip">2.</span> If transportation required under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_5C">Section 5.C.</a> is not provided within 30 minutes after block-in, the crew is authorized to obtain transportation and to charge these expenses as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_5A7">Section 5.A.7.</a> If the scheduled transportation from the layover location to the departure airport is not available in time to prevent a departure delay, the crew shall use their best efforts to obtain transportation as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_5A7">Section 5.A.7.</a></p>

Mini-snack contents shall be developed and revised in consultation with the MEC Trip Services Committee subject to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_5E6">Section 5.E.6.</a></p>
2423:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 5.E.1.a.ix." rel="tooltip">ix.</span> Jumpseaters will not be catered domestically, except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_5E1e">Section 5.E.1.e.</a></p>
2424:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 5.E.1.a.x." rel="tooltip">x.</span> On international trips scheduled to domestic parameters (pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1b">Section 12.D.1.b.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1c">c.</a>), menu selection shall be provided when available.</p>
2431:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 5.E.1.b.iv." rel="tooltip">iv.</span> An International flight shall not be delayed for catering if it is scheduled for snack or mini-snack service only, or if it is scheduled to domestic parameters, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1b">Section 12.D.1.b.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1c">12.D.1.c.</a></p>
2437:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 5.E.1.c." rel="tooltip">c.</span> If a pilot’s domestic flight sequence otherwise entitled only to a mini-snack (<a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_5E1ai">Section 5.E.1.a.i.</a>) blocks out between 0500 and 0830, such flight sequence shall receive a breakfast snack instead of a mini-snack.</p>
2445:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 5.E.4." rel="tooltip">4.</span> When combined in the same duty period with Company assigned flying, deadhead travel time (air or ground) shall be included in applying the catering provisions contained in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_5E1a">Section 5.E.1.a.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_5E1b">E.1.b.</a> Travel from airport to hotel is not deadhead by surface transportation deadhead (unless the arrival city and the next departure city are different, in which case it may be deadhead by surface transportation).</p>
2447:  <p id="link_5E6" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 5.E.6." rel="tooltip">6.</span> The Vice President, Flight Operations, or his designee, shall make arrangements for the catering required by this Section. The Company shall meet quarterly with the MEC Trip Services Committee to review catering and discuss possible modifications (e.g., composition and/or quality of mini-snack, snack, meal selections, etc.). Should the Company and the MEC Trip Services Committee fail to resolve or address concerns/problems to the satisfaction of the MEC Trip Services Committee, ALPA may elect to use the process outlined in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_5B4bii">Section 5.B.4.b.ii.</a> Additionally, the Association shall have the ability to meet with the Vice President, Flight Operations, or his designee, at mutually agreeable times and locations regarding catering concerns.</p>
2451:  <p>The Company shall provide each pilot with a parking space in his domicile (or base in case of an FDA base). If a pilot does not live at his domicile (or base in case of an FDA base), he may request a parking space at the Company airport facility, subject to availability and approval (For information regarding the parking allowance as a deviation expense, see <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_8C3f">Section 8.C.3.f.</a>).</p>

2488:    <p>A domicile shall remain a new domicile for a period of 12 months commencing with the activation of the first pilot assigned to that domicile, subject to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6A7">Section 6.A.7.</a> (establishment of an FDA). The establishment of Memphis (MEM) as the permanent domicile for all pilots on an FDA shall not constitute the establishment of a new domicile for purposes of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#section6">Section 6</a> and a pilot shall not become eligible for relocation benefits on the basis of his MEM FDA domicile.</p>

2634:  <p>If the residence to which the pilot is moving is already the property of the pilot, he shall not be entitled to a relocation allowance or the benefits provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6C12">Section 6.C.12.</a> (air transportation for housing searches). 2636:  <p>A pilot shall reimburse the Company for 100% of the relocation costs paid by the Company pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6D4">Section 6.D.4.</a> if the pilot subsequently is awarded a new crew position (in a different geographic location) for which he is awarded a training slot or base transfer date that is within the period of 36 months following the completion of his relocation to his first base.</p>
2739:      <p id="link_6C12ai" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 6.C.12.a.i." rel="tooltip">i.</span> The Company shall establish a relocation air travel expense bank for each pilot entitled to relocation air travel authorized by <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6C12A">Section 6.C.12.a.</a> The value of the pilot’s relocation air travel expense bank shall be equal to the reference fare quote obtained by the Company’s travel vendor pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6C12aiii">Section 6.C.12.a.iii.</a></p>
2742:      <p id="link_6C12aiii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 6.C.12.a.iii." rel="tooltip">iii.</span>   Within 3 days of the Relocation Department’s receipt of the pilot’s request for air travel authorized by <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6C12a">Section 6.C.12.a.</a>, the Company’s travel vendor shall obtain a fare quote (“reference fare quote”) for the total cost of economy class air travel for the pilot’s entire traveling party between the pilot’s currently assigned base and the pilot’s new base. The Company’s travel vendor shall transmit the reference fare quote electronically to the Company’s Relocation and Crew Travel Audit Departments and to the pilot.</p>
2743:      <p id="link_6C12aiv" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 6.C.12.a.iv." rel="tooltip">iv.</span>    Within 3 days of the pilot’s request for air travel authorized by <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6C12a">Section 6.C.12.a.</a>, the Company’s travel vendor shall also obtain a fare quote (“requested fare quote”) for the total cost of air travel for the pilot’s entire traveling party on the requested itinerary. The Company’s travel vendor shall transmit the requested fare quote electronically to the pilot, at which time the pilot may purchase tickets for his requested itinerary (as quoted) or make alternative arrangements with the Company’s travel vendor.</p>
2745:      <p id="link_6C12avi" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 6.C.12.a.vi." rel="tooltip">vi.</span>    Any air travel expenses in excess of the balance of the pilot’s relocation air travel expense bank shall be remitted to the Company by payroll deduction, as provided in Section <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_3E1avi">3.E.1.a.vi.</a>, from the pay check on the 15th of the month following the pilot’s purchase of air travel tickets authorized by Section 6.C.12.a.</p>

2780:      <p id="link_6E1bii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 6.E.1.b.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    Any cost for the transportation of the household goods of the pilot and his immediate family that is the responsibility of the pilot pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6E1bi">Section 6.E.1.b.i.</a> shall be paid by the pilot to the commercial carrier at the time those goods are transported, and shall not be billed to the Company.</p>
2781:      <p id="link_6E1biii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 6.E.1.b.iii." rel="tooltip">iii.</span>   This paragraph shall not apply to a pilot whose FDA assignment is his first crew position, or a pilot described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6E1a">Section 6.E.1.a.</a></p>
2783:    <p id="link_6E1c" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 6.E.1.c." rel="tooltip">c.</span>   A pilot awarded/assigned to an FDA as his first crew position shall be eligible for the relocation package described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6E1b">Section 6.E.1.b.</a>, excluding the relocation allowance described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6C2">Section 6.C.2.</a> The pilot, however, shall be eligible for an allowance of $2,000. That allowance shall be payable upon the completion of the pilot’s probationary period, provided he has not voluntarily bid out of the FDA prior to completion of his probationary period. The cost of moving the household goods of the pilot and his immediate family shall be limited to the lesser of the cost of moving those goods from his current residence or from MEM.</p>
2784:    <p id="link_6E1d" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 6.E.1.d." rel="tooltip">d.</span>   A pilot may receive relocation benefits prior to being activated into his new FDA crew position in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6A8">Section 6.A.8.</a> (Eligibility for Benefits Prior to Activation).</p>
2785:    <p id="link_6E1e" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 6.E.1.e." rel="tooltip">e.</span>   In addition to the relocation allowance provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6C2">Section 6.C.2.</a>, a pilot, other than a pilot awarded/assigned to an FDA as his first crew position, may be eligible for an FDA bonus as follows:</p>
2790:      <p id="link_6E1eiv" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 6.E.1.e.iv." rel="tooltip">iv.</span>    If the Company and the Association disagree as to the amount of an FDA bonus, if any, the disagreement may be submitted for resolution to the System Board. The System Board shall lack jurisdiction to establish FDA bonuses in excess of the maximums established in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6E1eii">Section 6.E.1.e.ii.</a></p>
2799:      <p id="link_6E2ai" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 6.E.2.a.i." rel="tooltip">i.</span> If a pilot receives a relocation package in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6E1">Section 6.E.1.</a> (Award/Assignment to an FDA), he shall be subject to the reimbursement provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6B6">Section 6.B.6.</a> through B.10.</p>
2800:      <p id="link_6E2aii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 6.E.2.a.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    If a pilot receives a relocation package in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6E1">Section 6.E.1.</a>, and subsequently receives a Stand In Bid Award to a crew position in a different FDA or a non-FDA crew position, the following shall apply:</p>
2802:        <p id="link_6E2aiia" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 6.E.2.a.ii.(a)." rel="tooltip">(a)</span>  he shall be subject to the provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6B6">Section 6.B.6.</a>, as if he had received a relocation package for a new domicile.</p>
2803:        <p id="link_6E2aiib" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 6.E.2.a.ii.(b)." rel="tooltip">(b)</span>  <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6B6">Section 6.B.6.</a> shall apply notwithstanding his entitlement to a relocation package for his new crew position.</p>
2804:        <p id="link_6E2aiic" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 6.E.2.a.ii.(c)." rel="tooltip">(c)</span>  If the number of pilots who are imminently subject to assignment pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24C2">Section 24.C.2.</a> exceeds the number of pilots who have been activated in the FDA position for 18 months or more, then this paragraph may be waived in seniority order for a number of pilots receiving a stand in bid award to a crew position in a different FDA or a non-FDA crew position not to exceed the difference between the number of pilots who are imminently subject to assignment pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24C2">Section 24.C.2</a>. and the number of pilots who have been activated in the FDA position for 18 months or more.</p>
2806:        <p>•    20 pilots in a crew position who are imminently subject to assignment pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24C2cib2">Section 24.C.2.c.i.(b)(2)</a>.</p>
2820:      <p id="link_6E2bii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 6.E.2.b.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    A pilot who is furloughed from an FDA, shall be eligible for relocation package #2, excluding the relocation allowance described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6C2">Section 6.C.2.</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6E1c">6.E.1.c.</a>, provided he relocates to his last pre-FDA residence or to MEM, at his option. If a furloughed pilot is recalled to an FDA base, he shall be eligible for the relocation package provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6E1c">Section 6.E.1.c.</a>, excluding the FDA bonus, if any, provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6E1e">Section 6.E.1.e.</a> However, he shall be eligible for an allowance of $2,000. If the pilot recalled from furlough is still a probationary pilot, the original payment of that allowance shall continue to be deferred until completion of his probationary period and no allowance shall be paid for the relocation back to an FDA location.</p>
2821:      <p id="link_6E2biii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 6.E.2.b.iii." rel="tooltip">iii.</span>   Notwithstanding the provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6A2">Section 6.A.2.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6A3">A.3.</a>, a pilot who is assigned from an FDA, or who is awarded a new crew position pursuant to a stand in bid award, shall be eligible for a relocation package #2, subject to the provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6E2aii">Section 6.E.2.a.ii.</a></p>
2832:    <p id="link_6E3b" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 6.E.3.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span>   A pilot covered by <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6E3">Section 6.E.3.</a> (this paragraph) shall reimburse the Company according to the proration schedule set forth in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6B9">Section 6.B.9.</a> He shall also be subject to the provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6B10">Section 6.B.10.</a> (withholding of relocation benefits).</p>
2835:  <p>Notwithstanding the weight limits established in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6C1a">Section 6.C.1.a.</a>, transportation of household goods shall be limited as follows, with any excess weight determined in accordance with the provisions in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6C1a">Section 6.C.1.a.</a>:</p>
2840:    <p id="link_6E4d" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 6.E.4.d." rel="tooltip">d.</span>   A pilot entitled to a paid relocation upon return from FDA as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6E2b">Section 6.E.2.b.</a>, shall be entitled to an increase in the weight limit originally shipped of 10% per year of international residence not to exceed a total increase of 40% (subject to the chargeable weight limitation in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6C1a">Section 6.C.1.a.</a>).</p>
2841:    <p id="link_6E4e" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 6.E.4.e" rel="tooltip">e.</span>   Notwithstanding the provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6E4a">Section 6.E.4.a.</a> through E.4.d., the weight limitation for a pilot leaving an FDA shall not be less than the amount originally shipped to the FDA plus the increase provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6E4d">Section 6.E.4.d.</a></p>
2858:    <p id="link_6Fb" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 6.F.1.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span>   For FDA moves pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6E">Section 6.E.</a>, either to or from the FDA, the pilot shall receive 7 days off.</p>
2861:  <p id="link_6F3" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 6.F.3." rel="tooltip">3.</span> The pilot shall be compensated an R-day value for each trip day or R-day that is dropped (without pay) as a relocation day under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6F">Section 6.F.</a> Relocation days that occur on days off shall not be compensated.</p>
2862:  <p id="link_6F4" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 6.F.4." rel="tooltip">4.</span> Credit Hours lost from a pilot’s BLG/RLG as a result of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6F">Section 6.F.</a> shall be eligible for make-up.</p>
2864:  <p id="link_6F6" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 6.F.6." rel="tooltip">6.</span> Days off for relocation also apply to pilots taking either of the crash pad move options as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6D2">Section 6.D.2.</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6D3">D.3.</a></p>
2871:  <p id="link_6G3" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 6.G.3." rel="tooltip">3.</span> Based on a review of all the circumstances, Human Resources, AOD, may determine that a pilot has completed his relocation even though some of the factors ordinarily establishing a completed relocation are absent. If the pilot subsequently fails to complete his relocation, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6G2">Section 6.G.2.</a>, the pilot shall be deemed never to have relocated and shall be obligated to reimburse the Company in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6B8">Section 6.B.8.</a></p>
2872:  <p id="link_6G4" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 6.G.4." rel="tooltip">4.</span> The Company may request documentation to establish that a pilot has completed his relocation, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6G2">Section 6.G.2.</a> The documentation may include, but is not limited to, settlement statements relating to the purchase and/or sale of residences; verification of the movement of household goods and automobile(s) to the new location; verification of the permanent relocation of the pilot; verification of the permanent relocation of the pilot’s spouse; verification of the permanent relocation of the pilot’s dependent children under the age of 18 years; establishment of a pilot’s residence at the new location for purposes of applicable property or state income taxes, driver’s license, automobile registration and voter’s registration. A pilot shall submit documentation requested by the Company in accordance with this paragraph.</p>
2873:  <p id="link_6G5" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 6.G.5." rel="tooltip">5.</span> If a pilot becomes obligated to reimburse the Company for expenditures related to relocation, he may request of Human Resources, AOD, a repayment schedule based on a mutually agreeable per pay check amount. If the parties are unable to agree on an amount to be deducted per pay check, the Company is authorized to initiate a payroll deduction as provided in Section <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_3E1avi">3.E.1.a.vi.</a> Unless mutually waived by both the pilot and Human Resources, AOD, the maximum period allowed for repayment under this provision shall not exceed nine (9) months.</p>
2874:  <p id="link_6G6" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 6.G.6." rel="tooltip">6.</span> Notwithstanding the provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6G5">Section 6.G.5.</a>, if a pilot’s obligation to reimburse the Company for expenditures related to relocation becomes the subject of a grievance filed pursuant to Section 20, the period contained in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6G5">Section 6.G.5.</a> shall not commence until final resolution of that grievance pursuant to Sections 20 and 21.</p>
2875:  <p id="link_6G7" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 6.G.7." rel="tooltip">7.</span> A pilot’s eligibility for staging jumpseat travel status as a pilot commuting to and from work at his new base expires 30 days following his receipt of the full relocation allowance provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6C2">Section 6.C.2.</a></p>
2877:  <p id="link_6G9" class="link_highlight">9. Notwithstanding other provisions in this Section, if a pilot is forced to leave his current geographic domicile (or base in the case of an FDA), due to legal restrictions, furlough, or assignment (as defined by Section 24) such pilot shall not incur any reimbursement obligations pursuant to this Section. Additionally, a pilot (including those pilots subject to the FDA LOA, ANC LOA, etc.) who exercises an Assignment Right of Return (ARR), as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24C2e">Section 24.C.2.e.</a>, shall not incur any reimbursement obligations pursuant to this Section.</p>
2889:  <p class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 7.A.2." rel="tooltip">2.</span> A vacation day shall be a 24 hour period corresponding to the local base day. A vacation period is a series of consecutive days posted and awarded as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_7C">Section 7.C.</a>, and rescheduled, if applicable, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_7A9">Section 7.A.9.</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_7E">7.E.</a></p>
2898:  <p class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 7.A.11." rel="tooltip">11.</span> As provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4I10">Section 4.I.10.</a>, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_14A7">Section 14.A.7.</a>, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25L13d">Section 25.L.13.d.</a> (Emergency Drop), and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25Z3">Section 25.Z.3.</a> (Bereavement Absence), a pilot may use available hours in his vacation bank to cover annual military training, to preclude or delay going on disability, for personal emergencies, and to add additional days for bereavement absence.</p>
2906:    <p id="link_7B1c" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 7.B.1.c." rel="tooltip">c.</span>   A pilot with longevity of at least 4 years, but less than 5 years, shall be eligible for 15 days vacation plus a pro rata share based on his longevity and the pro rata formula in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_7B5">Section 7.B.5.</a></p>
2908:    <p id="link_7B1e" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 7.B.1.e." rel="tooltip">e.</span>   A pilot with longevity of at least 9 years, but less than 10 years, shall be eligible for 22 days vacation plus a pro rata share based on his longevity and the pro rata formula in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_7B5">Section 7.B.5.</a></p>
2910:    <p id="link_7b1g" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 7.B.1.g." rel="tooltip">g.</span>   A pilot with longevity of at least 19 years but less than 20 years shall be eligible for 29 days vacation plus a pro rata share based on his longevity and the pro rata formula in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_7B5">Section 7.B.5.</a></p>
2913:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 7.B.2." rel="tooltip">2.</span> If a pilot does not complete 10 months in an active pay status during a calendar year due to retirement, furlough, disability, or unpaid leave(s) of absence (Section 13), other than leave due to on-the-job injury, he shall not be entitled to the full accrual as per <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_7B1">Section 7.B.1.</a> That pilot’s vacation accrual shall be 1/10th of the full accrual for each calendar month the pilot is in an active pay status. For purposes of this paragraph, a month shall be counted if the pilot is not retired, or on furlough, disability or unpaid leave of absence for more than 15 days during that month.</p>
2920:  <p id="link_7B5" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 7.B.5." rel="tooltip">5.</span> Vacation days earned on a pro rata basis (as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_7B1c">Section 7.B.1.c.</a>, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_7B1e">B.1.e.</a>, and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_71g">B.1.g.</a>) shall be computed at a rate of 0.7 days per month for each month of service, up to 10 months per calendar year, subject to the provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_7B4">Section 7.B.4.</a></p>
2970:    <p id="link_7E2a" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 7.E.2.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span> A pilot may enter a vacation slide submission during the Conflict Input Window immediately before the bid period in which a trip(s) affected by the slide (or the vacation period itself, if no trip is affected) is scheduled to begin, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25E2">Section 25.E.2.</a> (Conflict Input Window). A pilot may adjust his vacation period by sliding it up to a maximum of 5 days in either direction. However, the slide shall not reschedule any portion of that vacation into the preceding bid periods of November or December. A vacation period of more than 7 days, that begins in one bid period and ends in the following bid period, may be slid up to a maximum of 5 days in either direction.</p>
2974:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 7.E.2.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span> A pilot may slide a vacation to conflict with a carryover trip as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_7E2a">Section 7.E.2.a.</a>, only if he submits for the slide during the Conflict Input Window associated with the award of bid period in which the carryover trip began (e.g., the Conflict Input Window in the end of November (i.e., the Conflict Input Window for the December bid period award) is used to slide a January vacation to conflict with a December into January carryover trip).</p>
2975:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 7.E.2.c." rel="tooltip">c.</span> If a pilot slides his vacation period to within 48 hours of the scheduled end of a trip in which the last activity is an international duty period, that trip shall be deemed in conflict with the vacation period, except for a trip described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1ci">Section 12.D.1.c.i.</a></p>
2980:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 7.E.3.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   In addition to or in lieu of a vacation slide, a pilot awarded a regular line may expand his vacation period in either or both directions to conflict with a greater number of credit hours. However, a pilot may not expand his vacation from December into November, or from January into December. A pilot may submit for a vacation expansion during the Conflict Input Window immediately before the bid period in which a trip(s) affected by the expansion is scheduled to begin, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25E2">Section 25.E.2.</a></p>
2991:  <p>Each pilot shall have a vacation credit hour bank established at the beginning of the bid period commencing closest to January 1, each year, based upon the vacation hours he has accrued (as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_7B">Section 7.B.</a>). A pilot’s vacation credit hour bank shall be calculated by multiplying the number of vacation days by 6 CH. A pilot’s bank shall be adjusted for positive balances (as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_7I3d">Section 7.I.3.d.</a>, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_7E1bv">7.E.1.b.v.</a>, or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_7G5c">7.G.5.c.</a>), or negative credit hour balances from the previous year’s vacation bank.</p>
2996:  <p>A regular line holder shall be removed from a trip(s) in conflict with his vacation period (as awarded or slid) or vacation expansion. Conflict with an international duty free buffer, as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1d">Section 12.D.1.d.</a>, shall constitute a conflict with the trip protected by that buffer and may not be waived. The SCH value of the removed trip(s) shall be deducted from the pilot’s vacation credit hour bank.</p>
2999:  <p>Except as otherwise specifically provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25E4b">Section 25.E.4.b.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25E5">E.5.</a>, for secondary line holders, the following shall apply to secondary and custom line holders:</p>
3002:    <p class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 7.G.2.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span> A secondary line holder’s vacation credit hour bank shall be reduced by 6 CH for each day of vacation in the bid period not in conflict with a carryover trip or R-day, excluding the vacation buffer provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_7G2a">Section 7.G.2.a.</a> above.</p>
3005:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 7.G.2.c.i." rel="tooltip">i.</span> A conflict with an international duty free buffer (as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1d">Section 12.D.1.d.</a>) shall constitute a conflict with the trip protected by that buffer.</p>
3014:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 7.G.2.d.iii." rel="tooltip">iii.</span> For purposes of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25D2">Section 25.D.2.</a> (secondary line construction), hours deducted from the pilot’s vacation credit hour bank for the bid period, other than carryover credit hours from the previous bid period, shall be considered as trip credit hours.</p>
3015:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 7.G.2.d.iv." rel="tooltip">iv.</span> For purposes of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_7E1">Section 7.E.1.</a> (Vacation Change), hours deducted from the pilot’s vacation credit hour bank for the bid period, other than carryover credit hours from the previous bid period, shall be considered as trip credit hours constituting a trip guarantee.</p>
3016:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 7.G.2.d.v." rel="tooltip">v.</span> For purposes of minimum days off protection, vacation days shall not be considered days scheduled free from duty; vacation buffer days shall be considered days scheduled free from duty. <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1d">Section 12.D.1.d.</a> (international trip buffer) shall not apply when constructing a secondary line for a pilot with vacation in the bid period.</p>
3019:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 7.G.2.f." rel="tooltip">f.</span> The provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_7G2">Section 7.G.2.</a> shall apply to a pilot assigned a custom line (as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25I1a">Section 25.I.1.a.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25I1e">25.I.1.e.</a>).</p>
3027:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 7.G.3.c.i." rel="tooltip">i.</span> A conflict with an international duty free buffer (as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1d">Section 12.D.1.d.</a>) shall constitute a conflict with the trip protected by that buffer, and may not be waived.</p>
3035:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 7.G.3.d.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span> A pilot may enter preferences for reconstruction of his reserve line during the Conflict Input Window (as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25E2g">Section 25.E.2.g.</a>).</p>

Credit hours deducted from the pilot’s vacation credit hour bank (as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_7G3b">Section 7.G.3.b.</a>) shall be credited toward the pilot’s RLG.</p>
3040:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 7.G.3.d.vii." rel="tooltip">vii.</span> A reserve pilot’s leveling position shall include an R-day value for each day of vacation in the bid period, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4H2">Section 4.H.2.</a></p>
3044:    <p>A pilot with vacation during a month in which he holds a reserve line may extend the vacation that occurs in that month.
