3253:  <p>The intent of the deviation policy is to allow a pilot business travel flexibility in accordance with the options and conditions specified herein. Except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_8C1fii">Section 8.C.1.f.ii.</a>, a pilot who deviates is responsible for his scheduled, revised, rerouted, or canceled trip. A deviating pilot must ensure his compliance with FAR crew rest requirements prior to operating a Company flight. A pilot who deviates from a scheduled deadhead shall earn trip guarantee as if he were deadheading as scheduled.</p>
3259:      <p class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 8.C.1.a.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    Except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_8C1ai">Section 8.C.1.a.i.</a>, if a pilot is notified of a trip assignment less than 60 hours prior to showtime, upon notification, he shall advise the Company through VIPS of his deviation from a scheduled deadhead at the beginning of the trip.</p>
3287:      <p class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 8.C.1.d.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    For purposes of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_8C1d">Section 8.C.1.d.</a> (this paragraph) the showtime of a revenue flight shall be one hour prior to the scheduled departure of that flight.</p>
3306:      <p id="link_8C1fii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 8.C.1.f.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    If a pilot’s trip is revised after his initial deviation check-in and, as a result, the pilot is unable to report on time, the Company shall make best efforts to reposition the pilot for the trip. If the Company is unable to do so, the pilot shall be eligible for substitution and is authorized return deadhead transportation to base. The cost of the original deadhead tickets shall be deducted from the pilot’s deviation bank, however, the cost of the deviation ticket used, and the cost of his return ticket, shall be allowable as a claim, up to the applicable fare (as determined in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_8C2a">Section 8.C.2.a.</a>) for the original deadhead tickets, regardless of the pilot’s deviation bank balance. Such claim shall be specifically documented on a deviation expense report.</p>
3307:      <p id="link_8C1fiii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 8.C.1.f.iii." rel="tooltip">iii.</span>   A VLT/DRF/CMU pilot covered by <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_8C1fii">Section 8.C.1.f.ii.</a> shall not be eligible for substitution and shall earn the greater of 3:00 CH or duty rig computed from his scheduled showtime until the VIPS notification of the revision.</p>
3337:        <p class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 8.C.2.a.ii.(b)" rel="tooltip">(b)</span>  Any DBA balance remaining after application of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_8C2aiia">Section 8.C.2.a.ii.(a)</a> above shall be added to the pilot’s deviation bank in the immediately subsequent bid period.</p>
3354:    <p class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 8.C.2.d." rel="tooltip">d.</span>   All deadhead travel shall be classified into two categories, Front/Back-End, and Mid-Trip. For the purpose of deviation bank credit, each category shall be treated separately. However, if a deadhead trip is changed or canceled by the Company, the associated deadhead bank monies remain intact. Within each category, a pilot’s bank credit shall be determined as set forth in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_8C2a">Section 8.C.2.a.</a></p>
3360:    <p class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 8.C.2.f." rel="tooltip">f.</span>   A pilot in initial, transition or upgrade training (ITU) shall have a separate deviation bank established for the duration of such training. The training deviation bank shall be determined as set forth in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_8C2a">Section 8.C.2.a.</a></p>
3365:      <p class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 8.C.2.h.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    For all hotel rooms canceled by a pilot through CRS or other designated means at least 26 hours prior to the scheduled hotel check-in (i.e., in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_5B7">Section 5.B.7.</a>), the Company shall credit $35 (domestic hotel reservations), or $65 (international hotel reservations) to that pilot’s HRC bank, provided, however, that the pilot actually operated the trip containing the canceled hotel room(s).</p>
3373:  <p>Subject to the limitations and reporting provisions in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_8C4">Section 8.C.4.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_8C5">C.5.</a>, a pilot’s air travel, train travel, surface transportation, hotel use, parking and non-taxable per diem are allowable/reimbursable expenses as provided in this paragraph.</p>
3383:      <p class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 8.C.3.a.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    Air travel expenses shall be limited to the applicable fare (as determined in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_8C2a">Section 8.C.2.a.</a>) for the class of service for which the deviation travel would otherwise qualify under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_8A5">Section 8.A.5.</a></p>
3393:        <p id="link_8C3avb" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 8.C.3.a.v.(b)." rel="tooltip">(b)</span>  the provision of the e-mail in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_8C3ava">Section 8.C.3.a.v.(a)</a> shall entitle the pilot to be reimbursed for his deviation ticket up to the full fare first class cost of a direct, nonstop deviation deadhead whose origin and destination match the scheduled deadhead, regardless of his deviation bank value. A deviation deadhead covered by this paragraph must be among the standard routings scheduled by the carrier.</p>
3440:    <p>A pilot claiming hotel use as a deviation expense under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_8C3di">Section 8.C.3.d.i.</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_8C3dii">ii.</a> may also claim non-taxable per diem for the period covered by his hotel reimbursement claim (i.e., one night hotel use equals 24 hours per diem) and not otherwise covered by per diem for a scheduled trip. This per diem shall be paid at the rate for the city associated with the revenue portion of the trip.</p>
3453:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 8.C.4.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span> Expenses which are otherwise allowable/reimbursable, but which exceed the value of a pilot’s deviation bank are the pilot’s responsibility, and shall be handled in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_8C5b">Section 8.C.5.b.</a></p>
3454:      <p id="link_8C4c" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 8.C.4.c." rel="tooltip">c.</span>   The Company shall pay all fees associated with scheduled deadhead tickets. 3471:    <p id="link_8C5b" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 8.C.5.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span> If a pilot’s allowable deviation expenses for a bid period exceed the value of his deviation bank (as adjusted by operation of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_8C2aii">Section 8.C.2.a.ii.</a>, if applicable) for such bid period or if a pilot has incurred unallowable expenses, the Company shall utilize payroll deduction to satisfy the pilot’s balance, subject to the 25% limit expressed in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_3E">Section 3.E.</a></p>
3485:  <p id="link_9A2" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 9.A.2." rel="tooltip">2.</span> If a management pilot bumps a line pilot from his scheduled trip or a portion thereof, in accordance with other provisions of this Agreement, the line pilot shall receive the scheduled credit hours and deviation credit, if any, for the trip, or portion thereof, notwithstanding <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_8C2a">Section 8.C.2.a.</a> (trips flown).</p>
3486:  <p id="link_9A3" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 9.A.3." rel="tooltip">3.</span> If a management pilot flies a trip, or portion thereof, covered by this Agreement and it is not possible to identify the line pilot who would have been bumped and otherwise would be entitled to compensation as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_9A2">Section 9.A.2.</a> above, the scheduled credit hours for such trip, or portion thereof, either shall be paid to the Association or offset against monies owed by the Association to the Company pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_18C">Section 18.C.</a> The value of any monies owed or offset pursuant to this paragraph shall be determined by multiplying the number of credit hours flown by the average hourly pay rate system wide for the crew status in which the management pilot flew.</p>
3487:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 9.A.4." rel="tooltip">4.</span> Disputes arising from the application of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_9A2">Section 9.A.2.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_9A3">3</a>. shall be resolved as provided in Sections 20 and 21. In no event shall the Company be required to pay a trip guarantee pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_9A2">Section 9.A.2.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_9A3">3</a>. more than once.</p>

3503:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 9.A.7." rel="tooltip">7.</span> The Company will provide a means, via VIPS or successor automation, for each pilot to indicate his willingness to operate humanitarian or publicity flights (PDH assignments) for per diem only, and without any other compensation of any kind. 3527:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 9.E.2." rel="tooltip">2.</span> FPS/TAA shall bid for and be awarded a bid line for flying purposes or pay only, as determined by his manager, in his primary crew position. For purposes of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_9E">Section 9.E.</a> an FPS’s “primary crew position” means the crew position in which the pilot is currently performing his line flying activities (i.e., seniority bid position). Unless released to the line for an entire bid period by his manager, a FPS/TAA shall bid pay only, and shall be awarded a BLG/RLG and compensated as follows:</p>
3538:    <p id="link_9E2c" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 9.E.2.c." rel="tooltip">c.</span>   An FPS/TAA who performs FPS/TAA duties on a day(s) off in excess of the duty requirements contained in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_9E5b">Section 9.E.5.b.</a> shall be compensated as follows:</p>
3550:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 9.E.3.d." rel="tooltip">d.</span>   The crew position of an FPS/TAA who resigns, or is released from his FPS/TAA status absent an open System Bid or FTPA crew position, shall be determined by comparing his system-wide seniority against the results of the most recent System Bid. If the pilot is awarded or assigned a different crew position than his current crew position, his training, or base transfer activation, shall be determined in the same manner as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_13A6e">Section 13.A.6.e.</a></p>
3565:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 9.E.5.e." rel="tooltip">e.</span>   Additional work days may not be scheduled without an FPS/TAA’s consent. If the FPS/TAA performs assigned duties on a day previously scheduled free from duty, he shall be entitled to compensation as per <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_9E2c">Section 9.E.2.c.</a>, as applicable.</p>
3575:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 9.E.6." rel="tooltip">6.</span> An FPS/TAA pilot is eligible to participate in System Bids that close during his tenure as an FPS/TAA pilot, but will not receive an actual award without a release from his manager. Flight Project Specialist and Technical Advisor/Aircraft Pay Adjustment (FTPA) shall be administered in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11Q">Section 11.Q.</a> (Check Airman/Instructor Pilot Pay Adjustment (CIPPA)), as if the FPS/TAA were a Check Airman or Instructor Pilot.</p>
3630:<p>B.   A pilot covered by <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_10A">Section 10.A.</a> may not bid and be awarded a published line of flying covered by this Agreement.</p>
3631:<p>C.   A pilot returning from duty or assignment covered by <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_10A">Section 10.A.</a> shall have his crew position determined as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_10D">Section 10.D.</a>, provided that:</p>
3633:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 10.C.1" rel="tooltip">1.</span> the pilot has not forfeited his seniority as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_22B1e">Section 22.B.1.e.</a> (failure to return after leave of absence); and</p>
3635:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 10.C.3" rel="tooltip">3.</span> the pilot meets the requirements outlined in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24A3">Section 24.A.3.</a> (medical and professional certifications) for the appropriate crew seat.</p>
3637:<p id="link_10D" class="link_highlight">D. Such pilot’s crew position and training shall be determined in the same manner as a pilot returning from a leave of absence pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_13A6">Section 13.A.6.</a></p>

3748:        <p>c. For the purposes of Sections 4 and 12, these additional 30 minutes of showtime shall not be considered a standby period but will count as duty.</p>

3889:        <p>a.   During a Check Airman’s third consecutive pay only bid period, he shall be scheduled for 2 PDO fly days in lieu of scheduled training events, subject to the limitations contained in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11M9">Section 11.M.9.</a> (PDO Bid Period). Due to the lengths of trips in certain domiciles, PDO fly days may be pooled to accommodate a trip longer than 2 days.</p>
3890:        <p>b.   During a Check Airman’s fourth consecutive pay only bid period, he shall have eligibility equal to the CH value of 2 R-days (or a minimum of 4:30 CHs/day) available to him in the Secondary Working Window (SWW, see <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25E6">Section 25.E.6.</a>) (SWW Bid Period). The Check Airman’s schedule shall include 2 fewer instructional days in an SWW Bid Period, unless deferred in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11M10b">Section 11.M.10.b.</a></p>
3897:        <p>e. 3913:        <p>c.   A Check Airman will have corresponding proficiency (PRO) flying eligibility during the SWW (see <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25E6">Section 25.E.6.</a>) as follows:</p>
3915:          <p>i. 3926:        <p>d.   In no event shall a pilot begin a pay only SWW bid period below the applicable Minimum Bid Period Guarantee, subject to the provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4A">Section 4.A.</a></p>

Such activity does not constitute an excess of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11M6a">Section 11.M.6.a.</a> (maximum number of scheduled duty days). 3943:      <p>12. When assigned a combination of flight duties in an aircraft and other duties in a training base in a single pay only bid period, a combination of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11M6a">Section 11.M.6.a.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11M16">Section 11.M.16.</a> shall be used to determine the maximum number of events on a Check Airman’s schedule.</p>
3944:      <p id="link_11M13" class="link_highlight">13.    The Company may reschedule or cancel a Check Airman on an event-by-event basis (trip or training activity) to perform Check Airman duties with prior approval from the appropriate Standards or Training Manager, or his designee. Assignments that occur as a result of this provision shall be limited to the event type canceled (e.g., If the Company cancels a SIM event, the Check Airman shall be available for only SIM assignments). He shall be given at least 8 hours’ notice prior to a domestic trip/training activity or 12 hours’ notice prior to an international trip. A Check Airman shall not be required to work on a previously scheduled day(s) off without his consent, subject to the provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12A8">Section 12.A.8.</a></p>
3945:      <p>14.    Except for trips included on his awarded schedule during a non-instructional bid period, in the event that a Check Airman’s instruction/evaluation event (trip or training activity) is canceled, the Check Airman will be assigned instructional reserve days as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11N14">Section 11.N.14.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11N15">15.</a></p>

4035:        <p>b.   During an Instructor Pilot’s fourth consecutive pay only bid period, he shall have eligibility equal to the CH value of 2 R-days (or a minimum of 4:30 CHs/day) available to him in the Secondary Working Window (SWW) (See <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25E6">Section 25.E.6.</a>) (SWW Bid Period). The Instructor Pilot’s schedule shall include 2 fewer instructional days in an SWW Bid Period, unless deferred in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11N11b">Section 11.N.11.b.</a></p>
4055:          <p>Example: An Instructor Pilot is placed in pay only status for a third consecutive bid period (which, based on the pattern established in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11N9">Section 11.N.9.</a>, is an SWW Bid Period), and as such is entitled to a 2-day schedule reduction. He elects to defer that reduction, so his instructional schedule is not reduced. During his next SWW Bid Period, he elects not to defer, and also elects to use the previously deferred 2-day reduction. His training schedule for that bid period will be reduced by a total of 4 days.</p>
4057:        <p>c.   An Instructor Pilot will have corresponding proficiency (PRO) flying eligibility during the SWW (see <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25E6">Section 25.E.6.</a>) as follows:</p>
4070:        <p>d.   In no event shall a pilot begin a pay only SWW bid period below the applicable Minimum Bid Period Guarantee, subject to the provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4A">Section 4.A.</a></p>
4073:      <p id="link_11N13" class="link_highlight">13. In anticipation of an instructional bid period, for Instructor Pilots (and certain Check Airman, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11M11f">Section 11.M.11.f.</a>) who are not initially scheduled for instructional duties or evaluations in an aircraft:</p>
4085:          <p id="link_11N13bii" class="link_highlight">ii.    The Company may assign a maximum of 15 instructional days in a 4-week bid period, 19 instructional days in a 5-week bid period, and 22 instructional days in a 6-week bid period, except where otherwise further limited by <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11N11">Section 11.N.11.</a></p>
4086:          <p>iii.   If he so desires, an Instructor Pilot may pick up an instructional activity by using credits in his General Make-Up Bank (GMB). Such activity does not constitute an excess of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11N13bii">Section 11.N.13.b.ii.</a> (maximum number of scheduled duty days). The applicable credit hour deduction from his GMB shall be R-day value for each such activity.</p>
4103:      <p id="link_11N15" class="link_highlight">15.    Flight Training Scheduling (FTS) may change a pilot’s instructional reserve period (to/from IR-A, IR-B), consistent with the provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25M3d">Section 25.M.3.d.i. through vi.</a></p>
4117:          <p>i. travel between the assigned training base and offsite training in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11N17">Section 11.N.17.</a>; and</p>
4120:        <p>e.   The provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_5A">Section 5.A.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_5B">B.</a> shall not apply while an Instructor Pilot is performing duties in his assigned training base.</p>
4136:      <p>23.    An Instructor Pilot may agree to reschedule his assigned duty days. An Instructor Pilot shall not be entitled to additional compensation as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11N25aiii">Section 11.N.25.a.iii.</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11N25bii">b.ii.</a>, as a result of the application of this paragraph, provided he receives his original number of scheduled days off.</p>
4165:        <p>c. In the case of an initial or higher level qualification, an Instructor Pilot candidate shall be paid the bid period override for that qualification upon commencement of his required training. Once qualified, an Instructor’s Bid Period Override shall be administered in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11N25e">Section 11.N.25.e.</a></p>
4175:      <p>26. An Instructor Pilot may participate in System Bids that close during his tenure as an Instructor Pilot, but will not receive an actual award without a release from his Training Manager as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11Q1">Section 11.Q.1.</a></p>
4181:        <p>d.   The crew position of an Instructor Pilot who resigns, or is released from his Instructor Pilot status absent an open System Bid or CIPPA crew position, shall be determined by comparing his system-wide seniority against the results of the most recent System Bid. If the pilot is awarded or assigned a different crew position than his current crew position, his training, or base transfer activation, shall be determined in the same manner as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_13A6e">Section 13.A.6.e.</a></p>
4189:      <p>The provisions of Sections 9.A.1. (second sentence only), <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11M1b">11.M.1.b., and </a><a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11M1c">M.1.c.</a>, shall be waived in case of an aircraft type new to the Company fleet.</p>
4195:        <p>c.   Check Airmen will use normal bidding processes for BLG and schedule determination in accordance with the provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11M5">Section 11.M.5.</a>, as applicable. A Check Airman shall bid in a pay only status in his previous crew position until the Company publishes a bid period package for the new aircraft type, at which point the Check Airman shall bid in the new aircraft crew position.</p>
4202:            <p> Example: Pilot A, a 757 Captain, holds an award to A300 CAP and is receiving passover pay to A300 CAP. He was part of the initial cadre of Check Airmen for the 757. Under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11O2dii">Section 11.O.2.d.ii.</a>, the Check Airman is initially compensated at the A300 CAP rate while working as a 757 Check Airman. Then, however, Pilot A is assigned from the A300 CAP seat to the MD-11 F/O seat. Pilot A is compensated as a 757 CAP under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11O2dii">Section 11.O.2.d.ii.</a> in the same manner as that by which the “Nth” CIPPA positions are determined, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11Q3a">Section 11.Q.3.a.</a> (using MD-11 F/O as the “applicable crew position”).</p>
4209:          <p>iii.   The scheduling of training, or base transfer activation, required by application of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11O2ei">Section 11.O.2.e.i.</a> or ii. shall be determined in the same manner as <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_13A6e">Section 13.A.6.e.</a></p>
4211:        <p>f.   A Check Airman shall not incur a passover or CIPPA repayment or a down/lateral bid restriction relating to his participation as a Check Airman under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11O">Section 11.O.</a></p>
4216:        <p>b.   A Provo shall bid in a pay only status in his previous crew position until the Company publishes a bid period package for the new aircraft type, at which point the Provo shall bid for vacation in the new aircraft crew position, but shall receive average BLG (for pay only) for the new aircraft crew position. The Provo’s schedule shall be governed by the applicable provisions of Section 11 as if the Provo was bidding in pay only status. Any revenue flying assignments must be accomplished in accordance with the provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25U">Section 25.U.</a> (Bumping for Training).</p>
4231:          <p>iii.   The scheduling of training, or base transfer activation, required by application of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11O3fi">Section 11.O.3.f.i.</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11O3fii">ii.</a> shall be determined in the same manner as <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_13A6e">Section 13.A.6.e.</a></p>
4233:        <p>g.   A Provo shall not incur a passover or CIPPA repayment obligation or a down/lateral bid restriction relating to the pilot’s participation as a Provo under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11O">Section 11.O.</a></p>
4238:        <p>b.   An initial cadre Check Airman shall be considered to be in the pool of pilots in the crew position for which the pilot is receiving the pay rate (e.g., a MD-11 MEM Captain, selected as an initial cadre pilot candidate, holds an award on the initial System Bid for the 757 MEM Captain, and receives, through the operation of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11O">Section 11.O.</a>, the pay rate for an MD-11 Captain; if a System Bid publishes a Current Staffing Level greater than Maximum Staffing Level, in the MD-11 MEM Captain crew position, the pilot will be considered as participating in that pool, and not as a 757 MEM Captain). If the pilot’s participation in that System Bid was in the crew position for which the pilot is performing duties as a Check Airman, the Company may continue to use the pilot as a Check Airman if the pilot is re-designated a Provo. In such case, the Company may continue to use the (newly designated) Provo until the expiration of 24 months following the introduction of the new aircraft into revenue service or 6 months after the close of that System Bid, whichever is later.</p>
4243:        <p id="link_11O5a" class="link_highlight">a.   In addition to other provisions of the Agreement, for each Provisional Check Airman who has been “activated” in the crew position as allowed under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11O3">Section 11.O.3.</a>, and for each Check Airman who activated earlier than his seniority would have dictated, one Line Pilot who holds an award for the new aircraft crew position will be entitled to the new aircraft pay rate if it is higher than their present rate.</p>
4251:        <p>b.   For Line Pilots receiving the new aircraft pay rate in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11O5a">Section 11.O.5.a.</a>, such pay shall end upon the earlier of:</p>
4266:      <p>The Company’s ability to assign an Instructor to conduct non-Validation/Evaluation Continuing Qualification (CQ) simulator event(s) resulting from a revision(s) to the CQ curriculum shall be subject to the process described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11A3a">Section 11.A.3.a.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11A3b">b.</a></p>
4270:        <p>b. Any crew seat not occupied by a pilot in training shall be occupied by a pilot who is current and qualified in that crew seat, except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11P6c">Section 11.P.6.c.</a> below.</p>
4281:      <p>11. Notwithstanding <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11P10">Section 11.P.10.</a>, and available seating permitting, a Check Airman or Instructor Pilot may observe, at the request of a pilot, his flight simulator training, aircraft training, OE or validation/evaluation event. In those cases, a Check Airman/Instructor Pilot is not entitled to additional compensation.</p>
4320:        <p>c.   In the event a CIPPA eligible pilot is not released to receive an actual award in another, subsequent System Bid, as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11Q2">Section 11.Q.2.</a>, he shall begin to receive his intervening CIPPA consistent with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11Q3a">Section 11.Q.3.a.</a></p>
4321:        <p>d.   A CIPPA eligible pilot who exhausts the full 24 bid periods described in Section 11.Q.3.b.v. above shall be released from his Check Airman or Instructor Pilot status, and he shall enter the pool of ITU training bidding in the same manner as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_13A6e">Section 13.A.6.e.</a> for the notional crew position award upon which his CIPPA was most recently based.</p>
4325:        <p>e.   A pilot’s monthly CIPPA dollar amount shall be determined by comparing his currently awarded crew position to his currently awarded notional (i.e., CIPPA eligible) crew position, and using the corresponding value in the SDP chart found in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24E">Section 24.E.</a></p>
4326:        <p>f.   CIPPA shall be paid on a monthly basis in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_3E1a">Section 3.E.1.a.</a></p>
4330:          <p>ii.    The pilot withdraws from training for the crew status upon which his CIPPA was based, unless extenuating circumstances existed for such withdrawal (<a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11J2a">Section 11.J.2.a.</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11J3">Section 11.J.3.</a>).</p>
4355:      <p id="link_12A2" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.A.2." rel="tooltip">2.</span> Except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12B3aiii">Section 12.B.3.a.iii.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12B3ciii">B.3.c.iii.</a> (Airport Standby), and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25M1g">Section 25.M.1.g.</a> (Reserve), a pilot shall be subject to operational limitations during a duty period within a trip. At all other times, a pilot shall be subject to scheduled limitations.</p>
4357:      <p>If the Company’s operations are disrupted due to extenuating circumstances not within the control of the Company, including, but not limited to, severe weather, natural disasters, abnormal ATC limitations or significant system disruptions, the Vice President, Flight Operations, or his designee, may declare an operational emergency. When an operational emergency is declared, all flight, duty time and rest limitations may be extended/reduced to FAR limits, except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D9">Section 12.D.9.</a> An operational emergency may be declared for a specific sort facility, a region of the system, nationwide or worldwide. In addition, the Company shall communicate the reasons for an operational emergency as soon as practicable but no later than 72 hours following the declaration thereof. In case of an operational emergency declared under this paragraph, the processes described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C5bii">Section 12.C.5.b.ii.</a> (domestic) and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D6cii">12.D.6.c.ii.</a> (international) shall apply.</p>
4363:              <p id="link_12A4aii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.A.4.a.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    more than 2 hours prior to showtime as required by <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1g">Section 12.D.1.g.</a> in situations involving ground transit time exceeding 1 hour; or</p>
4389:            <p id="link_12A6b" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.A.6.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span>   Should an operational emergency be declared as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12A3">Section 12.A.3.</a> due to severe weather, mechanical difficulties, or other extenuating circumstances in a designated sort facility, flight crews may be rescheduled or diverted to their base. Under these circumstances, the pilot’s base will be treated as a normal alternate and not as a base. As such, the trip will not terminate, but will continue as if originally transiting the scheduled sort facility (i.e., hub turn outbound or layover in base as if the pilot was on a layover at the originally scheduled sort facility).</p>
4391:      <p id="link_12A7" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.A.7." rel="tooltip">7.</span> The Company shall provide a bid period report to the Association which indicates the dates, flights and relevant circumstances in which the Vice President, Flight Operations, or his designee, exercised his authority to operationally extend a pilot beyond the <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C5">Section 12.C.5. and </a><a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D6">12.D.6.</a> operational duty limitations or as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12B3biic">Section 12.B.3.b.ii.(c)</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12B3diic">Section 12.B.3.d.ii.(c)</a>, except for extensions due to an operational emergency declared under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12A3">Section 12.A.3.</a></p>
4399:            <p id="link_12A8b" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.A.8.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span>   maintenance or weather disruptions particular to the pilot’s specific flight shall, but only to that limited extent, provide the Company with the ability to exceed the 36/84 hour limit without the pilot’s consent. Notifications of the use of this provision shall occur using the provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12A7">Section 12.A.7.</a></p>
4408:              <p id="link_12A9biii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.A.9.b.iii." rel="tooltip">iii.</span>   The pilot may be removed from his trip and placed in sick leave status as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_14B5">Section 14.B.5.</a>, subject to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12A9f">Section 12.A.9.f.</a> below; the pilot shall automatically be returned from sick leave at the conclusion of his trip.</p>
4413:            <p id="link_12A9f" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.A.9.f." rel="tooltip">f.</span>   A pilot who calls fatigued away from base during a trip shall be treated in the same manner as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_14B4">Section 14.B.4.</a>, and shall have local transportation and lodging provided by the Company.</p>
4414:            <p id="link_12A9g" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.A.9.g." rel="tooltip">g.</span>    The FERC shall meet and discuss all pilot fatigue calls made subsequent to actual trip check-in. For instances to which <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12A9biii">Section 12.A.9.b.iii.</a> applied, the FERC will evaluate the circumstances surrounding the fatigue call and will attempt to reach a consensus concerning compensation for that trip, or portion thereof, not operated owing to the fatigue call.</p>
4433:            <p id="link_12A10b" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.A.10.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span>   The Association consents to the study of ULR pairings (Category 1). Specific ULR pairing designs shall be approved in advance, unanimously by the Data Collection Steering Committee (DCSC) (e.g., flight sequence, layover times, location, departure and arrival times, time free from duty prior to and after the pairing). The DCSC will make decisions based upon available sleep science. Such pairings shall comply with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12E">Section 12.E.</a></p>
4438:            <p id="link_12A10g" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.A.10.g." rel="tooltip">g.</span>   FRMS study pairings not assigned by the applicable assignment window, as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25G3a">Section 25.G.3.a.</a>, shall be:</p>
4441:              <p id="link_12A10gii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.A.10.g.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    Notwithstanding <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25P">Section 25.P.</a>, assigned to management pilots as originally designed but without data collection. <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_9A3">Section 9.A.3.</a> shall not apply to management assignments pursuant to this paragraph.</p>
4445:            <p id="link_12A10j" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.A.10.j." rel="tooltip">j.</span>   Association members of the DCSC and FRMG shall be removed from flying as provided for FOQA Gatekeepers under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_18A2a">Section 18.A.2.a.</a> and shall be compensated and treated accordingly under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_18B">Section 18.B.</a></p>
4472:            <p id="link_12B1f" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.B.1.f." rel="tooltip">f.</span>   Except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12B2">Section 12.B.2.</a>, when the last activity of a duty period is a deadhead by surface transportation that duty period shall terminate at the scheduled arrival time of the surface deadhead.</p>
4492:            <p id="link_12B3biic" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.B.3.b.ii.(c)." rel="tooltip">(c)</span>  The 12 hour rest requirement provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12B3biia">Section 12.B.3.b.ii.(a)</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12B3biib">(b)</a> may be reduced to the rest requirements of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C6">Section 12.C.6.</a>, or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D7">12.D.7.</a>, as applicable. This may only be done by the Vice President, Flight Operations, or his designee, in cases of operational emergency, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12A3">Section 12.A.3.</a>, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C5b">12.C.5.b.</a>, or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D6c">12.D.6.c.</a> If that occurs, the reduction in rest shall be reported to the Association in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12A7">Section 12.A.7.</a></p>
4493:            <p id="link_12B3biid" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.B.3.b.ii.(d)." rel="tooltip">(d)</span>  If the pilot returns to base within his standby period, the provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12B3bvi">Section 12.B.3.b.vi.</a>, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12B3bvii">vii.</a>, and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12B3bviii">viii</a>. shall apply.</p>
4501:          <p id="link_12B3bviii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.B.3.b.viii." rel="tooltip">viii.</span>  If a pilot resumes base hotel standby duty as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12B3bvi">Section 12.B.3.b.vi.</a>, or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12B3bvii">vii.</a>, CRS may:</p>
4515:          <p id="link_12B3cvi" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.B.3.c.vi." rel="tooltip">vi.</span>    If a pilot resumes standby duty as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12B3civ">Section 12.B.3.c.iv.</a>, or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12B3cv">v.</a>, CRS may:</p>
4525:            <p id="link_12B3cviiib" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.B.3.c.viii.(b)." rel="tooltip">(b)</span>  the pilot may be scheduled to layover in his base prior to the application of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12B3cviiia">Section 12.B.3.c.viii.(a)</a>.</p>
4531:          <p id="link_12B3dii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.B.3.d.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    A field hotel standby pilot may only be assigned duty commencing during the standby period. However, if a pilot’s pairing is revised, in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25S">Section 25.S.</a>, the following shall apply:</p>
4535:            <p id="link_12B3diic" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.B.3.d.ii.(c)." rel="tooltip">(c)</span>  The 12 hour rest requirement provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12B3diia">Section 12.B.3.d.ii.(a)</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12B3diib">(b)</a> may be reduced to the rest requirements of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C6">Section 12.C.6.</a>, or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D7">12.D.7.</a>, as applicable. This may only be done by the Vice President, Flight Operations, or his designee, in cases of operational emergency, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12A3">Section 12.A.3.</a>, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C5b">12.C.5.b.</a>, or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D6c">12.D.6.c.</a> If that occurs, the reduction in rest shall be reported to the Association in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12A7">Section 12.A.7.</a></p>
4536:            <p id="link_12B3diid" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.B.3.d.ii.(d)." rel="tooltip">(d)</span>  If the pilot returns to his standby city within his standby period, the provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12B3dvi">Section 12.B.3.d.vi.</a>, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12B3dvii">vii.</a>, and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12B3dviii">viii.</a> shall apply.</p>
4544:          <p id="link_12B3dviii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.B.3.d.viii." rel="tooltip">viii.</span>  If a pilot resumes field hotel standby duty as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12B3dvi">Section 12.B.3.d.vi.</a>, or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12B3dvii">vii.</a>, CRS may:</p>
4553:            <p id="link_12B3dixb" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.B.3.d.ix.(b)." rel="tooltip">(b)</span>  the pilot may be scheduled to layover in his base prior to the application of Section <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12B3dixa">12.B.3.d.ix.(a).</a></p>
4563:        <p>Domestic provisions apply to activities conducted entirely within the contiguous 48 states, and to trips constructed under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1b">Section 12.D.1.b.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1c">c.</a> (International Provisions).</p>
4571:        <p id="link_12C2a" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.C.2.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   A pilot shall not be scheduled as an operating crew member in excess of 8 block hours during a single duty period or during any consecutive 24 hour period, except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C2b">Section 12.C.2.b.</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C2d">d.</a></p>
4572:        <p id="link_12C2b" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.C.2.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span>   A pilot may be scheduled as an operating crew member to exceed 8 block hours during any 24 consecutive hours. Prior to exceeding 8 ABH in that period, however, he shall have received an intervening legal rest period of twice the block hours flown since his last legal rest period, or 9 hours, whichever is greater, except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C2cii">Section 12.C.2.c.ii.</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C2ciii">iii.</a></p>
4573:        <p id="link_12C2c" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.C.2.c." rel="tooltip">c.</span>   A pilot originally scheduled under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C2a">Section 12.C.2.a.</a>, or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C2b">b.</a>, but who, due to headwinds, ATC delays or other unavoidable circumstances (including an intermediate stop for these reasons) is projected to exceed the limitations contained in those paragraphs, may continue to the extent permitted by FAR regulations. Duty time and rest limitations as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C5">Section 12.C.5.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C6">C.6.</a> still apply.</p>
4576:          <p id="link_12C2cii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.C.2.c.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    If a pilot is originally scheduled to exceed 8 block hours in 24 consecutive hours, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C2b">Section 12.C.2.b.</a>, but due to headwinds, ATC delays or other unavoidable circumstances (including any intermediate stops for these reasons), cannot receive the minimum required legal rest period, the following shall apply:</p>
4595:            <p id="link_12C2dib" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.C.2.d.i.(b)." rel="tooltip">(b)</span>  As awarded/assigned, he may be scheduled for one additional flight segment after having exceeded 7:35 block hours during that 24 consecutive hour period. Operationally, however, he may block-out on two scheduled flight segments during the duty period after having exceeded 8 ABH during that 24 consecutive hour period, provided that his intervening rest (described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C2dia">Section 12.C.2.d.i.(a)</a>) was at least 10:15; and</p>
4607:        <p>Crew Planning limitations shall apply until 48 hours prior to showtime of a trip or series of trips, except that such limitations do not apply to a sequence of trips that includes an optional assignment (e.g., make-up, trip trade, volunteer or draft). Trips constructed and revisions that occur after that time shall be governed by <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C4">Section 12.C.4.</a> through C.6., as applicable.</p>
4634:        <p>If the showtime for a duty period is between 0500 and 1559 LBT, that duty period shall be limited to a maximum of 13 hours scheduled, except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C4d">Sections 12.C.4.d.</a>, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C4e">e.</a>, or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C4f">f.</a></p>
4636:        <p>If the showtime for a duty period is between 1600 and 0059 LBT, that duty period shall be limited to a maximum of 11:30 hours scheduled, except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C4d">Sections 12.C.4.d.</a>, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C4e">e.</a>, or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C4f">f.</a></p>
4638:        <p>If the showtime for a duty period is between 0100 and 0459 LBT, that duty period shall be limited to a maximum of 9 hours scheduled, except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C4g">Section 12.C.4.g.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C4h">C.4.h.</a></p>
4640:        <p>Transitions between the scheduled duty limits set forth in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C4a">Section 12.C.4.a.</a>, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C4b">b.</a>, and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C4c">c.</a> shall be as follows:</p>
4650:          <p id="link_12C4ei" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.C.4.e.i." rel="tooltip">i.</span> If the duty period is less than the scheduled on-duty limitations of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C4a">Section 12.C.4.a.</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C4b">b.</a> (i.e., 13 Day and 11:30 Night), then the applicable scheduled on-duty limit (i.e., 13 Day and 11:30 Night) shall still apply.</p>
4651:          <p id="link_12C4eii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.C.4.e.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>   If the duty period comprised of 2 trips exceeds the scheduled on-duty limitations of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C4a">Section 12.C.4.a.</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C4b">b.</a> (i.e., 13 Day and 11:30 Night), then the duty period shall be limited to a maximum of 13:30 (Day)/13:00 (Night) scheduled on-duty.</p>
4653:        <p id="link_12C4f" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.C.4.f." rel="tooltip">f.</span>   If a duty period is comprised exclusively of deadhead, the scheduled on-duty limitations contained in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C4a">Section 12.C.4.a.</a>, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C4b">b.</a>, or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C4c">c.</a> shall apply.</p>
4658:          <p id="link_12C4gii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.C.4.g.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    If the duty period began in the day or night period, the entire duty period may be scheduled up to 2 hours beyond the scheduled limitations in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C4a">Section 12.C.4.a.</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C4b">b.</a>, in order to accomplish the deadhead. However, the portion of the duty period prior to check-in for the deadhead shall be scheduled to the on-duty limitations contained in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C4a">Section 12.C.4.a.</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C4b">b.</a>, as applicable.</p>
4661:        <p id="link_12C4i" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.C.4.i." rel="tooltip">i.</span>   If a pilot is scheduled to deadhead to base after revenue flying, and his duty period exceeds 10 hours, he may obtain a hotel room at Company expense, in order to take a later flight, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_5B1f">Section 5.B.1.f.</a></p>
4757:        <p>A pilot shall not be operationally extended more than 1:30 past the applicable scheduled on-duty limitation, except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C5aii">Section 12.C.5.a.ii.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C5b">12.C.5.b.</a> The “applicable scheduled on-duty limitation” is the maximum scheduled on duty limitation in each category (i.e., day, night, critical, deadhead to base or optional trip trade, VLT, etc.), with reference to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C4a">Section 12.C.4.a.</a>, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C4b">b.</a>, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C4c">c.</a>, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C4d">d.</a>, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C4e">e.</a>, or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C4f">f.</a>, except that if the scheduled duty limit is blended, then the operational duty limit shall be 1:30 more than that specific blended limit.</p>
4759:          <p id="link_12C5ai" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.C.5.a.i." rel="tooltip">i.</span> If a pilot’s duty period was properly scheduled as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C4div">Section 12.C.4.d.iv.</a>, such pilot’s scheduled duty limit remains the maximum scheduled on duty limit for his category, regardless of operational events affecting the pilot’s scheduled ground time, or ability to use his day room (e.g., delayed inbound).</p>
4768:          <p id="link_12C5bi" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.C.5.b.i." rel="tooltip">i.</span> A pilot may, subject to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C5bii">Section 12.C.5.b.ii.</a>, be scheduled to continue up to FAR duty limits, with the prior approval of the Vice President, Flight Operations, or his designee, if necessary to complete his scheduled or rescheduled flight sequence or return to base, whichever occurs first. Block time limitations as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C2c">Section 12.C.2.c.</a> still apply.</p>
4773:            <p id="link_12C5biic" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.C.5.b.ii.(c)." rel="tooltip">(c)</span>  Should it be determined that the pilot requires more rest than the legal rest provided pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C5biib">Section 12.C.5.b.ii.(b)</a>, the pilot may be removed from the balance of his trip and be placed in sick leave status. If the pilot is placed in sick leave status the pilot shall be automatically returned from sick leave at the conclusion of his trip.</p>
4774:            <p id="link_12C5biid" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.C.5.b.ii.(d)." rel="tooltip">(d)</span>  The FERC shall meet and discuss all instances to which <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C5bii">12.C.5.b.ii.</a> applied.</p>
4776:          <p id="link_12C5biii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.C.5.b.iii." rel="tooltip">iii.</span>   Deadheads that are necessary in any of the situations described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C5bii">Section 12.C.5.b.ii.</a> shall be accomplished in accordance with the Agreement.</p>
4786:          <p id="link_12C6bi" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.C.6.b.i." rel="tooltip">i.</span> 17 hours prior to performing his next duty as an operating crew member, when <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C2b">Sections 12.C.2.b.</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C2c">c.</a> are applicable. This rest period may be operationally reduced as necessary, consistent with FAR limitations; or</p>
4787:          <p id="link_12C6bii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.C.6.b.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    13 hours prior to performing his next duty as an operating crew member, when <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C2di">Sections 12.C.2.d.i.</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C2dii">ii.</a> are applicable. This rest period may be operationally reduced to 12 hours.</p>
4790:        <p id="link_12C6d" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.C.6.d." rel="tooltip">d.</span>   If a pilot operationally receives a layover of less than 11 hours, immediately following operation in the critical period, his next layover must be at least 12 hours, unless the remainder of his trip contains only deadheading, except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12A3">Section 12.A.3.</a> (operational emergency).</p>
4797:        <p id="link_12D1a" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.D.1.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   Except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1b">Section 12.D.1.b.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1c">c.</a>, international provisions apply to flight activities of pilots that originate from, have a destination of, or make an intermediate stop at a location outside the contiguous 48 states. A scheduled international flight activity that actually operates entirely within the 48 contiguous states shall be governed by the domestic provisions contained in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C">Section 12.C.</a></p>
4798:        <p id="link_12D1b" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.D.1.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span>   Domestic rest limitations may be applied to SIBA and FDA trips operating entirely outside the locations described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1ci">Section 12.D.1.c.i.</a>, provided that they are scheduled not to exceed domestic block hour and on-duty limitations. Such trips must also meet the following:</p>
4808:          <p id="link_12D1bv" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.D.1.b.v." rel="tooltip">v.</span> An international legal rest period must follow a deadhead to and from a SIBA or FDA base in a trip on which a pilot, other than a pilot on SIBA or FDA, deadheads to and from a SIBA or FDA base to perform flying described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1b">Section 12.D.1.b.</a> (i.e., the pilot is not assigned to the SIBA or FDA location, but is assigned to fly a trip at such a location).</p>
4813:          <p id="link_12D1cii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.D.1.c.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>   For FDA pilots, trips operated exclusively within the “European theater.” For purposes of this provision, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1cii">Section 12.D.1.c.ii.</a>, the “European theater” includes airports west of 40 degrees east longitude, north of 30 degrees north latitude and east of 10 degrees west longitude.</p>
4818:          <p id="link_12D1ciii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.D.1.c.iii." rel="tooltip">iii.</span>   If the Company opens a new FDA to operate trips that are not in the European theater, the parties shall meet and discuss whether trips assigned to that base should be eligible for construction under Section <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1c">12.D.1.c.</a> If the Company and the Association agree, trips in that new FDA may be constructed under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1c">Section 12.D.1.c.</a></p>
4823:          <p id="link_12D1dii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.D.1.d.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    A pilot shall be relieved of all duty and reserve availability for at least 48 consecutive hours at the conclusion of an international trip that exceeds 120 hours TAFB, except for trips scheduled in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1ci">Section 12.D.1.c.i.</a> If the 48 hour buffer conflicts with an R-24 pilot’s notification window, he shall be responsible for reserve assignments placed in VIPS at least 24 hours prior to the scheduled showtime of the assignment (as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25M3avb">Section 25.M.3.a.v.(b)</a>).</p>
4824:          <p id="link_12D1diii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.D.1.d.iii." rel="tooltip">iii.</span>   A pilot may waive the international buffers set forth in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1di">Section 12.D.1.d.i.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1dii">ii.</a> A pilot is deemed to have waived any conflict with the international buffer resulting from a bid line adjustment, reassignment trip, or a volunteer or draft assignment.</p>
4830:          <p id="link_12D1eii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.D.1.e.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    operational requirements prevent the positioning pilot from being scheduled in compliance with normal scheduling parameters (i.e., <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D5">Section 12.D.5.</a>); and</p>
4832:          <p id="link_12D1eiv" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.D.1.e.iv." rel="tooltip">iv.</span>    the class of service for a deadhead scheduled for less than 16 hours on duty shall comply with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_8A5ci">Section 8.A.5.c.i.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_8A5cii">ii.</a> The class of service for a deadhead scheduled to exceed 16 hours on duty shall comply with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_8A5civb">Section 8.A.5.c.iv.(b)</a>. A lower class of service may be authorized by the Vice President, Flight Operations, or his designee. In any case, the pilot’s deviation bank shall be credited as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_8A5cvi">Section 8.A.5.c.vi.</a> (highest available class); and</p>
4857:      <p>The international grid and its related crew planning limitations shall apply until 96 hours prior to the showtime of an international trip or series of trips, other than those scheduled in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1b">Section 12.D.1.b.</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1c">c.</a> Trips constructed and revisions that occur after that time shall be governed by <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D3">Section 12.D.3.</a> through D.10.</p>
5118:          <td><p><a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D5b">Section 12.D.5.b.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D5c">c.</a></p></td>
5132:        <p>A pilot operating as part of a two pilot crew shall not be scheduled in excess of the block hour limitation provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C2a">Section 12.C.2.a.</a> through c. (8-in-24 and related rules).</p>
5144:        <p>A pilot operating as part of a two pilot crew shall be subject to the operational block hour limitations provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C2a">Sections 12.C.2.a.</a> through c. (8-in-24 and related rules).</p>
5146:        <p>If a pilot operating as part of a three pilot crew (CAP and F/O and RFO or RF2) is projected to exceed the scheduled block hour limitations provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D3b">Section 12.D.3.b.</a>, since the completion of his last international legal rest period due to headwinds, ATC limitations, or other unavoidable circumstances (including an intermediate stop for these reasons), he may continue to his base or his original destination, whichever occurs first. However, a crew shall not block out from a location after having exceeded 12 ABH in a 24 hour period without a legal rest period.</p>
5153:        <p>If a duty period is comprised entirely of deadhead, that duty period shall be limited to a maximum of 16 hours scheduled on duty, except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D5c">Section 12.D.5.c.</a></p>
5155:        <p>Deadheads may be scheduled over 16 hours, but not more than 22 hours (<a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_8A3bvii">Section 8.A.3.b.vii.</a>), in a single duty period subject to the procedures outlined in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_8A5civ">Section 8.A.5.c.iv</a>.</p>
5159:        <p id="link_12D6a" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.D.6.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   The 13:30 hour scheduled on-duty limitation contained in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D5a">Section 12.D.5.a.</a> may be operationally extended to a maximum of 15:00 hours.</p>
5160:        <p id="link_12D6b" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.D.6.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span>   The 16 hour scheduled on-duty limitation contained in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D5b">Section 12.D.5.b.</a> may be operationally extended to a maximum of 17:30 hours.</p>
5167:          <p id="link_12D6ci" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.D.6.c.i." rel="tooltip">i.</span> A pilot may, subject to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D6cii">Section 12.D.6.c.ii.</a>, be scheduled to continue on duty up to 1:30 past operational limits, or 16 hours, whichever is greater, with the prior approval of the Vice President, Flight Operations, or his designee, if necessary to complete his scheduled or rescheduled flight sequence or return to base, whichever occurs first. Block time limitations as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D4">Section 12.D.4.</a> still apply.</p>
5172:            <p id="link_12D6ciic" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.D.6.c.iii.(c)." rel="tooltip">(c)</span>  Should it be determined that the pilot requires more rest than the legal rest provided pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D6ciib">Section 12.D.6.c.ii.(b)</a>, the pilot may be removed from the balance of his trip and be placed in sick leave status. If the pilot is placed in sick leave status, the pilot shall be automatically returned from sick leave at the conclusion of his trip.</p>
5173:            <p id="link_12D6ciid" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.D.6.c.iii.(d)." rel="tooltip">(d)</span>  The FERC shall meet and discuss all instances to which <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D6cii">Section 12.D.6.c.ii.</a> applied.</p>
5175:          <p id="link_12D6ciii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.D.6.c.iii." rel="tooltip">iii.</span>   Deadheads that are necessary in any of the situations described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D6cii">Section 12.D.6.c.ii.</a> shall be accomplished in accordance with the Agreement.</p>
5182:        <p id="link_12D7b" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.D.7.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span>   An international duty period shall be preceded by a duty free period of not less than 12 hours, except for international trips scheduled to domestic parameters (as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1b">Section 12.D.1.b.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1c">c.</a>).</p>
5187:          <p id="link_12D7ciii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.D.7.c.iii." rel="tooltip">iii.</span>   to a minimum of 12 hours, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D7d">Section 12.D.7.d.</a></p>
