5190:        <p id="link_12D7e" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.D.7.e." rel="tooltip">e.</span>   Except for international trips scheduled to domestic parameters (as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1b">Section 12.D.1.b.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1c">c.</a>), upon completion of an international duty period and prior to a domestic duty period, a pilot shall receive a minimum international legal rest period unless a greater legal rest period is required.</p>
5209:        <p>The following additional limits apply to trips governed by <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D3">Section 12.D.3.</a> through 8., even in situations covered by <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12A3">Section 12.A.3.</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D6ci">12.D.6.c.i.</a></p>
5211:        <p id="link_12D9b" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.D.9.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span>   Any extension beyond operational limits as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12A3">Section 12.A.3.</a>, or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D6ci">D.6.c.i.</a>, shall be limited to 1:30 past operational limits, or 16 hours, whichever is greater.</p>
5214:      <p>This paragraph applies to all international trips except for international trips constructed under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1b">Section 12.D.1.b.</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1c">c.</a></p>
5219:          <p id="link_12D10ii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.D.10.a.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    A pilot’s layover was less than the applicable International Grid Minimum Layover (i.e., 14 hours or 12 based on the chart in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D2e">Section 12.D.2.e.</a>).</p>
5220:          <p id="link_12D10aiii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.D.10.a.iii." rel="tooltip">iii.</span>    A pilot received more than 4 “not adjusted” rests in a row. Each rest after 3 non-adjusted rests shall be a separate GPE event. An initial GPE occurs when the pilot’s fifth duty period begins without the pilot having received at least 18 hours free from duty preceding the beginning of that duty period. For purposes of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D10aiii">Section 12.D.10.a.iii.</a> (this paragraph) only, an unassigned hotel standby period shall be counted as part of the rest periods preceding and/or following it (e.g., an unassigned 11:30 hotel standby period, followed by a 12:30 rest period will be counted as an adjusted rest).</p>
5223:          <p>If a pilot’s trip did not conform to 30-in-120 (as set forth in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D2g">Section 12.D.2.g.</a>, except using 30 instead of 32 hours), he shall be paid 3 CH in addition to all other compensation regardless of the 48-hour period as stated in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D10c">Section 12.D.10.c.</a>, and the event shall be additive to the total count of GPEs for the trip.</p>
5225:          <p>If a pilot’s trip did not conform to 34-in-168 (as set forth in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D2g">Section 12.D.2.g.</a>, except using 34 instead of 36 hours), he shall be paid 3 CH in addition to all other compensation regardless of the 48-hour period as stated in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D10c">Section 12.D.10.c.</a>, and the event shall be additive to the total count of GPEs for the trip.</p>
5227:        <p id="link_12D10" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.D.10.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span>   If all GPEs in a trip touch a single 48 hour period, no grid penalty shall be due, except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D10av">Section 12.D.10.a.v.</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D10avi">vi.</a></p>
5274:      <p id="link_12Ec" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.E.3." rel="tooltip">3.</span> As provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12A10">Section 12.A.10.</a>, ULR operations shall be evaluated as part of the FRMS. In addition to the provisions in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12A10">Section 12.A.10.</a>, following the FRMS study, and with the unanimous approval of the Scientific Advisory Committee, the Company may seek approval by the FAA for ULR city pair flight segments which shall include the specific pairing design as approved by the DCSC. If approved, the specific pairing design shall not be materially altered without the consent of the Association.</p>
5276:      <p>Upon the FAA’s approval of ULR operations under the Company’s FRMS, and notwithstanding <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D8">Section 12.D.8.</a>, all ULR-related provisions contained in this Agreement shall become immediately applicable for the specific pairing design approved by the FAA.</p>
5282:        <p>A ULR crew may be scheduled to a maximum of 20 hours on duty, which may be extended to 21:30 hours operational. Any extension beyond the operational limit up to legal limits shall include the protections contained in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D6c">Section 12.D.6.c.</a></p>
5288:        <p id="link_12Edh" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 12.E.4h." rel="tooltip">h.</span>   The parties recognize that the matters governed by <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12E">Section 12.E.</a> are new to the system and involve as yet unforeseen operational considerations. As a result, the parties foresee that flexibility will be required in order to ensure the smoothest possible transition to the application of ULR rules. To that end, measures facilitating the implementation, operation, and/or administration of the provisions in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12E">Section 12.E.</a> may be implemented if agreed upon in writing by the Vice President, Labor Relations and the Association’s MEC Chairman.</p>
5301:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 13.A.1." rel="tooltip">1.</span> A pilot’s filing for a leave of absence shall be directed to his Fleet Captain. The filing shall be submitted as far in advance as practicable prior to the intended start of the leave filed for, except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_13B1">Section 13.B.1.</a> (Personal Leave of Absence). The filing shall contain a statement of the type of leave and the reason(s) for which the leave of absence is being filed for, except that reasons for a Medical Leave of Absence shall be sent to the Company’s aeromedical advisor, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_13C">Section 13.C.</a> The pilot’s Fleet Captain, or his designee, shall respond in writing to a filing for a leave of absence as soon as practicable, but in no event later than 15 calendar days following receipt of the filing.</p>
5302:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 13.A.2." rel="tooltip">2.</span> A pilot returning from a leave of absence is expected to possess FAA certificates and ratings consistent with the crew status to which the pilot is returning, as provided in Section <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24A3a">24.A.3.a.</a></p>
5303:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 13.A.3." rel="tooltip">3.</span> A pilot returning from a leave of absence, other than a medical leave of absence, who does not possess an FAA medical certificate, shall be placed on sick leave or Medical Leave of Absence, provided the pilot is otherwise eligible for that leave as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_13C">Section 13.C.</a> (including verification of his medical condition by the Company’s aeromedical advisor if required by the Company).</p>
5304:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 13.A.4." rel="tooltip">4.</span> Rules of conduct applicable to pilots in active service apply to pilots on leaves of absence. The standard for administering discipline and discharge for a pilot on a leave of absence shall be as provided in Section 19. Notice for preliminary hearings and other disciplinary proceedings shall be sent in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_19E1">Section 19.E.1.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_19F4">Section 19.F.4.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_19F5">5.</a> A pilot may designate in writing an alternative mailing address for all notices.</p>
5310:      <p id="link_13A6ai" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 13.A.6.a.i." rel="tooltip">i.</span> The contact shall occur at least 30 days prior to the anticipated end of his leave of absence. The Fleet Captain shall confirm, in writing if requested, the return date and resumption to active pay status, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_13A6aii">Section 13.A.6.a.ii.</a></p>
5311:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 13.A.6.a.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    Provided that a pilot has complied with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_13A6ai">Section 13.A.6.a.i.</a>, the pilot shall be returned to active pay status upon his return. Failure to comply with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_13A6ai">Section 13.A.6.a.i.</a> may result in the pilot’s return to active pay status being delayed an amount equal to the notification delay. In no case shall the pilot be returned to active pay status later than 30 days following the pilot’s return date.</p>
5325:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 13.A.6.c.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    A System Bid closed during his absence, but he did not (or could not) select a new crew position (as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_13A6bii">Section 13.A.6.b.ii.</a>).</p>
5327:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 13.A.6.d." rel="tooltip">d.</span>   If upon returning to active status from a leave of absence, the pilot’s current crew position differs from the pilot’s currently awarded/assigned crew position, the pilot’s training shall be handled in the same manner as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_13A6e">Section 13.A.6.e.</a></p>
5328:    <p id="link_13A6e" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 13.A.6.e." rel="tooltip">e.</span>   If the pilot selects a new crew position (as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_13A6bii">Section 13.A.6.b.ii.</a> above), training for that crew position shall be as follows:</p>
5340:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 13.A.6.f." rel="tooltip">f.</span> A pilot returning from a leave of absence who requires training prior to returning to line flying shall be compensated as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4I6">Section 4.I.6.</a></p>
5343:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 13.A.6.g.i." rel="tooltip">i.</span> A pilot whose return coincides with the beginning of a bid period shall be afforded the opportunity to bid for that bid period in the normal bid process prior to his return, in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25C6">Section 25.C.6.</a></p>
5344:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 13.A.6.g.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    A pilot who returns for a portion of a bid period shall be assigned a custom line (<a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25I">Section 25.I.</a>) for the bid period in which he returns.</p>
5362:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 13.A.13.d." rel="tooltip">d.</span>   If a pilot’s vacation is unable to be rescheduled/assigned as provided above, the vacation bank shall be bought back, subject to the provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_7G6">Section 7.G.6.</a>, or as an exception to the 40% buy back, the pilot may request to have the CH of vacation paid. Any vacation not bought back shall be a positive adjustment to the pilot’s vacation bank for the following year.</p>
5365:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 13.A.14." rel="tooltip">14.</span>    Any medical information received by the Company’s aeromedical advisor under this Section shall be treated on the same basis as medical information in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_15H">Section 15.H.</a></p>
5375:      <p id="link_13C2" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 13.C.2." rel="tooltip">2.</span> The Company may require a pilot filing for a Medical Leave of Absence to submit medical documentation substantiating the need for such leave from a physician selected by the pilot. Such medical documentation shall be submitted to the Company’s aeromedical advisor. The Company’s aeromedical advisor shall inform the pilot’s Fleet Captain as to whether the pilot is able to perform his duties due to illness or injury, in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_15H">Section 15.H.</a> Disputes concerning a pilot’s physical condition shall be resolved as provided in Section 15 (Medical Standards).</p>
5384:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 13.D.5." rel="tooltip">5.</span> Contract requirements and guidance pertaining to short-term periods of service (less than 31 days) are found in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25X">Section 25.X.</a></p>
5430:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 14.A.1." rel="tooltip">1.</span> The purpose of sick leave is to protect a pilot from loss of pay, to the extent of his sick leave accrual, when the pilot is unable to perform his assigned duties because of injury, physical or mental illness, or trip fatigue as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12A9">Section 12.A.9.</a>, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C5bii">Section 12.C.5.b.ii.</a>, and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D6c">Section 12.D.6.c.</a></p>
5434:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 14.A.3.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   If a pilot is on furlough on the last day of the calendar year, the balance of his regular sick account, if any, shall be transferred to his disability sick account or to the surplus program, as applicable in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_14D">Section 14.D.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_14E">14.E.</a></p>
5451:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 14.A.6.c." rel="tooltip">c.</span>   The pilot has requested to utilize his disability sick account in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_14D2a">Section 14.D.2.a.</a></p>
5453:  <p id="link_14A7" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 14.A.7." rel="tooltip">7.</span> A pilot may elect to use vacation CH to delay or avoid going on disability. Failure to exercise this election is a factor that may result in forfeiture of CH from his vacation bank pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_7G6">Section 7.G.6.</a> (40% limitation on vacation buy back).</p>
5464:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 14.B.2.b.i." rel="tooltip">i.</span> At 0700 LBT each day, any trip with 120 hours TAFB or more, with a showtime during the next two local base days that is assigned to a pilot who is on sick leave shall be available in open time for Bid Line Adjustments as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25L">Section 25.L.</a> At 1000 LBT, such trips shall become available for assignment by CRS.</p>
5465:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 14.B.2.b.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    At 0700 LBT each day, any trip with less than 120 hours TAFB, with a showtime during the next local base day that is assigned to a pilot who is on sick leave shall be available in open time for Bid Line Adjustments as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25L">Section 25.L.</a> At 1000 LBT, such trips shall become available for assignment by CRS, with the exception of trips with a showtime prior to 1800 LBT that same day, which shall become available for assignment by CRS at 0900 LBT.</p>
5472:      <p id="link_14B2ciii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 14.B.2.c.iii." rel="tooltip">iii.</span>   A reserve pilot on sick leave shall be assigned open time as if he were not on sick leave (<a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25G3">Section 25.G.3.</a> Open Time Assignment and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25M6">Section 25.M.6.</a> Reserve Assignment Options). A reserve pilot will maintain his leveling position on the reserve list, and the scheduled credit hours for any trips he is assigned and removed as sick will be credited toward his RLG/mini-RLG and deducted from his sick bank. Commencing at 0900 LBT each day, a reserve pilot with an assignment(s) having a showtime during the next day shall be removed for sick leave and such assignment shall be available for open time assignment by CRS.</p>
5476:  <p>A pilot who is no longer ill or injured shall promptly notify the Company via VIPS, consistent with other provisions of this Agreement (e.g., medical clearance if required, Section 15 process if applicable). Except as provided by <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12A9">Section 12.A.9.</a>, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C5bii">Section 12.C.5.b.ii.</a>, and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D6c">Section 12.D.6.c.</a>, a pilot shall remain in sick leave status until he notifies the Company via VIPS of his ability to return to flight status and, if applicable, is released by the Company aeromedical advisor to return to duty. If the pilot so elects, in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_14A5a">Section 14.A.5.a.</a>, then he shall be given his original assignment(s) if it has not been reassigned to another pilot.</p>
5493:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 14.B.5.f" rel="tooltip">f.</span>   The sick leave account of a pilot scheduled for recurrent training shall be charged for all hours of pay received (as applicable in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4I4">Section 4.I.4.</a>, Recurrent Training Pay), but not worked as a result of sick leave.</p>
5494:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 14.B.5.g" rel="tooltip">g.</span>   If a pilot, having commenced initial, transition or upgrade training, is unable to attend that training due to sick leave, he shall be compensated as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4I5">Section 4.I.5.</a>, and his sick leave account(s) shall be reduced by 3 CH for each day sick on a scheduled event, not to exceed his BLG/RLG.</p>
5501:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 14.B.5.i.iii." rel="tooltip">iii.</span>   If he is unavailable for a day(s) of substitution eligibility, and a deduction was not made as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_14B5ii">Section 14.B.5.i.i.</a> for that day, trip rig shall be calculated for the period the pilot is unavailable due to sick leave, and shall be credited toward his substitution guarantee and deducted from his sick leave account.</p>
5506:  <p>A pilot who has been on sick leave for at least 30 days prior to the monthly bid closing and/or is expected to be on sick leave for the entire bid period shall bid pay only unless his Fleet Captain authorizes him to bid a line for flying purposes. However, a pilot who, at the time of bid closing, is activated but is not qualified in his assigned crew position shall be handled in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25C6">Section 25.C.6.</a> Unless such pilot is assigned a custom line as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25I">Section 25.I.</a>, he shall be compensated the BLG or RLG of his pay only line and his sick leave account(s) shall be reduced by the same amount. If assigned a Custom Line, any credit hours earned as a result shall be credited to the applicable sick leave account(s).</p>
5514:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 14.C.2." rel="tooltip">2.</span> A pilot not in active pay status on the first day of the first bid period of a calendar year shall be credited with 6 CH for each bid period remaining in the calendar year beginning with the bid period in which he returns to paid status, subject to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_14C5">Section 14.C.5.</a></p>
5515:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 14.C.3." rel="tooltip">3.</span> During the calendar year in which a pilot is hired, he shall be credited with 6 CH for each bid period remaining in such calendar year, subject to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_14C5">Section 14.C.5.</a></p>
5520:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 14.C.6.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   A pilot removed from an activity due to sick leave shall have the credit for that activity(ies) charged against his regular sick account. However, a pilot may elect to have that sick leave charged to his disability sick account provided he complies with the requirements of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_14D2">Section 14.D.2.</a></p>
5521:    <p id="link_14C6b" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 14.C.6.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span>   At the end of the last bid period of each calendar year, any hours remaining in a pilot’s regular sick account shall be transferred to his disability sick account, subject to the disability sick account ceiling (as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_14D1">Section 14.D.1.</a>). Any sick leave credits in excess of the disability sick account ceiling shall be transferred to the surplus program provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_14E">Section 14.E.</a></p>
5540:  <p>A pilot is eligible to make up CH drawn from his disability sick account as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_14D2a">Section 14.D.2.a.</a></p>
5544:  <p>As provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_14C6b">Section 14.C.6.b.</a>, the number of hours remaining in each pilot’s regular sick account shall be added to the existing balance in that pilot’s disability sick account subject to the account ceiling. If the addition of these hours would cause the balance of the pilot’s disability sick account to exceed the disability sick account ceiling, the value of the excess hours shall be deposited into the pilot’s Employer Contribution Unused Sick Leave Account within the Federal Express Corporation Profit Sharing Plan. The amount of the deposit shall be determined by multiplying the excess CH by the pilot’s pay rate at the end of the calendar year, or if he is no longer in active employment, by his last pay rate. The deposit shall be made during the first bid period of the following calendar year as provided in Section 28. Pilots who would otherwise have been eligible for a contribution into the pilot’s Employer Contribution Unused Sick Leave Account within the Federal Express Corporation Profit Sharing Plan but for the termination of his employment, including retirement, death or resignation, prior to the close of the calendar year shall have the value of any surplus contributed to the pilot’s Employer Contribution Unused Sick Leave Account.</p>
5548:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 14.F.1." rel="tooltip">1.</span> A pilot who sustains a workers’ compensable injury or illness covered by <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#section16">Section 16</a> shall be eligible for up to 168 CH of occupational injury/illness leave for each occupational injury or illness. Occupational injury/illness leave may be used for a recurrence of an occupational injury or illness up to the balance of the 168 CH not used for the original occurrence of the injury or illness. Occupational injury/illness leave is a non-accruable benefit. Sick leave shall not be used for occupational injuries or illnesses until occupational injury/illness is exhausted.</p>
5570:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 15.A.3." rel="tooltip">3.</span> While a VIPS notification(s) of a pilot’s pending FAA medical certificate expiration is provided to each pilot, it is the pilot’s responsibility to know and meet the medical standards by possessing a valid FAA medical certificate. Failure of a pilot to receive a VIPS notice shall not excuse the pilot’s failure to maintain his/her valid FAA medical certificate. If a pilot fails to provide the Company with confirmation via VIPS that he has a valid medical certificate as required by this paragraph, before 0900 LBT on the day prior to the showtime of a trip or R-day scheduled to start within the time period as stated in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_15A2">Section 15.A.2.</a>, the trip or R-day shall be removed without pay, and the pilot shall not be eligible for make-up. Trip(s) or R-day(s) shall no longer be removed after the pilot provides the Company with the required validation.</p>
5575:  <p id="link_15B2" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 15.B.2." rel="tooltip">2.</span> If an active pilot (or an inactive pilot receiving LTD benefits) incurs medical expenses in order to qualify for an FAA medical certificate, which are not covered by <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_15B1">Section 15.B.1.</a>, the following shall apply:</p>
5586:    <p id="link_15B2b" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 15.B.2.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span>   A pilot who incurs medical expenses covered by <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_15B2">Section 15.B.2.</a> shall submit or cause to have submitted a medical insurance claim for any such expenses that are covered by insurance. The pilot shall provide a copy of any response(s) to the medical insurance claim to his Fleet Captain within a reasonable time after receiving same. The pilot shall remit to the Company the amount of any insurance claim that was both paid by the Company and reimbursed by the insurance plan. The primary purpose of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_15B2b">Section 15.B.2.b.</a> is to allow any group health insurance discount to be recognized for medical charges that arise out of this section and to avoid any double payment being made for the same service. If a pilot gets reimbursed from both the Company and the service is also covered and paid through the group health plan, the pilot may receive a reimbursement from the health care provider for an overpayment that actually belongs to the Company. In this case, a pilot should remit or cause to have remitted the extra monies paid back to the Company.</p>
5595:    <p id="link_15C1b" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 15.C.1.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span>   If a law or regulation mandates that a testing program be changed, but affords multiple options by which compliance can be achieved, then the Company and the Association shall meet to discuss the available alternatives. The initial meeting shall commence no later than 60 days following the date the final rule regarding the alternative methods is published in the Federal Register. Should the parties be unable to mutually agree on an alternative testing method within 60 days, then each side may elect to advocate an alternative before a mutually selected arbitrator from the non-disciplinary panel. The parties’ presentations shall be in writing unless either party elects an in-person hearing. The arbitrator shall select the method of testing from the two alternatives presented. If the Company is required to implement a change prior to the conclusion of the process described in this paragraph, nothing in this paragraph shall prevent it from doing so (subject to change depending on the outcome of the <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_15C1b">Section 15.C.1.b.</a> process).</p>
5599:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 15.C.3." rel="tooltip">3.</span> If the Company has a reasonable basis to believe that a pilot’s ability to perform his duties is impaired for reasons relating to substances not covered by the legally mandated drug testing programs referred to above, the pilot’s case shall be handled as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_15D">Section 15.D.</a></p>
5606:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 15.D.4." rel="tooltip">4.</span> The Company shall pay for all examinations, tests or evaluations performed or directed by its aeromedical advisor. If the pilot needs to travel from the pilot’s permanent, primary address in connection with a Company directed examination(s), test(s) and/or evaluation(s) pursuant to this paragraph, the Company shall provide and arrange transportation, lodging and per diem as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#section5">Section 5</a>.</p>
5613:      <p id="link_15D5ci" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 15.D.5.c.i." rel="tooltip">i.</span> if the pilot supplies the Company’s aeromedical advisor with medical documentation substantiating his disagreement, he shall be placed or remain on sick leave, disability or medical leave of absence, as applicable. He shall remain in that status until his case is resolved as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_15D7">Section 15.D.7.</a></p>
5614:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 15.D.5.c.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    if the pilot does not supply medical documentation supporting his disagreement within 30 days from receipt of the Company’s aeromedical advisor’s determination, he shall be placed on personal leave of absence. If warranted by extenuating circumstances, the System Chief Pilot shall extend the 30 day period. If the pilot subsequently supplies the required documentation, his status shall be determined pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_15D5ci">Section 15.D.5.c.i.</a></p>
5616:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 15.D.5.d." rel="tooltip">d.</span>   If the Company’s aeromedical advisor finds the pilot not fit for duty and the pilot disagrees, the pilot shall be placed or remain on sick leave, disability or medical leave of absence, as applicable, until the Company’s aeromedical advisor determines the pilot to be fit for duty, or his case is resolved as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_15D7">Section 15.D.7.</a></p>
5618:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 15.D.6." rel="tooltip">6.</span> The Company shall give written notice to ALPA that the Company’s aeromedical advisor has issued a direction to a pilot under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_15D3">Section 15.D.3.</a> or that the Company’s aeromedical advisor has issued a determination to a pilot under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_15D5">Section 15.D.5.</a> Such notice shall occur as close in time to the Company’s aeromedical advisor’s notice to the pilot as is reasonably practical under the circumstances.</p>
5649:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 15.G.1." rel="tooltip">1.</span> Flight Management shall not require a pilot to submit to a psychological or psychiatric examination. However, flight management may refer a pilot to the Company’s aeromedical advisor in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_15D1">Section 15.D.1.</a> (reasonable basis to question fitness). A pilot may be required to undergo a psychological/psychiatric examination if directed by the Company’s aeromedical advisors based on their independent evaluation, in accordance with Section 15. The evaluation conducted by the Company’s aeromedical advisors is expected to include contact with the pilot and any other preliminary evaluation that is necessary in order to reach an independent, informed decision as to the need for further testing.</p>
5650:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 15.G.2." rel="tooltip">2.</span> Nothing contained in this Section shall be construed to permit the Company to require a pilot to submit to any medical treatment or invasive procedure which is not consistent with reasonable and current medical practice or which poses an unreasonable threat to the pilot’s health. This paragraph shall not be construed to prohibit testing for drugs, alcohol and, if applicable, other substances pursuant to the provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_15C">Section 15.C.</a></p>
5652:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 15.G.2.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   If the Company’s aeromedical advisor determines that a treatment, procedure or evaluation is appropriate in the circumstances of a case, he shall consult with the pilot’s physician or a physician associated with the Association’s aeromedical office, as applicable, for the purpose of determining the permissibility of that treatment, procedure or evaluation under the provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_15G">Section 15.G.</a> (this paragraph). The issue shall be resolved by mutual agreement of those 2 physicians.</p>
5670:<p><strong>B.</strong> Notwithstanding the provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_16A">Section 16.A.</a>, if a pilot suffers an otherwise compensable injury and is ineligible for workers’ compensation benefits due solely to the geographic location at which the injury occurred, the Company shall provide him with benefits no less favorable than the benefits for which he would have been eligible in the state in which he is domiciled.</p>
5673:<p><strong>E.   </strong>If a pilot has sustained a workers’ compensable injury or illness covered by this Section, his occupational illness/injury payments shall be an offset against his workers’ compensation benefits. If, having exhausted his occupational injury/illness leave, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_14F">Section 14.F.</a>, a pilot receives workers’ compensation payments and sick leave pay at the same time, he may use only enough sick leave so that the workers’ compensation payments plus the sick leave pay equals 100 percent of his BLG/RLG.</p>
5692:<p><strong>C.</strong> The benefits described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_17A">Section 17.A.</a> shall not apply to:</p>
5695:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 17.C.2." rel="tooltip">2.</span> Conduct not relating to operation of Company aircraft that would constitute just cause for termination or which could have led to the pilot’s imprisonment for more than 30 days under Federal law or the laws of the State of Tennessee, if established. The benefits described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_17A">Section 17.A.</a>, shall not be withheld pursuant to this paragraph until the Company has presented the pilot with notice of its intent to apply this paragraph, and has allowed the pilot to respond.</p>
5698:<p><strong>E.</strong> Should the pilot’s spouse and/or eligible dependents wish to continue health coverage beyond the end of the appropriate benefit continuation period provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_17A">Section 17.A.</a>, they may do so under the provisions of COBRA. Pilots and their spouses and/or eligible dependents needing more information regarding COBRA (including time limits) should refer to Section 27 of this Agreement.</p>
5707:  <p id="link_18A1" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 18.A.1." rel="tooltip">1.</span> During their terms of office, and with 30 days written notice prior to the beginning of the first affected bid period, the following shall be removed from flying as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_18B1b">Section 18.B.1.b.</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_18B1c">c.</a><!--:</p-->
5714:    <p id="link_18A1f" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 18.A.1.f." rel="tooltip">f.</span>   other pilots designated by the MEC Chairman; provided, however, the total number of pilots removed under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_18A1">Section 18.A.1.</a> shall not exceed 10, except with the Company’s agreement.</p>
5718:    <p id="link_18A2a" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 18.A.2.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   Pilots, not designated by the MEC Chairman as described above in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_18A1f">Section 18.A.1.f.</a>, and comprising the MEC negotiating committee (up to five pilots), members of the System Board of Adjustment, FOQA Gatekeepers, and Training Review Board (TRB) members, shall be removed from flying at the Association’s notification, provided that the Association complies with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_18A4a">Section 18.A.4.a.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_18A4c">c.</a> Removals sent later than the 3 business day window shall not be unreasonably denied.</p>
5719:    <p id="link_18A2b" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 18.A.2.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span>   MEC members, or designees (one substitute for each absent MEC member) attending quarterly meetings, the ALPA Executive Vice-President, and members of the Pilot Benefit Review Board shall be removed from flying at the Association’s notification if the notification is made prior to the close of the Conflict Input Window as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25E2">Section 25.E.2.</a> for the affected bid period, and the Association complies with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_18A4a">Section 18.A.4.a.</a> If a removal is sent subsequent to the applicable Conflict Input Window, the trip removal will be processed under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_18A3">Section 18.A.3.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_18A4">4</a>. (excluding <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_18A4b">A.4.b.</a>), except that removals for pilots holding a secondary line shall be treated as having been sent prior to the close of the Conflict Input Window.</p>
5729:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 18.A.4.f." rel="tooltip">f.</span>   A pilot removed from flying for Association business shall remain on Association business for the entire period for which he was removed, except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_18A6">Section 18.A.6.</a> (sick leave).</p>
5738:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 18.A.5.e." rel="tooltip">e.</span>   The Association will be billed, pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_18C">Section 18.C.</a>, for the difference of the BLG/RLG minus the vacation value.</p>
5746:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 18.A.6.a.iii." rel="tooltip">iii.</span>   Once a trip removal code has been changed from Association business status to sick leave, no further removal changes will be made, except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_18A6c">Section 18.A.6.c.</a></p>
5755:  <p id="link_18B1" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 18.B.1." rel="tooltip">1.</span> Compensation for Full Bid Period Removals and Pilots Listed in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_18A1">Section 18.A.1.</a></p>
5758:    <p id="link_18B1b" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 18.B.1.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span>   Notwithstanding <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_18B1a">Section 18.B.1.a.</a>, the pilots listed in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_18A1">Section 18.A.1.</a> shall not bid lines in their respective aircraft and seat position. They shall be compensated based on the number of CH established by the MEC. The MEC shall advise the Company each year by the end of the November bid period as to the monthly credit hours for each pilot for the following year. In no event shall this CH number for the new year be greater than the system-wide average of the highest lines with carryover for the current calendar year (the cap for the upcoming calendar year shall be derived from the system-wide average of the highest lines with carryover, in the bid periods of January through December of the current year).</p>
5762:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 18.B.1.b.iii." rel="tooltip">iii.</span>   With 30 days written notice to the Company, the Association may elect to process trip removals for an MEC officer(s) as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_18A2a">Section 18.A.2.a.</a>, rather than as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_18B1b">Section 18.B.1.b.</a>, or vice versa.</p>
5764:    <p id="link_18B1c" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 18.B.1.c." rel="tooltip">c.</span>   Notwithstanding <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_18B1a">Section 18.B.1.a.</a>, during their terms of office, pilots elected to function as a national officer of the Association or IFALPA, or appointed to national Association or IFALPA offices, shall not bid lines in their respective aircraft and seat position. They shall be compensated at the pay rate and the number of CH established in accordance with ALPA/IFALPA Constitution and By-laws and policies.</p>
5776:    <p id="link_18B4b" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 18.B.4.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span></p>   The following applies to a pilot who receives a notional System Bid award or assignment, pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_18B4a">Section 18.B.4.a.</a>, and who would require training for that crew position. That pilot will have his system-wide seniority compared against those who were actually awarded/assigned the applicable crew position (and who also require training), in order to establish their “Nth” position.<p></p>
5781:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 18.B.4.b.iii." rel="tooltip">iii.</span>   Pilots who are assigned the crew position shall be listed in inverse seniority order after the pilots in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_18B4bii">Section 18.B.4.b.ii.</a></p>
5783:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 18.B.4.c." rel="tooltip">c.</span>   Pilots subject to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_18B4b">Section 18.B.4.b.</a> will begin to earn the applicable hourly rate either:</p>
5791:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 18.B.4.e." rel="tooltip">e.</span>   A pilot who does not receive a notional award pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_18B4a">Section 18.B.4.a.</a>, or whose period of unavailability did not include any System Bid closings, will return to his current crew position when the Company receives notification of his availability. If such pilot requires requalification training, he will be assigned to a training date as soon as practicable.</p>
5828:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 18.C.3." rel="tooltip">3.</span> The Company shall bill the Association on a monthly basis for 95% of the compensation paid to pilots on Association business for trips or R-days missed, excluding trips dropped as a result of vacation pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_18A5">Section 18.A.5.</a>, or sick leave pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_18A6">Section 18.A.6.</a> In addition, the Company shall bill the Association an override of 20% of the amount invoiced pursuant to this paragraph for ordinary compensation related costs incurred by the Company for items such as payroll taxes and the costs of benefits.</p>
5835:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 18.C.6.c." rel="tooltip">c.</span>   ASAP Event Review Committee, including training for members of the ERC (subject to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_18C4">Section 18.C.4.</a>);</p>
5849:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 18.C.6.q." rel="tooltip">q.</span>   Pilot Scheduling Improvement Team (subject to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25BBH2b">Section 25.BB.H.2.b.</a>);</p>
5855:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 18.C.6.w." rel="tooltip">w.</span>   Scheduling Improvement Group (subject to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25BBh2a">Section 25.BB.H.2.a.</a>);</p>
