5869:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 18.D.1." rel="tooltip">1.</span> Any pilot removed from flying for Association business shall maintain currency unless unable to do so for reasons not related to Association business leave provided, however, that MEC officers, members of the MEC Negotiating Committee, along with pilots elected to a national office of the Association or IFALPA office, pilots appointed to national Association or IFALPA positions, and other pilots designated by the MEC Chairman under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_18A1f">Section 18.A.1.f.</a> may elect not to maintain currency.</p>
5870:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 18.D.2." rel="tooltip">2.</span> A pilot removed for an entire bid period for Association business shall be permitted, during that same bid period, to bump a pilot(s) in his seat and equipment type to maintain currency, in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25L11">Section 25.L.11.</a></p>
5876:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 18.E.3." rel="tooltip">3.</span> <span lang="ja-JP">The number of hours of compensation to which the Company is entitled to reimbursement pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_18C">Section 18.C.</a>, due to a pilot’s removal from flying for Association business shall be reduced on an hour-for-hour basis by that pilot’s AFB credit. In the event a pilot’s AFB credit exceeds the hours of his compensation to which the Company is entitled to reimbursement pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_18C">Section 18.C.</a>, the pilot shall be compensated for the excess AFB credit hours (by submission of a pay log). If a pilot is removed from an AFB trip prior to block-out due to sick leave, he shall not earn any CH for that trip and no deduction shall be made from his sick leave account.</span></p>
5877:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 18.E.4." rel="tooltip">4.</span> <span lang="ja-JP">Invoices submitted to the Association pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_18C">Section 18.C.</a>, shall state for each AFB trip the pilot’s name, employee number, domicile, trip, pairing number and the amount of compensation offset by the AFB trip.</span></p>
5925:      <p><em>Intent: The following example applies to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_19E1">Section 19.E.1.</a></em></p>
5935:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 19.E.1.c.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    Information provided along with the Notice of Hearing, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_19E1aii">Section 19.E.1.a.ii.</a>, need not be reproduced under this paragraph.</p>
5937:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 19.E.1.d." rel="tooltip">d.</span>   The pilot shall be afforded the opportunity to respond to information described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_19E1c">Section 19.E.1.c.</a> before a decision is rendered. If necessary, the hearing shall be delayed or continued in order to provide the pilot with adequate time to prepare and/or respond. The Company may continue to investigate the circumstances of a particular case and to gather additional documentation after the close of the hearing.</p>
5949:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 19.E.3." rel="tooltip">3.</span> The Association has the right to have a representative present at any disciplinary hearing. The Association shall be given notice prior to any disciplinary hearing in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_19F5">Section 19.F.5.</a></p>
5967:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 19.F.9.c." rel="tooltip">c.</span>   If the pilot signs the letter and there is no correspondence from the Association within the same 7 day period indicating the Association’s disagreement, no further action is necessary, and the discipline will be fully precedential in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_19C">Section 19.C.</a> absent a specific agreement to the contrary.</p>
5968:    <p id="link_19F9d" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 19.F.9.d." rel="tooltip">d.</span>   If the pilot declines to sign the hearing waiver, then the Company may elect to conduct a <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_19E">Section 19.E.</a> hearing on the matter.</p>
5972:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 19.F.9.e.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    The Company may conduct a preliminary hearing under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_19E">Section 19.E</a>, in which case, any discipline, and the precedential effect thereof, would be determined in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_19C">Section 19.C.</a></p>
5974:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 19.F.9.f." rel="tooltip">f.</span>   In any case, if the Company offers discipline in the context of a hearing waiver, but ultimately holds a preliminary hearing on the matter (whether under the process described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_19F9d">Section 19.F.9.d.</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_19F9e">e.</a>), the offer of discipline and the hearing waiver, and any discussions pertaining to that offer, shall be considered settlement discussions and shall carry the same evidentiary protections that normally accompany such discussions.</p>
5976:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 19.F.10." rel="tooltip">10.</span>   When mutually agreeable, the Company may conduct disciplinary hearings pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_19E">Section 19.E.</a> by telephonic and/or video conference.</p>
5997:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 20.A.2." rel="tooltip">2.</span> Notwithstanding the time limitation in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_20B1">Section 20.B.1.</a> above, grievances arising out of clerical or bookkeeping errors may be filed outside the 60 day period provided that they:</p>
6028:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 20.F.1.c.i." rel="tooltip">i.</span> the Company’s obligations under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_20D1">Section 20.D.1.</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_20D4">D.4.</a> shall not be diminished by this provision; and</p>
6044:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 21.A.1." rel="tooltip">1.</span> The disciplinary System Board shall have jurisdiction over disputes between a pilot(s) or the Association and the Company growing out of grievances, or out of the interpretation or application of any of the terms of the Agreement, which are processed under Section 19 of this Agreement and which are submitted to the System Board as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_21B">Section 21.B.</a> A neutral arbitrator from the disciplinary panel shall hear such disputes as the sole member of the Board unless either party elects to proceed before a 3-person board. Any such election must be made at least 45 days prior to the System Board proceeding.</p>
6045:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 21.A.2." rel="tooltip">2.</span> The non-disciplinary System Board shall have jurisdiction over disputes between a pilot(s) or the Association and the Company growing out of grievances, or out of the interpretation or application of any of the terms of the Agreement, which have been processed under Section 20, and which have been submitted to the System Board as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_21B">Section 21.B.</a> Such disputes shall be heard by a 3-person System Board unless either party elects to proceed before a 5-person System Board. Any such election must be made at least 45 days prior to the System Board proceeding.</p>
6076:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 21.C.2.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span>   Disputes between pilots or the Association and the Company, which are processed under Section 19 of this Agreement and which are submitted to the System Board as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_21B">Section 21.B.</a>, may be consolidated by mutual agreement of the Company and the Association.</p>
6100:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 21.E.2.c.i." rel="tooltip">i.</span> If an arbitrator(s) appeared on both exchanged lists described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_21E2a">Section 21.E.2.a.</a>, such arbitrator(s) shall be accepted as a member of the respective panel. If the panel is not complete, then;</p>
6112:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 21.E.3.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   Should vacancies occur on either panel of neutral members, other than by operation of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_21E5">Section 21.E.5.</a>, the parties shall attempt to agree on a replacement within 30 days after the vacancy occurs. If the parties are unable to agree on a replacement, the vacancy shall remain unfilled.</p>
6130:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 21.E.5.a.ii.(c)." rel="tooltip">(c)</span>  If no arbitrator appeared on both lists, the parties shall determine whether either party is willing to accept an arbitrator from the other party’s list. If a mutually acceptable arbitrator is found, such arbitrator shall be impaneled. If not, then the parties shall use the process described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_21E2ciii">Section 21.E.2.c.iii.</a>(a) through (c) to fill the vacancy.</p>
6137:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 21.E.5.b.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    If the removed arbitrator originally appeared on both parties’ list, then his replacement shall be accomplished as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_21E5ai">Section 21.E.5.a.i.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_21E5aii">ii.</a></p>
6138:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 21.E.5.b.iii." rel="tooltip">iii.</span>   If the removed arbitrator originally appeared only on one party’s list, then, within 30 days following the removal, that party shall submit a list of 7 arbitrators. Within 15 days following receipt of the list, the parties shall determine whether there is a mutually acceptable arbitrator. If not, then the parties shall use the process described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_21E2ciii">Section 21.E.2.c.iii.</a>(a) through (c) to fill the vacancy.</p>
6187:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 22.A.1.h." rel="tooltip">h.</span>   Rejecting an offer of retirement under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_23A2c">Section 23.A.2.c.</a></p>
6209:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 22.E.2." rel="tooltip">2.</span> Notwithstanding the provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_22E1">Section 22.E.1.</a>, a probationary pilot is subject to the provisions of Section 23.</p>
6218:  <p id="link_23A1" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 23.A.1." rel="tooltip">1.</span> Except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_23A1b">23.A.1.b.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_23A2">A.2.</a>, if the Company determines it is necessary to reduce the number of active pilots, the Company shall furlough pilots in reverse order of system seniority as listed on the Master Seniority List. All pilots holding a seniority number at the time of furlough shall be subject to the provisions of Section 23 regardless of their employment status at that time (e.g., active flying service, leave of absence, disability, probationary pilots). Reductions in the number of pilots shall be accomplished as follows:</p>
6224:  <p id="link_23A2" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 23.A.2." rel="tooltip">2.</span> Notwithstanding the provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_23A1">Section 23.A.1.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_23B1">B.1.</a>, the following apply to a pilot subject to a regulated age restriction:</p>
6228:    <p id="link_23A2c" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 23.A.2.c." rel="tooltip">c.</span>   A restricted pilot who cannot move to or be accommodated as a Second Officer from another crew position because his relative seniority is less than the current population of Second Officers or there are no Second Officer crew seats, shall be offered the opportunity to retire as provided in the Agreement. Following a pilot’s rejection of the offer, the pilot shall be released from employment as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_22B1">Section 22.B.1.</a>, and shall not be considered as having been furloughed in cases where the only crew status the pilot can occupy is Second Officer.</p>
6232:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 23.A.5." rel="tooltip">5.</span> A furloughed pilot shall retain his regular and disability sick accounts in accordance with the provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_14A3">Section 14.A.3.</a></p>
6234:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 23.A.7." rel="tooltip">7.</span> The continuation of a pilot’s benefits beyond his furlough date shall be governed by applicable state or federal laws except that a pilot shall continue to be eligible for Company related insurance programs for the period, if any, during which he is entitled to receive furlough pay as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_23E">Section 23.E.</a></p>
6237:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 23.A.10." rel="tooltip">10.</span>    Recall shall be offered to all pilots on furlough prior to the employment of a new hire pilot, except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_23A2b"></a><a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_23A2b">Section 23.A.2.b.</a></p>
6242:  <p id="link_23B1" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 23.B.1." rel="tooltip">1.</span> Except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_23A2">Section 23.A.2.</a>, pilots, including pilots who have not completed their probationary period, shall be recalled from furlough in order of system seniority.</p>
6251:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 23.B.4.e." rel="tooltip">e.</span>   For purposes of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_22B1d">Section 22.B.1.d.</a>, the pilot shall be considered as having returned to a flying position.</p>
6255:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 23.B.7." rel="tooltip">7.</span> A pilot’s election to decline recall and remain on furlough in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_23B4">Section 23.B.4.</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_23B5">5.</a> shall not extend the period of 7 years referred to in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_22B1g">Section 22.B.1.g.</a></p>
6264:  <p>A pilot to whom a furlough notice has been issued may compete for available non-flying employment with the Company for which he is qualified for a period of 90 days following the effective date of his furlough or until expiration of the period, if any, during which the pilot is entitled to receive furlough pay, whichever is later. If a pilot is offered and accepts non-flying employment, his pay, working conditions and benefits, including any relocation benefits, shall be determined by Company policies pertinent to that position. A furloughed pilot may not work in a non-flying position with the Company at the same time that he is receiving furlough pay as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_23E1">Section 23.E.1.</a> If mutually acceptable to the pilot and the Company, however, such pilot may waive all or a portion of his furlough pay in order to begin his non-flying employment sooner.</p>
6318:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 23.E.3." rel="tooltip">3.</span> If a pilot receiving furlough pay is recalled, his furlough pay shall terminate on the date he resumes active employment. However, if the pilot has elected reduced payments in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_23E2">Section 23.E.2.</a>, he shall receive 60 hours of furlough pay per bid period, on a pro-rated basis, if applicable, for the period he was on furlough, not to exceed the maximum furlough pay to which the pilot was entitled pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_23E1">Section 23.E.1.</a></p>
6336:            <p id="link_24A3a" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.A.3.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   Prior to commencing training for a Captain or First Officer crew position, a pilot must possess a current FAA medical certificate for that crew position, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_15A">Section 15.A.</a>, and an Airline Transport Pilot Certificate.</p>
6337:            <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.A.3.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span>   If a pilot does not possess the requisite certifications as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24A3a">Section 24.A.3.a.</a>, he may be removed from that award/assignment and, if removed, shall remain in his current crew position.</p>
6379:            <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.B.2.e." rel="tooltip">e.</span>   Required certificates for each crew position as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24A3">Section 24.A.3.</a></p>
6384:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.B.5." rel="tooltip">5.</span> The published results of a System Bid (as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24C1">Section 24.C.1.</a>) shall be available in the Company’s appropriate electronic system (currently the PFC website) for a minimum of 7 years.</p>
6387:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.B.8." rel="tooltip">8.</span> For the purposes of a System Bid, a pilot shall bid from his currently awarded/assigned crew position. However, a pilot who is assigned from a crew position into which he never activated and to a crew position in the same geographic location as the base associated with his current crew position will not be eligible for the relocation benefits described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6A2">Section 6.A.2.</a> (Assignment).</p>
6400:      <p id="link_24C2" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.C.2." rel="tooltip">2.</span> Except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24C2e">Section 24.C.2.e.</a>, the System Bid shall be processed in system-wide seniority order, as follows:</p>
6411:          <p id="link_24C2ci" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.C.2.c.i." rel="tooltip">i.</span> A pilot will be awarded as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24C2cib">Section 24.C.2.c.i.(b)</a>, or awarded/assigned as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24C2cia">Section 24.C.2.c.i.(a)</a>, such crew position, provided that he is:</p>
6418:              <p>A crew position awarded pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24C2cib">Section 24.C.2.c.i.(b)</a> shall be considered a Stand In Bid Award</p>
6421:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.C.2.c.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    A pilot who is subject to assignment, and who is not assigned in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24C2a">Sections 24.C.2.a.</a>, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24C2b">b.</a>, or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24C2ci">c.i.</a>, will be assigned to a different crew position as follows:</p>
6423:            <p id="link_24C2ciia" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.C.2.c.ii.(a)." rel="tooltip">(a)</span>  If the pilot has not listed a crew position on his standing bid that he can hold as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24C2cia">Section 24.C.2.c.i.(a)</a>, then he will be assigned to the U.S. based crew position with the highest pay rate that his seniority will allow him to hold, and in which he would have the highest relative seniority, from among those crew positions whose Dynamic Staffing Level is less than the Maximum Staffing Level.</p>
6424:            <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.C.2.c.ii.(b)." rel="tooltip">(b)</span>  If the pilot cannot hold any crew position as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24C2ciia">Section 24.C.2.c.ii.(a)</a>, he will be assigned to the most junior held, U.S.-based crew position regardless of the Maximum Staffing Level.</p>
6437:              <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.C.2.e.ii.(b).(2)." rel="tooltip">(2)</span>    If the pilot is not awarded the crew position via the exercise of an ARR, his remaining standing bid shall be considered as otherwise provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24C2">Section 24.C.2.</a></p>
6444:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.C.3.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   No pilot may be assigned to an FDA crew position unless the pilot includes the FDA crew position in his standing bid in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24C2cia">Section 24.C.2.c.i.(a).</a> If no pilot on the Master Seniority List expresses a preference by standing bid for an FDA crew position, the Company may hire a pilot into it in accordance with &lt;<a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24C2d">Section 24.C.2.d.</a></p>
6447:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.C.3.d." rel="tooltip">d.</span>   A pilot assigned from an FDA may elect to hold required training, or a base transfer activation (BTA), in abeyance until the fulfillment of his minimum FDA commitment period, if any, provided the FDA is not being closed prior to the end of such commitment period. This election shall be by written notification to the Crew Staffing department within 10 days following the publication of the applicable System Bid results, as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24C1">Section 24.C.1.</a> If the pilot elects to hold the training or BTA in abeyance, he will not be in the applicable pool for BTA or ITU bidding. The Company shall notify the pilot of an assigned training start or BTA date. Such date shall be at least 60 days after the date on which the Company’s notification was posted, and no later than 60 days beyond the fulfillment of the pilot’s minimum FDA commitment period. Exercise of this provision will not create any SDP entitlement for any pilot. Following notification, the date may not be changed without the consent of the pilot.</p>
6450:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.C.5." rel="tooltip">5.</span> A pilot released from his currently awarded or assigned crew position in accordance with other provisions of this Agreement shall remain in his current crew position. If the pilot’s current crew position is unavailable for reasons identified in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11J4">Section 11.J.4.</a>, his crew position shall be determined as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11J5">Section 11.J.5.</a></p>
6458:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.D.2.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span>   If the pilot could not have held the superseding crew position on the System Bid from which his prior award/assignment resulted, then the award/assignment of his training slot for the superseding crew position shall be handled in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24D4">Section 24.D.4.</a></p>
6460:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.D.3." rel="tooltip">3.</span> Notwithstanding <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24D2">Section 24.D.2.</a>, a pilot who has already begun to train for his prior award/assignment must activate prior to being awarded/assigned to a training or BTA date for his superseding award.</p>
6474:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.D.4.b.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    Except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24D4biii">Section 24.D.4.b.iii.</a> through viii., pilots will be awarded to training slots in seniority order. Pilots requiring Initial, Transition, or Upgrade training may only bid for an ITU training slot (an ITU training slot is considered one training type). Pilots requiring only a 24-Requal may only bid for a 24-Requal training slot. Pilots requiring only a 24-Downbid may only bid for a 24-Downbid slot. Pilots requiring only 24-Differences training may only bid for a 24-Differences slot.</p>
6485:            <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.D.4.b.iv.(b)." rel="tooltip">(b)</span>  A pilot who is denied a training slot award shall be entitled to Slot Denial Payment(s) (SDP) in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24E">Section 24.E.</a></p>
6486:            <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.D.4.b.iv.(c)." rel="tooltip">(c)</span>  The denied training slot shall be awarded to the next eligible, junior pilot(s) who bid for that slot, except when he is also denied by operation of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24D4biva">Section 24.D.4.b.iv.(a).</a> If there are no remaining junior pilot(s), that training slot shall be considered unfilled.</p>
6494:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.D.4.b.vii." rel="tooltip">vii.</span>   If a pilot is inversely assigned to a training slot as the result of a more junior, eligible pilot being bypassed as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24D4bv">Section 24.D.4.b.v.</a>, he shall be eligible for inverse SDP, in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24E8">Section 24.E.8.</a></p>
6499:        <p>If the Company desires to begin training prior to the Training Bid as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24D4a">Section 24.D.4.a.</a>, the Company shall provide the ability for pilots to bid and be awarded training dates as follows:</p>
6508:          <p id="link_24D4cii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.D.4.c.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    The awarding (and any denial and/or assignment) of Pre-Bid Period Package training slots shall be the same as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24D4b">Section 24.D.4.b.</a></p>
6514:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.D.5.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   Separate and apart from the Training Bid, the Company shall also conduct a single BTA bid (i.e., not monthly). Such bid will include a list of all available BTA dates applicable to the most recent System Bid’s awards/assignments, with the awarded/assigned BTA dates handled in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25C6">Section 25.C.6.</a></p>
6519:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.D.5.c.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    For pilots who were assigned the crew position to which their base transfer applies, BTA dates will be assigned in inverse seniority order, beginning with the first available BTA date from among those BTA dates remaining unawarded after the application of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24D5ci">Section 24.D.5.c.i.</a></p>
6540:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.D.7.c." rel="tooltip">c.</span>   No later than the close of the applicable Training Bid, the Company shall post a notification to any pilot who is denied a training slot award due to regulated age. The denied pilot shall not appear on subsequent Training Bids under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24D4aiii">Section 24.D.4.a.iii.</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24D4cic">D.4.c.i.(c).</a></p>
6541:        <p id="link_24D7d" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.D.7.d." rel="tooltip">d.</span>   A pilot denied a training slot award in accordance with Section 24.D.7.a., and whose crew position award was not the result of a down/lateral bid, will be eligible for Regulated Age SDP as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24E3">Section 24.E.3.</a></p>
6545:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.D.7.e.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    Enter into the Training Bid procedures as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24D4a">Section 24.D.4.a.</a> and b.</p>
6548:        <p id="link_24D7g" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.D.7.g." rel="tooltip">g.</span>   A pilot who is eligible for Regulated Age SDP shall participate in subsequent System Bids if the Maximum Staffing Level in his currently awarded crew position is lower than its Current Staffing Level. In such case, the pilot may be awarded or assigned a new crew position by operation of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24C">Section 24.C.</a> That pilot may become eligible for Regulated Age SDP (for his newly awarded or assigned crew position) by operation of Section 24.D.7.</p>
6554:  <p id="link_24E1" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.E.1." rel="tooltip">1.</span> If a pilot is denied a training slot as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24D4biva">Section 24.D.4.b.iv.(a)</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24D4cii">D.4.c.ii.</a>, he will be entitled to a Slot Denial Payment (SDP). The SDP shall correspond to the bid period containing the denied training slot award, and each subsequent bid period, except as provided below.</p>
6556:  <p id="link_24E3" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.E.3." rel="tooltip">3.</span> A pilot who is denied a training slot award pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24D7d">Section 24.D.7.d.</a> (Regulated Age), shall be entitled to SDP in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24E1">Section 24.E.1.</a> The pilot shall continue to receive the applicable SDP through the month in which he starts training, resulting from a subsequent System Bid, in which he was not denied a training slot award due to his regulated age.</p>
6557:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.E.4." rel="tooltip">4.</span> In subsequent bid period(s), if a pilot (except for a pilot described by <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24E2">Section 24.E.2.</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24E3">3</a>.):</p>
6562:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.E.5." rel="tooltip">5.</span> The SDP shall be paid in the monthly payroll cycle as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_3E1">Section 3.E.1.</a></p>
6563:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.E.6." rel="tooltip">6.</span> Only one pilot will be eligible for continuous SDP, per training slot. However, there may also be a single SDP associated with that same training slot, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24E2">Section 24.E.2.</a></p>
6671:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.E.10." rel="tooltip">10.</span>    Repayment of SDP and Inverse SDP, from pilots who do not activate in the crew position for which the SDP or Inverse SDP was paid, shall be exclusively limited to withdrawals from training (other than withdrawals accomplished in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11J2a">Section 11.J.2.a.</a>).</p>
6692:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.F.2." rel="tooltip">2.</span> For the purposes of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24F1e">Section 24.F.1.e.</a>, previous down/lateral awards pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24F1a">Sections 24.F.1.a.</a>, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24FAb">b.</a>, or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24F1d">d.</a> shall not be considered.</p>
6700:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.F.6.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span>   If the Company hires fewer pilots than are needed to fill all crew positions up to the Minimum Staffing Level, the Company may designate the crew positions to be made available for bidding by only the affected new hire pilots in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24F6a">Section 24.F.6.a.</a></p>
6702:        <p id="link_24F6d" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.F.6.d." rel="tooltip">d.</span>   If, through the application of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24F6c">Section 24.F.6.c.</a>, a junior pilot is activated into a higher paying crew position for which a senior pilot(s) did not have the opportunity to bid, the eligible senior pilot(s) shall be eligible for New Hire Junior Activation Compensation.</p>
6703:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.F.6.e." rel="tooltip">e.</span>   If a new hire pilot changes his initial crew position pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24F6c">Section 24.F.6.c.</a>, the Company shall activate him at his new base consistent with the Company’s staffing requirements.</p>
6704:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.F.6.f." rel="tooltip">f.</span>   Except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6E1c">Section 6.E.1.c.</a>, a new hire pilot shall not become entitled to a relocation package pursuant to Section 6 as a result of the application of this paragraph.</p>
6706:      <p id="link_24F7" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.F.7." rel="tooltip">7.</span> New Hire Junior Activation Compensation due in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24F6d">Section 24.F.6.d.</a> shall (for the senior pilot):</p>
6718:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.F.7.c.vii." rel="tooltip">vii.</span>   the date the next most senior available pilot (compared with the junior pilot identified in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24F7cvi">Section 24.F.7.c.vi.)</a> is no longer activated in, or would no longer have been (if the standard in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24F7cvi">Section 24.F.7.c.vi.</a> is applied) activated in, the crew position that generated the New Hire Junior Activation Compensation, if the junior pilot was not awarded a crew position on that subsequent System Bid (e.g., the junior pilot was on leave when the System Bid closed);</p>
6723:      <p id="link_24F8" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.F.8." rel="tooltip">8.</span> Repayment to the Company of New Hire Junior Activation Compensation paid in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24F6d">Section 24.F.6.d.</a>, from pilots who do not activate in the crew position that generated the New Hire Junior Activation Compensation, shall be exclusively limited to situations in which the pilot:</p>
6725:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.F.8.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   withdrew from training, before or after such training began, for a subsequently awarded or assigned crew position with a rate of pay the same or higher than his New Hire Junior Activation Compensation, other than as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11J2a">Section 11.J.2.a.</a>; or</p>
6730:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.F.9." rel="tooltip">9.</span> If a pilot entitled to New Hire Junior Activation Compensation in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24F6d">Section 24.F.6.d.</a> requires additional training, his New Hire Junior Activation Compensation shall not accrue during the delay in training caused by his performance.</p>
6738:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.G.3." rel="tooltip">3.</span> He will then be activated on the first day of the bid period following that bid period in which his training would have begun (pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24G2">Section 24.G.2.</a>), had he required it.</p>
6743:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 24.H.2." rel="tooltip">2.</span> The Transition Period shall begin on the date the first System Bid conducted pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24B">Section 24.B.</a> is posted and shall end 60 days after the second System Bid conducted pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24B">Section 24.B</a>. has been trained to completion. In no event, however, shall the Transition Period be less than 18 months or greater than 30 months in duration.</p>
6759:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.A.6." rel="tooltip">6.</span> Trips published in a bid period package that subsequently become available as open time shall remain in the same base during the bid period. Flying not published in a bid period package, including newly constructed trips as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25G5">Section 25.G.5.</a> (certain open time assignments), may be assigned by the Company to any base.</p>
6776:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.A.7.e." rel="tooltip">e.</span>   other reserve information as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25A8">Section 25.A.8.</a>; and</p>
6795:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.B.1." rel="tooltip">1.</span> The Company shall publish (electronically or otherwise, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25B3">Section 25.B.3.</a>) a bid period package for each base and, as necessary, a bid period supplemental package. At least one of these packages shall contain, at a minimum, the following information, current as of the publication date:</p>
6812:        <p id="link_25B1p" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.B.1.p." rel="tooltip">p.</span>    Identification of lines in the top 50% of that bid period package’s lines, in terms of scheduled block hours, for the purpose of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25C10a">Section 25.C.10.a.</a></p>
6835:      <p id="link_25C6" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.C.6." rel="tooltip">6.</span> A pilot may only be awarded a line, for flying purposes, for the crew position (i.e., domicile, aircraft, seat) in which he is currently activated and qualified at the time of bid closing. However, a pilot changing domiciles in the same crew status (i.e., aircraft, seat) shall bid and be awarded a line in his new crew position prior to his activation into that new crew position. Such pilot’s activation date shall be the first day of a bid period, or if operating a carryover trip, at the conclusion of such trip. If a pilot is activated but not qualified in his crew position at the time of bid closing, he shall be assigned a custom line as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25I">Section 25.I.</a></p>
6854:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.C.12.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   A pilot scheduled for recurrent training in the following bid period shall bid for a recurrent training session during the Bid Period Processing Conflict Input Window as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25E2">Section 25.E.2.</a></p>
6855:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.C.12.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span>   Bids shall be awarded during the Conflict Processing Window as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25E3">Section 25.E.3.</a>, and a pilot shall be notified of the award prior to the opening of the View/Add Window as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25E4">Section 25.E.4.</a></p>
6856:        <p id="link_25C12c" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.C.12.c." rel="tooltip">c.</span>   Recurrent training bids shall be awarded by seniority, provided, however, that a pilot shall not be awarded a recurrent training session in conflict with any other known absence (e.g., vacation period, leave of absence) or carry-out activities from the previous bid period (e.g., carry-out trip or R-days). If a pilot bids a recurrent training session in conflict with a vacation buffer, that buffer will be deemed waived. Conflicts between recurrent training and vacation will be determined based upon the vacation period as awarded, or as adjusted in the Conflict Input Window as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25E2b">Section 25.E.2.b.</a></p>
6857:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.C.12.d." rel="tooltip">d.</span>   If a pilot cannot be awarded a recurrent training session based on his seniority as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25C12c">Section 25.C.12.c.</a>, the following shall apply:</p>
6860:          <p id="link_25C12dii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.C.12.d.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    The pilot shall be assigned recurrent training avoiding conflicts if possible. If recurrent training must be assigned in conflict with a trip(s) or R-day block (other than a carry-out trip or R-day(s), which will not be conflicted with under this paragraph), those conflicts shall be handled as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25C12f">Section 25.C.12.f.</a></p>
6864:            <p id="link_25C12diiib" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.C.12.d.iii.(b)." rel="tooltip">(b)</span>  if the pilot is in his grace month, then upon completion of the bid period processing, the Training Department will coordinate his recurrent training assignment and any conflicts will be handled as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H">Section 25.H.</a></p>
6869:        <p id="link_25C12f" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.C.12.f." rel="tooltip">f.</span>   Following the award during the Conflict Processing Window, a trip or block of R-days in conflict with the recurrent training session award shall be treated as a phase-in conflict as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25F">Section 25.F.</a> (e.g., the trip or R-day block shall be dropped and be eligible for make-up under the CIA assignment code), with the pilot having the ability to enter bids during the following View/Add Window. If a recurrent training session award conflicts with any portion of a block of R-days, the entire block shall be dropped as a phase-in conflict and the pilot shall not be responsible for any of the R-days in that block.</p>
6886:        <p id="link_25D2b" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.D.2.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span>    Secondary lines shall be constructed in seniority order during the Secondary Working Window (SWW), as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25E">Section 25.E.</a></p>
6888:        <p id="link_25D2d" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.D.2.d." rel="tooltip">d.</span>    Secondary lines may be constructed using trips, base simulator support events (as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25L15">Section 25.L.15.</a>), reserve blocks, or combinations of the three; however:</p>
6906:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.D.2.e.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    Shall otherwise conform to the line spread provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4E1d">Section 4.E.1.d.</a></p>
6909:        <p id="link_25D2g" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.D.2.g." rel="tooltip">g.</span>    Carryover CH will not be part of the BLG/RLG for a secondary line except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25E4biii">Section 25.E.4.b.iii.</a> If it is not possible to build a secondary line within the line spread without creating a conflict, then the line will be built below the spread. In such case, the difference between that secondary line’s BLG/RLG, and the applicable crew position’s regular line average BLG shall be eligible for Priority Non-Premium (PNP) make-up.</p>
6913:        <p id="link_25D2k" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.D.2.k." rel="tooltip">k.</span>    A secondary line awardee may make other elections, during the first 48 hours of the Secondary Working Window (SWW), as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25E6b">Section 25.E.6.b.</a></p>
6922:        <p id="link_25D3e" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.D.3.e." rel="tooltip">e.</span>   Among published reserve lines in each bid period package there shall be a minimum of 13% R-24 lines with a minimum of one R-24 line (described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25M2">Section 25.M.2.</a>). The Company and the SIG shall coordinate to establish a percentage of R-24 lines by bid period package, and this percentage shall be reevaluated on a quarterly basis.</p>
6930:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.E.1.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   Election of minimum days off protection as a result of phase-in, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25F7">Section 25.F.7.</a>;</p>
6933:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.E.1.d." rel="tooltip">d.</span>   Waiver of 1-in-10 (<a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C1c">Section 12.C.1.c.</a>) to avoid phase-in conflict.</p>
6938:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.E.2.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   Worksheet for minimum days off protection as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25F7">Section 25.F.7.</a>;</p>
6939:        <p id="link_25E2b" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.E.2.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span>   Submissions for vacation adjustments (including waiver of vacation buffer for a secondary or reserve line) as provided in Section 7.E.2. and 3., and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_7G3">Section 7.G.3.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_7G4">4.</a>;</p>
6943:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.E.2.f." rel="tooltip">f.</span>   Submission to drop carryover trips under 72 hours TAFB as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25F3a">Section 25.F.3.a.</a>; and</p>
6949:      <p>The View/Add Window is a period of not less than 48 hours beginning at the close of the Bid Period Conflict Processing Window. During the View/Add Window, a pilot shall have the ability to view open time (conflicted regular line trips and reserve blocks, as well as all remaining open trips, reserve blocks not included in regular/reserve line construction, and open base simulator support events as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25L15">Section 25.L.15.</a>).</p>
6954:          <p id="link_25E4ai" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.E.4.a.i." rel="tooltip">i.</span> Bids for make-up trips due to phase-in conflict, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25F">Section 25.F.</a>;</p>
6955:          <p id="link_25E4aii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.E.4.a.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>   Bids for vacation make-up as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_7G5">Section 7.G.5.</a>;</p>
6974:              <p>For the purposes of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25E6bib">Section 25.E.6.b.i.(b)</a>, additional vacation days (i.e., “extended” vacation days) are always added to the end of the vacation period as awarded. However, if adding an extended vacation day to the end of the pilot’s awarded vacation period could cause that extended vacation day to either fall beyond the end of the upcoming bid period or touch Thanksgiving Day, Christmas Eve, Christmas Day, New Year’s Eve, or New Year’s Day, that extended vacation day will be added to the beginning of the pilot’s awarded vacation period. If adding an extended vacation day to the beginning of the pilot’s awarded vacation period would cause that extended vacation day to either fall into the current bid period or touch Thanksgiving Day, Christmas Eve, Christmas Day, New Year’s Eve, or New Year’s Day, the pilot’s submission to add that extended vacation day will not be granted.</p>
6983:      <p id="link_25E5" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.E.5." rel="tooltip">5.</span>   The View/Add Processing Window is a period of not more than 24 hours (beginning when the View/Add Results are posted) during which time the Company shall process submissions, requests, and designations from secondary line awardees transmitted to the Company pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25E4b">Section 25.E.4.b.</a> During the View/Add Processing Window, the Company shall:</p>
6985:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.E.5.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span> Comply with each submission given staffing in each crew position, which shall be processed in seniority order within the submission type, from secondary line awardees with an awarded vacation period(s) in the upcoming bid period, and who wish to avail themselves of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25E4bia">Section 25.E.4.b.i.(a)</a>. In no case shall a submission be approved if it creates a conflict with recurrent training or a known absence (e.g., jury).</p>
6986:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.E.5.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span> Comply with each submission given staffing in each crew position, which shall be processed in seniority order within the submission type, from pilots without any awarded vacation periods in the upcoming bid period who wish to avail themselves of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25E4bib">Section 25.E.4.b.i.(b).</a> In no case shall a submission be approved if it creates a conflict with recurrent training or a known absence (e.g., jury).</p>
7004:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.E.5.b.v." rel="tooltip">v.</span> A pilot’s election to slide, shrink, or eliminate his vacation footprint, in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25E6bi">Section 25.E.6.b.i.</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25E6bii">ii.</a>, has the effect only of enhancing a pilot’s flexibility during the SWW window. That election does not change the credit hour draw against his vacation bank as determined by the View/Add window.</p>
7018:          <p class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.F.1.b.iv." rel="tooltip">iv.</span>    The provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25F1bi">Section 25.F.1.b.i.</a>, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25$1bii">ii.</a>, and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25F1biii">iii.</a> do not apply operationally or during the application of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25M3d">Section 25.M.3.d.</a></p>
7020:        <p id="link_25F1c" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.F.1.c." rel="tooltip">c.</span>   a pilot is awarded/assigned a recurrent training session in conflict with a trip or block of R-days, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25C12dii">Section 25.C.12.d.ii.</a>, or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25C12f">C.12.f.</a></p>
7022:      <p id="link_25F2" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.F.2." rel="tooltip">2.</span>   Conflicts relating to on-duty limitations shall be determined based upon scheduled duty limitations, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C4">Section 12.C.4.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D5">D.5.</a></p>
7033:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.F.5." rel="tooltip">5.</span> In the event of a phase-in conflict with a trip(s) on a regular line in the new bid period, the trip(s) in the new bid period shall be dropped without pay and the pilot shall be eligible to make-up the CH value of trip(s) dropped due to phase-in conflict prior to construction of secondary lines, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25E4">Section 25.E.4.</a>, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25L1">L.1.</a>, and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25L6">L.6.</a></p>
7036:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.F.6.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   If other than a vacation conflict, the block containing that R-day(s) in the new bid period shall be dropped and the pilot shall be eligible to make-up an R-day value(s), as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25E4">Section 25.E.4.</a>, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25L1">L.1.</a>, and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25L6">L.6.</a>;</p>
7039:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.F.6.b.i." rel="tooltip">i.</span> The pilot’s vacation bank shall be charged only for the CH value of those R-days in conflict (as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_7G3">Section 7.G.3.</a>); and</p>
7040:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.F.6.b.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    Those R-days not in conflict (as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_7G3">Section 7.G.3.</a>) shall remain on his schedule, and his vacation bank shall not be charged for their CH value.</p>
7046:        <p id="link_25F7b" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.F.7.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span>   If a pilot is unable to protect his minimum days off as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25F7a">Section 25.F.7.a.</a>, the pilot shall have the ability to drop a trip(s) even though the drop(s) would cause his line to contain more than the minimum number of days off. He may request which trip(s) or R-day(s) will be dropped. The pilot shall then be eligible for make-up to the extent necessary to restore the CH value of a trip(s) dropped in the View/Add Window, prior to construction of secondary lines.</p>
7047:        <p class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.F.7.c." rel="tooltip">c.</span>   Adjustments to a pilot’s line in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25F7a">Section 25.F.7.a.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25F7b">F.7.b.</a>, shall be made in accordance with Section 25.E.</p>
7051:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.F.8.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   Unless the conflict is waived, the first reserve period will be dropped and eligible for make-up as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25E4">Section 25.E.4.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25L1">Section 25.L.1.</a>, and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25L6">L.6.</a></p>
7054:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.F.8.b.i." rel="tooltip">i.</span> an RP-A pilot shall be available for notification pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25M3cia">Section 25.M.3.c.i.(a)</a>, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25M3cib">(b)</a>, or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25M3cic">(c)</a>, as appropriate.</p>
7061:      <p id="link_25G1" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.G.1." rel="tooltip">1.</span> Following resolution of phase-in conflicts, open time may be used in the following order: training assignments, phase-in make-up (including MUV, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_7G5a">Section 7.G.5.a.</a>), and then substitution/reassignment. Remaining open time shall be used for construction of secondary lines. After construction of secondary lines, open time may be used at any time prior to or during a bid period for PMU, substitution/reassignment, custom line construction, advance reserve assignment, advance volunteer assignment, make-up, training assignment and Association Fly Back (AFB). However, during the first 12 hours after the publication of open time, only pilots shall have access to open time trips starting in the new bid period. The Company may also use open time before the assignment window in order to assign a trip to an R-24 pilot.</p>
7079:        <p id="link_25G3a" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.G.3.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>    Except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25G3ai">Section 25.G.3.a.i.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25G3aii">ii.</a>, at 0900 LBT each day the Company shall begin to assign open time trips and base standbys with showtimes through the next 40.5 hours.</p>
7081:          <p id="link_25G3ai" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.G.3.a.i." rel="tooltip">i.</span> At 0700 LBT each day, any trip with 120 hours TAFB or more, with a showtime during the next two local base days that is assigned to a pilot who is on sick leave shall be available in open time for Bid Line Adjustments as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25L">Section 25.L.</a> At 1000 LBT, such trips shall become available for assignment by CRS.</p>
7082:          <p id="link_25G3aii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.G.3.a.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    At 0700 LBT each day, any trip with less than 120 hours TAFB, with a showtime during the next local base day that is assigned to a pilot who is on sick leave shall be available in open time for Bid Line Adjustments as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25L">Section 25.L.</a> At 1000 LBT, such trips shall become available for assignment by CRS, with the exception of trips with a showtime prior to 1800 LBT that same day, which shall become available for assignment by CRS at 0900 LBT.</p>
7084:        <p id="link_25G3b" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.G.3.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span>    Open time not assigned as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25G1">Section 25.G.1.</a> shall be assigned in the following order:</p>
7100:        <p id="link_25G3c" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.G.3.c." rel="tooltip">c.</span>    Notwithstanding <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25G3b">Section 25.G.3.b.</a>, the Company may assign open base airport standbys to reserve pilots prior to any other category.</p>
7102:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.G.4." rel="tooltip">4.</span> The Company may assign a VLT or DRF ahead of reserve, due to operational requirements, notwithstanding <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25G3">Section 25.G.3.</a> If necessary to prevent or mitigate a departure delay, the Company may make an open time assignment other than as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25G3">Section 25.G.3.</a> and will report the specific circumstances of such assignment(s) to the Association in the bid period report under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_9B">Section 9.B.</a></p>
7103:      <p id="link_25G5" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.G.5." rel="tooltip">5.</span> If an open time trip cannot be assigned through the application of Section 25.G.3.b.i. through v., that trip may be canceled and a new trip(s) may be constructed and assigned according to this paragraph (<a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25G">Section 25.G.</a>). This procedure may only be done inside the open time assignment window, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25G3">Section 25.G.3.</a></p>
7142:        <p>The pilot is removed from the trip due to his recurrent training, other than as a phase-in conflict (See <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25F1c">Section 25.F.1.c.</a>).</p>
7147:        <p>A pilot who is eligible for substitution may be offered a substitution assignment at any time. He shall be available to receive substitution offers during the availability periods described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H3b">Section 25.H.3.b.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H3c">c.</a></p>
7151:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.H.3.b.i." rel="tooltip">i.</span> If his substitution window, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H4">Section 25.H.4.</a>, is shorter than 72 hours, he shall have no substitution responsibility after his initial availability period.</p>
7157:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.H.3.b.iii." rel="tooltip">iii.</span>   A pilot entitled to elect OTP under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H3bii">Section 25.H.3.b.ii.</a> may do so until the first 0900 LBT after the end of his initial availability period. If the pilot has not elected OTP by that time, he will remain in substitution.</p>
7175:        <p>A pilot eligible for substitution may be held at the airport for up to 4 hours after the showtime of the trip for which he was reporting, however, he shall not be held beyond the scheduled duty limitations applicable to that trip. A pilot on airport hold in MEM shall be eligible for a room in the crew rest facility. A pilot on airport hold shall earn 6 CH toward his substitution guarantee, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4L4">Section 4.L.4.</a></p>
7183:        <p>If a pilot becomes eligible for substitution as a result of his recurrent training, any substitution eligibility created will adhere to the provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H3a">Section 25.H.3.a.</a>, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H3b">b.</a>, and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H3c">c.</a> (see also <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25C12diiib">Section 25.C.12.d.iii.(b))</a>. His substitution window shall be as follows:</p>
7184:        <p>Example: Recurrent training creates substitution eligibility for a 7 day trip, and the pilot is eligible for substitution for 4 days. This shall be treated as if it were a 4 day trip, for purposes of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H3a">Section 25.H.3.a.</a>, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H3b">b.</a>, and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H3c">c.</a></p>
7197:          <p>In <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H4bi">Section 25.H.4.b.i.</a>, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H4bii">ii.</a>, and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H4biii">iii</a>., when the trip dropped for recurrent training is in actual conflict with the pilot’s recurrent training footprint, the pilot’s substitution window will be scheduled to touch either end of his recurrent training, unless the pilot requests otherwise and an alternative arrangement can be made. If the trip dropped due to recurrent training is not in actual conflict with the training, the SUB window will be based on the footprint of the trip dropped, rather than the recurrent training footprint.</p>
7225:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.H.5.f.i." rel="tooltip">i.</span> If a pilot is offered a substitution trip during his initial availability period, and he is not already at the airport, the showtime for that assignment shall be at least the minimum reserve report status applicable to his base, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25M3a">Section 25.M.3.a.</a> (e.g., R-1.5).</p>
7232:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.H.5.g." rel="tooltip">g.</span>   A pilot shall not be given a substitution assignment that would cause him to be illegal for his next assignment, except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H2i">Section 25.H.2.i.</a></p>
7240:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.H.6.b.i." rel="tooltip">i.</span> fails to satisfy availability or contact requirements specified in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H3">Section 25.H.3.</a>; or</p>
7249:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.H.6.c." rel="tooltip">c.</span>   A pilot may reject a substitution assignment offered other than as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H6biii">Section 25.H.6.b.iii.</a>, or in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H5b">Section 25.H.5.b.</a>, without loss of trip guarantee (i.e., night or critical flying offered to day flyer).</p>
7251:          <p>Example: A pilot in the second day of a six day substitution window is not offered a substitution assignment during his 1000-1600 LBT availability period. A 3 day trip becomes available and CRS calls the pilot at 1730 to see if the pilot would like the trip as a substitution assignment. The pilot may decline the substitution offer without loss of trip guarantee because the trip was not offered at any of the times described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H6biii">Section 25.H.6.b.iii.</a></p>
7263:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.H.7.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   A pilot may not accept a volunteer trip that operates during any portion of his substitution window, except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H8b">Section 25.H.8.b.</a>, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H8c">c.</a>, and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H8d">d.</a></p>
7267:        <p class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.H.7.e." rel="tooltip">e.</span>   If a pilot is inadvertently assigned a VLT trip in conflict with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H8">Section 25.H.8.</a> (this paragraph), he shall earn compensation for that trip at 150% of his normal pay rate, or be notified of removal prior to block-out.</p>
7277:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.H.10.b.i." rel="tooltip">i.</span> If a pilot accepts a reassignment trip he shall earn the higher of trip guarantee for the original trip(s) or trip guarantee for the reassignment trip, calculated as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4M1">Section 4.M.1.</a> (Reassignment Trip Pay). That pilot shall be released from all substitution obligations relating to his original trip.</p>
7290:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.H.11.c." rel="tooltip">c.</span>   If, while still eligible to elect OTP, a pilot forfeits trip guarantee as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H6">Section 25.H.6.</a>, he shall be placed in OTP automatically.</p>
7302:        <p class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.I.1.f." rel="tooltip">f.</span>   he becomes qualified after the bid award closed, and as a result, did not receive a line for flying (see <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25C6">Section 25.C.6.</a>).</p>

7336:    <p>A pilot whose training requires aircraft line flying (e.g., OE, line check) and who is not currently assigned a trip that provides the required flying, may be assigned a trip(s) as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25G1">Section 25.G.1.</a> (Open Time Assignments).
