7347:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.K.1." rel="tooltip">1.</span> The Company may advance assign a reserve pilot in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25G1">Section 25.G.1.</a> (Open Time Assignments) only for the following purposes:</p>
7352:        <p class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.K.1.d." rel="tooltip">d.</span>   to cover an open base simulator support event (as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25L15">Section 25.L.15.</a>), in which case such assignment shall not be awarded prior to the end of the first twelve hours of each bid period’s open time release. Base simulator support events assigned pursuant to this paragraph (<a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25K">Section 25.K.</a>) shall be on the same voluntary only basis (i.e., pass down option available, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25M6d">Section 25.M.6.d.</a>), and the following shall apply:</p>
7359:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.K.3." rel="tooltip">3.</span> A pilot shall not be removed from an advance reserve assignment except for the reasons stated in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H2a">Section 25.H.2.a.</a>, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H2c">H.2.c.</a>, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H2f">H.2.f.</a> through H.2.j., and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25M1b">25.M.1.b.</a> Upon notification of removal from an advance reserve assignment, a pilot shall return to reserve status for any of his originally scheduled block of R-days which remain after he was notified of his removal.</p>
7360:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.K.4." rel="tooltip">4.</span> A trip assigned in advance reserve status is not eligible for bid line adjustments as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25L">Section 25.L.</a>, and is not eligible for substitution.</p>
7362:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.K.6." rel="tooltip">6.</span> A pilot shall be credited toward leveling upon assignment as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4H">Section 4.H.</a></p>

7401:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.L.4.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   He shall remain in OTP status until the close of the final bid period of pay protection as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4N1">Section 4.N.1.</a> (PMU Trip Pay).</p>
7406:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.L.4.f." rel="tooltip">f.</span>   An OTP pilot’s eligibility for volunteer shall be governed by <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H8">Section 25.H.8.</a></p>
7410:      <p>A pilot shall have the ability to submit for a specific trip(s) or standby(s) from open time (as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25G2">Section 25.G.2.</a>) to make up eligible PNP hours as follows:</p>
7418:        <p id="link_256a" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.L.6.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   A pilot shall have the ability to submit for a specific trip(s) or standby(s) from open time (as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25G2">Section 25.G.2.</a>) to make up eligible credit hours. These submissions, along with trip trades, will be processed in the order received.</p>
7419:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.L.6.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span>   A pilot may submit for an assignment (as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25G2">Section 25.G.2.</a>) to make up eligible credit hours.</p>
7436:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.L.6.g." rel="tooltip">g.</span>   A pilot entitled to make up an R-day(s) will have an R-day value added to his make-up eligibility for each R-day. He shall make up that R-day(s) in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25L6a">Section 25.L.6.a.</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25L6b">b.</a></p>
7439:      <p>Submissions for AFB shall be administered as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25L6">Section 25.L.6.</a></p>
7442:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.L.8.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   A pilot shall have the ability to submit to trade his trip(s) for another trip(s) in open time. The net effect of any trade(s) in a bid period (including similar footprint trades, as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25L8b">Section 25.L.8.b.</a> may not increase his BLG, as published, by more than 12 CH.</p>
7466:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.L.9.a.iii." rel="tooltip">iii.</span>   A trip trade between pilots may be processed when received, notwithstanding <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25L1a">Section 25.L.1.a.</a></p>
7467:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.L.9.a.iv." rel="tooltip">iv.</span>    A mutual bump shall be subject to the provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25L11">Section 25.L.11.</a></p>
7486:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.L.10.c." rel="tooltip">c.</span>   Submissions for a trip pick-up may be processed when received, notwithstanding <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25L1a">Section 25.L.1.a.</a></p>
7494:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.L.11.a.iii." rel="tooltip">iii.</span>  is bumped under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_9A2">Section 9.A.2.</a></p>
7501:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.L.11.b.iv" rel="tooltip">iv.</span> The pilot operating the trip shall earn per diem, international override and overage, if applicable. He shall earn deviation credit for the trip, if applicable, except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_9A2">Section 9.A.2.</a> (management bump).</p>
7522:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.L.14.a.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    a trip pick-up as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25L10">Section 25.L.10.</a></p>
7554:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.M.1.c." rel="tooltip">c.</span>   If a reserve assignment operationally extends more than 2 hours into a pilot’s day off, he shall accrue reserve overage (as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4BB8b">Section 4.BB.8.b.</a>), and shall have the ability to drop a subsequent R-day, if any, in the current bid period without pay. CRS shall make reasonable efforts to accommodate a pilot’s request as to the subsequent R-day to be dropped. Such R-day shall be at the beginning or end of a block of R-days remaining on his line, unless the pilot agrees otherwise.</p>
7563:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.M.1.f.i." rel="tooltip">i.</span> trip canceled (<a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H2a">Section 25.H.2.a.</a>);</p>
7564:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.M.1.f.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    trip revised to extend more than two hours into his day off, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25M1b">Section 25.M.1.b.</a>;</p>
7565:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.M.1.f.iii." rel="tooltip">iii.</span>   early show without notice (<a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H2c">Section 25.H.2.c.</a>);</p>
7566:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.M.1.f.iv." rel="tooltip">iv.</span>    weather restrictions (<a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H2f">Section 25.H.2.f.</a>);</p>
7567:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.M.1.f.v." rel="tooltip">v.</span> FAR or other governmental authority (<a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H2g">Section 25.H.2.g.</a>);</p>
7568:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.M.1.f.vi." rel="tooltip">vi.</span>    Contract limitations (<a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H2h">Section 25.H.2.h.</a>);</p>
7569:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.M.1.f.vii." rel="tooltip">vii.</span>   Operational conflict (<a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H2i">Section 25.H.2.i.</a>);</p>
7570:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.M.1.f.viii." rel="tooltip">viii.</span>  Duplicate or other assignment error, as defined in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25AA1">Section 25.AA.1.</a></p>
7596:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.M.2.b.i." rel="tooltip">i.</span> RP-24 lines (minimum as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25D3e">Section 25.D.3.e.</a>), and at least one of the following:</p>
7605:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.M.3.a.i." rel="tooltip">i.</span> Pilots on R-1.5 status must be given at least 1:30 hours’ notice prior to the showtime of any assignment. However, an R-1.5 pilot on a RP-A (or an RP-A+ if an Operational Emergency has been declared under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12A3">Section 12.A.3.</a>) may be given 1 hour notice prior to showtime if there is no airport standby pilot who could be given the assignment, and the pilot is given late call parking. For purposes of this Agreement, the parking lot in the Flight Operations areas in Anchorage is late call parking. Memphis, and any future bases, shall either have designated late call parking or this provision will not apply.</p>
7620:            <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.M.3.a.vi.(d)" rel="tooltip">(d)</span>  Any assignment to base hotel standby shall be made in leveling order, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25M6">Section 25.M.6.</a> An R-24 pilot shall not be assigned to a base airport standby without first having been assigned to base hotel standby.</p>
7657:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.M.3.d.v." rel="tooltip">v.</span> If a reserve pilot is assigned 2 reserve trips with showtimes in different RPs, his RP for the balance of the block of R-days shall be the RP applicable to the second trip, unless his RP subsequently is changed as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25M3d">Section 25.M.3.d.</a> (this paragraph).</p>
7659:          <p id="link_25M3dvii" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.M.3.d.vii." rel="tooltip">vii.</span> If a pilot’s RP is changed, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25M3d">Section 25.M.3.d.</a>, the pilot shall receive 1:30 CH disruption pay in addition to RLG.</p>
7681:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.M.5.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span>   A reserve pilot shall accrue leveling credit as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#section4">Section 4.</a></p>
7690:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.M.5.d." rel="tooltip">d.</span>   The reserve assignment lists shall be updated, and may be viewed by pilots in VIPS, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25A7">Section 25.A.7.</a></p>
7691:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.M.5.e." rel="tooltip">e.</span>   Reserve assignments shall be made in order of reserve leveling except as provided otherwise in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25K">Section 25.K.</a> (advance reserve assignment) and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25M6">25.M.6.</a> (reserve open time assignments).</p>
7709:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.M.6.c." rel="tooltip">c.</span>   Notwithstanding <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25M6a">Section 25.M.6.a.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25M6b">b.</a> (leveling order):</p>
7711:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.M.6.c.i." rel="tooltip">i.</span> Reserves who elected the “first fly” option as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25M4">Section 25.M.4.</a> shall be assigned in seniority order, prior to pilots who have not elected that option, until they have accrued 75% of RLG. A “first fly” reserve pilot who has met or exceeded 75% of RLG shall thereafter be assigned without regard to “first fly.” The 75% limitation shall not apply to R-days that are part of a mini-RLG.</p>
7712:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.M.6.c.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>    The Company may assign a reserve outside of leveling order to satisfy FAR minimum block hour requirements following training for a new crew position, and pilot proficiency requirements. The pilot shall also have the ability to submit a PDO bump to satisfy such requirements, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25L11a">Section 25.L.11.a.</a> Such submissions shall be granted if CRS determines that the pilot is not on target to meet proficiency or consolidation requirements and that the trip requested is an appropriate means of addressing that issue.</p>
7714:        <p id="link_25M6d" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.M.6.d." rel="tooltip">d.</span>    In the event that a reserve pilot is assigned a base simulator support event (as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25L15">Section 25.L.15.</a>), in normal leveling (non-“first SIM”) order, he may elect to “pass down” that assignment to a pilot lower on the leveling list. If all eligible reserve pilots have elected to “pass down” a base simulator support event, such activity shall not be assigned to a reserve.</p>
7722:        <p id="link_25M6h" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.M.6.h." rel="tooltip">h.</span>    To facilitate reserve assignments, CRS may remove 1 R-day from the beginning or end of a subsequently scheduled block of R-days in the same bid period and add that day to the end of a reserve pilot’s current block of R-days in order to complete a reserve assignment. No more than 1 R-day per line, per bid period, may be moved without a pilot’s approval. A reserve trip must begin on an originally scheduled R-day. A pilot subject to the provisions of this paragraph shall receive 3 CH disruption pay in addition to his RLG. This paragraph shall not apply unless the reserve assignment could not be assigned to an exact availability match, or to a reserve whose availability is one day greater than the assignment’s duration (i.e., “best fit +1”), as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25M6bi">Section 25.M.6.b.i.</a></p>
7723:        <p id="link_25M6i" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.M.6.i." rel="tooltip">i.</span>    A reserve pilot may be offered an assignment scheduled to extend beyond the end of his block of R-days. The acceptance of such an assignment is at the pilot’s option. If the pilot accepts the assignment, the portion of the trip that extended beyond his scheduled block of R-days shall be compensated as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4H9">Section 4.H.9.</a> (150% calculated like carryover trip), and the pilot’s responsibility for his remaining R-days on his reserve line shall continue. The Company shall provide a means for a pilot to declare to CRS his willingness to accept such an extension, in local base day increments.</p>
7740:      <p>VLT assignments shall be made during the open time assignment window provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25G3">Section 25.G.3.</a> as follows:</p>
7756:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.N.3.d." rel="tooltip">d.</span>   A pilot’s eligibility for a VLT trip that operates during a portion of his substitution window shall be governed by <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25H8">Section 25.H.8.</a></p>
7759:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.N.3.g." rel="tooltip">g.</span>   When a VLT assignment is revised prior to block-out and does not meet the pilot’s stated limitations in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25N1a">Section 25.N.1.a.</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25N1b">b.</a>, such VLT pilot shall be removed from the assignment and shall be compensated as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4Q2">Section 4.Q.2.</a></p>
7780:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.O.6." rel="tooltip">6.</span> When a DRF assignment is revised prior to block-out and would otherwise be eligible for substitution, such DRF pilot shall be removed from the assignment and shall be compensated as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4Q2">Section 4.Q.2.</a></p>
7783:    <p>If an open time trip cannot be assigned to a line pilot as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25G">Section 25.G.</a>, except for substitution, that trip may be assigned to a management or supervisory pilot during the period of 9 hours prior to showtime for a domestic trip or 13 hours prior to showtime for an international trip.</p>
7786:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.O.1." rel="tooltip">1.</span> The Company may remove a pilot from his assigned trip and assign him as a base replacement to another trip when CRS determines that the assignment of that trip as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25G">Section 25.G.</a> would cause a departure delay.</p>
7789:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.O.4." rel="tooltip">4.</span> If a reserve pilot is reassigned under the circumstances described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25Q1">Section 25.Q.1.</a>, he shall not be considered to be on a base replacement trip.</p>
7793:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.R.1." rel="tooltip">1.</span> The Company may offer a field emergency assignment to a pilot not currently on a trip to replace another pilot who is unable to complete his trip in progress, if that pilot cannot be replaced as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25G">Section 25.G.</a></p>
7802:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.R.4." rel="tooltip">4.</span> A field emergency pilot shall be provided his choice of business jumpseat or an appropriate class of deadhead travel, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_8A3">Section 8.A.3.</a>, to return to his original point of departure at the completion of the trip.</p>
7807:      <p id="link_25S2" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.S.2." rel="tooltip">2.</span>   Trips in the following pay codes are eligible for disruption compensation: TRP, SON, SWP, M/U, MUV, MUD, MUS, PDO, PNP, AFB, and CIA. If a pilot’s eligible trip results in a disruption, the pilot shall receive disruption pay, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4W">Section 4.W.</a>, in addition to all other compensation for that trip. The pilot must operate the disruption in order to receive the corresponding pay.</p>
7817:            <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.S.2.a.ii.(c)." rel="tooltip">(c)</span>  during a duty period that was paid as an extra duty period as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4Y">Section 4.Y.</a>;</p>
7835:          <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.S.2.c.iii." rel="tooltip">iii.</span>   Cancellation of a layover (e.g., trip with one layover becomes an out and back with no layover (this is a duty period disruption under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25S2bi">Section 25.S.2.b.i.</a>), or a multiple layover trip has fewer layovers due to returning to base early).</p>
7838:            <p>Determining whether more than 50% of the layovers have changed (for purposes of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25S">Section 25.S.</a>) will be determined in accordance with the following methodology:</p>
7851:        <p>A single layover disruption for a trip occurs if a domestic trip (including a <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1ci">Section 12.D.1.c.i.</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1cii">ii.</a> trip), as awarded/assigned, is scheduled for a single layover but actually operates as a domestic trip with a single layover to a different airport, as determined by the airport identifier.</p>
7857:    <p>If a pilot’s duty period is extended beyond operational limits (as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12C5">Section 12.C.5</a>. or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D6">12.D.6.</a>), by the Vice President, Flight Operations, or his designee, or the pilot voluntarily extends beyond such limits as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D6bii">Section 12.D.6.b.ii.</a>, such pilot shall receive FAR extension pay in addition to all other compensation as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4X">Section 4.X.</a> (FAR Extension Pay).</p>
7872:    <p>Trips in the following pay codes are eligible for extra duty period pay: TRP, SON, SWP, M/U, MUV, MUD, MUS, PDO, PNP, AFB, and CIA. If the actual number of duty periods operated in a pilot’s eligible trip exceeds the number of duty periods scheduled when the pilot was awarded the trip, the pilot shall be compensated extra duty period pay (3:30 CH at his normal pay rate for each additional duty period), in addition to all other compensation, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4Y">Section 4.Y.</a></p>
7876:      <p class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.V.2." rel="tooltip">2.</span> If all scheduled duty periods can be paired with actual duty periods using <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25V1">Section 25.V.1.</a>, then all unpaired duty periods are “extra duty periods;”</p>
7895:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.X.5." rel="tooltip">5.</span> Contract requirements and guidance pertaining to long-term periods of service (more than 30 days) are found in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_13D">Section 13.D.</a></p>
7919:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.Y.3.c." rel="tooltip">c.</span>   Call-in jury service that becomes in-person jury service shall be treated in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25Y3a">Section 25.Y.3.a.</a></p>
7925:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.Z.1." rel="tooltip">1.</span> In the event of a death in a pilot’s immediate family (spouse, child, parent, sister, brother, father-in-law, mother-in-law, grandparent, or grandchild, including half and current step relations), the pilot, after notifying the Company of the decedent’s name, address, relationship to the pilot, and date of death, shall receive bereavement absence with pay for a maximum of 3 consecutive days. The 3 days shall begin within 7 days after the date of death. Pay for bereavement absence shall be as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_4I8c">Section 4.I.8.c.</a></p>
7945:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.AA.3.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   If operational circumstances permit, such pilot shall be removed from the assignment and it shall be reassigned to the pilot who should have received the assignment, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25AA2a">Section 25.AA.2.a.</a></p>
7953:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.AA.5.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25AA">Section 25.AA.</a> shall not apply to pilots in substitution or reserve status.</p>
7954:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.AA.5.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span>   <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25AA">Section 25.AA.</a> shall be applied one time for each qualifying error. If a single assignment error results in several pilots receiving different trips than they would have received but for the error, the provisions of this paragraph only apply to the pilot who received the first trip in error, and the pilot who was denied the first trip due to the error.</p>
7958:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.AA.6.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   A pilot shall have the ability to submit for a compensatory make-up assignment in the same manner as for regular make-up assignments as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25L6">Section 25.L.6.</a></p>

8026:      <p> The SIG shall work to ensure that the collection of SIG parameters are effective in guiding pairing generation so that the automated solutions further the goals for the SIG process as outlined in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25BBA">Section 25.BB.A.</a> To facilitate this process, there shall be two types of SIG parameters—hard parameters and soft parameters, both of which are applicable in the bid period package construction process.</p>
8029:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 25.BB.C.1.e.ii." rel="tooltip">ii.</span>  The Company may override a soft parameter(s), provided it gives at least 45 days written notice, prior to the delivery of the preliminary pairings, of its intent to do so and the reasons therefore. This notice shall be sent to the MEC Scheduling Chairman. The Association may dispute the Company’s decision via the VP/MEC Chairman track for resolution of disputes as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25BBG">Section 25.BB.G.</a> Other soft parameters may be added by agreement of the Association and the Company.</p>

8057:      <p>The construction of the monthly flight schedule is influenced by numerous groups within the Company. Promoting the closest practical coordination between the core groups responsible for the final airline schedule is essential to accomplishing the goals stated in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25BBA">Section 25.BB.A.</a> The groups most directly involved in affecting the published flight schedule are: Global Network Planning, Crew Resource Planning, Flight Management, GOC, CRS, Aircraft Acquisitions, Charter Operations, and Flight Safety.</p>

If a particular flight sequence which is the cause of a dispute appears in several pairings, those pairings shall count as one pairing for purposes of the 5%.</p>

Any changes to the Group Health Plan for Pilots can only be made as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_27A3">Section 27.A.3.</a></p>
8589:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 27.G.3." rel="tooltip">3.</span> For domestic based pilots, the Company shall provide medical benefits (including pharmacy, mental health and substance abuse benefits) under the Group Health Plan for Pilots, administered by Anthem. The Health Savings Account (HSA), as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_27N">Section 27.N.</a>, and the Health Reimbursement Account (HRA), as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_27O">Section 27.O.</a>, shall be administered by HealthEquity. Effective January 1, 2017, the Company shall provide the Plan options as described in Section 27, Appendix A. For domestic based pilots, effective January 1, 2017, the Company shall provide dental and vision benefits as described in Section 27, Appendix A (except as modified pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_27G13">Section 27.G.13.</a>).</p>
8592:      <p id="link_27G6" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 27.G.6." rel="tooltip">6.</span> The Company will provide the Association with the initial monthly contributions/premiums for all Group Health Benefits on November 2, 2015, or as soon as practicable thereafter. Beginning in 2017, in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_27A11">Section 27.A.11.</a>, those monthly contributions/ premiums for each tier of each plan shall be as follows:</p>
8641:      <p id="link_27G12" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 27.G.12." rel="tooltip">12.</span>    On January 1, 2017, the Company will offer Anthem’s Health Rewards program (wellness program) for pilots and eligible spouses enrolled in the CDHP Purple and Orange options. After completing a Health Assessment and participating in two (2) wellness programs, the pilot and the pilot’s eligible spouse will each earn $300 to be deposited in the HSA (or credited to the HRA as applicable) annually (as soon as practicable after January 1). All information and data submitted by a pilot or a pilot’s spouse related to Health Assessments and wellness programs shall be protected health information that shall not be used by the Company or Anthem for any purpose other than administration of the Group Health Plan for Pilots. The entire cost of amounts earned under this <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_27G12">Section 27.G.12.</a> shall be borne by the Company and shall not be included in total projected costs or actual costs under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_27G6">Section 27.G.6.</a></p>
8656:      <p id="link_27G16" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 27.G.16." rel="tooltip">16.</span>    The Group Health Plan for Pilots shall provide that determination of the premiums/contributions to be paid by a pilot’s survivors for health coverage (assuming the survivors are eligible for survivor health coverage under the foregoing provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_27G">Section 27.G.</a>) shall be as follows, where the pilot’s survivors, prior to the pilot’s death, were covered, along with the pilot, as a single group under a single coverage tier. The Company will provide survivor health coverage, under the foregoing provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_27G">Section 27.G.</a> to all of the eligible survivors as a single group under a single coverage tier. The Company will send one information packet to the surviving spouse; if there is not a surviving spouse, the packet will be sent to the oldest child. If all survivors agree on a single coverage tier, only one survivor (the surviving spouse if there is one, otherwise the oldest child) will be charged for the coverage. If all the survivors cannot agree on a single coverage tier, then the survivors will divide themselves into as many separate groups as desired, with the goal of having the least number of coverage groups possible. Each coverage group will be charged for coverage at the applicable rate for that group’s coverage tier. For each coverage group, only one survivor (the surviving spouse if there is one, otherwise the oldest child in the coverage group) will be charged for the coverage. An adult survivor may elect to leave a coverage group and elect either to maintain coverage at the rate applicable to the survivor as an individual (assuming the survivor continues to be eligible for survivor health coverage) or to maintain no coverage, but once an adult survivor elects to leave a coverage group, he or she may not elect to return to that coverage.</p>
8660:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 27.H.1." rel="tooltip">1.</span> The Company shall provide medical benefits (including pharmacy, mental health and substance abuse benefits), dental benefits and vision benefits to pilots who have retired on or after February 4, 1999, and their eligible covered spouses and dependents, and their eligible survivors, in accordance with the terms of the Federal Express Corporation Retiree Group Health Plan for Pilots. A pilot must comply with the requirements of the Retiree Group Health Plan for Pilots or lose or risk losing coverage. Any changes to the Retiree Group Health Plan for Pilots can only be made as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_27A3">Section 27.A.3.</a></p>
8670:        <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 27.H.3.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   The Retiree Group Health Plan for Pilots shall provide coverage solely for the retiring pilot and/or his eligible spouse and dependents for the period prior to their attaining Medicare eligibility age. Retiring pilots who have attained Medicare eligibility age may, if eligible, elect coverage under the Premium Reimbursement Plan described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_27I">Section 27.I.</a></p>
8709:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 27.H.9." rel="tooltip">9.</span> The Retiree Group Health Plan for Pilots shall be amended to provide changes consistent with the changes to the Group Health Plan for Pilots provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_27G14">Section 27.G.14.</a> (regarding benefit modifications), <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_27G15">Section 27.G.15.</a> (regarding transparency systems), and <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_27G16">Section 27.G.16.</a> (regarding survivors’ premiums/contributions). In addition, the Buy Up Option, CDHP Purple Option (Without HSA/HRA) and CDHP Orange Option (Without HSA/HRA) under the Retiree Group Health Plan for Pilots shall be amended to provide the same changes as are made to the Buy Up Option, CDHP Purple Option and CDHP Orange Option under the Group Health Plan for Pilots pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_27A11">Section 27.A.11.</a>, whether or not such changes affect application of the Excise Tax to the options under the Retiree Group Health Plan for Pilots.</p>
8739:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 27.I.9." rel="tooltip">9.</span> With the exception of the remittance of contributions on behalf of pilots as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_27I3">Section 27.I.3.</a> above, the Company will have no administrative responsibility for the PRP and/or VEBA. However, the Company will provide to the Board such relevant data as is readily available from the Company’s records (or its vendors’ records) and which is necessary or appropriate for the Administrative Board’s proper administration of the PRP.</p>
8746:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 27.J.2." rel="tooltip">2.</span> A pilot shall be eligible for LTD Plan benefits upon exhaustion of his regular and disability sick accounts, as described in Section 14, or upon his experiencing a seat change or upon moving to a non-pilot position because of disability, as described in the LTD Plan. Except as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_27J7">Section 27.J.7.</a>, disability benefits paid to pilots who are disabled prior to October 30, 2006, shall be governed by the terms of the disability plans in effect on the date of commencement of the disability. Pilots who become disabled on or after October 30, 2006, shall be governed by the provisions below.</p>
8747:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 27.J.3." rel="tooltip">3.</span> LTD Plan benefits payable to a pilot whose disability commences on or after October 30, 2006, shall equal 60% of monthly earnings, as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_27J6">Section 27.J.6.</a>, for the first 24 months that a pilot is eligible to receive benefits under the LTD Plan, subject to the limits in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_27J7">Section 27.J.7.</a> Thereafter, benefits payable to a pilot who becomes disabled and continues to have an occupational disability shall equal 50% of monthly earnings, as described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_27J6">Section 27.J.6.</a>, and subject to the limits in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_27J7">Section 27.J.7.</a> Such benefits shall be paid through the earlier of the date on which such pilot (1) ceases to be disabled, or (2) the date on which the pilot attains age 65.</p>
8751:      <p id="link_27J7" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 27.J.7." rel="tooltip">7.</span> A pilot’s monthly LTD Plan benefit during the first 24 months of disability may not exceed 60% of the monthly compensation limit set forth in Code § 401(a)(17). A pilot’s monthly LTD Plan benefit following the first 24 months of disability may not exceed 50% of the monthly compensation limit set forth in Code § 401(a)(17). Increases to this limit shall be indexed based on periodic adjustments to the limitations of Code § 401(a)(17). The benefit amount adjustments made under this <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_27J7">Section 27.J.7.</a> are not intended to be one-time adjustments; rather, adjustments will continue to be made in the future, for benefits paid thereafter, at the time of future adjustments to the limitations of Code § 401(a)(17). This <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_27J7">Section 27.J.7.</a> shall apply to all pilots, whether their benefits began before or after the signing of this Agreement. In the event the limit set forth in Code § 401(a)(17) is decreased legislatively, the Company shall establish a VEBA to cover pilots in the LTD Plan only. Compensation used to calculate benefits to be paid from the newly established VEBA shall be limited annually to the greater of (1) the highest limit under Code § 401(a)(17) in effect at any time prior to it being decreased or (2) the current limit in effect under Code § 401(a)(17).</p>
8760:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 27.J.15." rel="tooltip">15.</span>    LTD benefits shall be reduced by other benefits and income received during the disability period, as described in the LTD Plan except: (i) as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_27J13">Section 27.J.13.</a>, and (ii) the amount of a pilot’s Social Security Disability Income which shall be offset from his LTD benefits in an amount equal to 70% (100% with respect to disabilities commencing prior to October 30, 2006) of the Social Security Disability Income payable to the pilot (excluding any amount payable to the pilot on account of any member of the pilot’s family).</p>
8765:      <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 27.J.20." rel="tooltip">20.</span>    The Company’s agreement with the current administrator (Aetna Life Insurance Company) of LTD Plan benefits under <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_27J">Section 27.J.</a> will provide that at any time such entity is also the administrator of benefits under any FDX MEC-sponsored disability plan, a pilot may elect to direct the administrator in writing to share amongst the Federal Express Corporation LTD Plan for Pilots and the FDX MEC sponsored disability plan any and all medical records or medical reports received from any current treating providers, with respect to any one of such plans. Regardless of the sharing of information, each plan shall be administered independently according to its specific plan provisions and procedures and there shall be no collaboration between the Federal Express Corporation LTD Plan for Pilots Plan Administrator and the FDX MEC sponsored Disability Plan Administrator in claims payment decisions under each plan. The pilot must sign and date an Authorization to Share Information Form, approved by both FedEx and the FDX MEC. The pilot is required to provide an updated Authorization to Share Information Form as required by Aetna Life Insurance Company. At any time such entity is not Aetna Life Insurance Company for both the Federal Express Corporation LTD Plan for Pilots and the FDX MEC sponsored disability plan, information will not be shared unless the Company is able to negotiate the same arrangement with the new vendor.</p>

9600:  <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 29.A.3." rel="tooltip">3.</span> If a pilot covered by this Agreement is delinquent, or becomes delinquent in the payment of fees, dues and assessments or the service charge as stated in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_29A1">Section 29.A.1.</a>, the Association will notify him with a copy to the Vice President, Flight Operations, or his designee, and the designated Company official in Labor Relations, that the pilot is delinquent and not complying with contract requirements and may be subject to separation from employment. Such letter will also notify the pilot that he must remit the required payment within a grace period of 15 days or risk being separated from employment.</p>
9605:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 29.A.4.c." rel="tooltip">c.</span>   Within 30 days of receipt of such notification the Vice President, Flight Operations, or his designee, and the designated Company official in Labor Relations, will give the pilot written notification of his employment status as a pilot. Any separation will automatically be held in abeyance for 10 days from the postmark date of mailing of the notification. If the pilot files an appeal in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_29A4di">Section 29.A.4.d.i.</a>, the separation will be further held in abeyance pending the exhaustion of the appeal process in this Section. A pilot who is sent a separation notice will be placed on an unpaid personal leave of absence until the appeal process is final.</p>

Notice to the Company shall be sent to the Vice President, Flight Operations, or his designee, and the designated Company official in Labor Relations, as set forth in the provisions of this Agreement. Notice to ALPA shall be sent to the Vice President - Finance, 535 Herndon Parkway, Herndon, VA 20170. Notice to pilots shall be sent to a pilot’s permanent, primary address. As provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_26N2">Section 26.N.2.</a>, a pilot must keep his permanent, primary address current. Such information shall be shared electronically with the Association pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_26R">Section 26.R.</a> and will be used for correspondence under this section. The notice of delinquency under this paragraph will be deemed to be received by the pilot on the fifth day after its postmark date of mailing, when mailed by the Association by Certified Mail, Return Receipt Requested, or by FedEx Overnight Letter, to such pilot’s permanent, primary address.</p>

9685:    <p id="link_31C2a" class="link_highlight"><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 31.C.2.a." rel="tooltip">a.</span>   In order for the Company to reopen the Agreement early pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_31C2">Section 31.C.2.</a>, the Company must deliver written notice of early reopening to the Association’s MEC Chairman. In no event, however, shall either party deliver a written notice of early reopening pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_31C2a">Section 31.C.2.a.</a> to the other party during the October or November bid periods.</p>
9686:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 31.C.2.b." rel="tooltip">b.</span>   If either party elects to exercise early reopening of this Agreement pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_31C2">Section 31.C.2.</a>, the Agreement shall become amendable on the 180th day following the delivery of a party’s written notice of early reopening to the other party.</p>
9687:    <p><span class="tooltipline" title="Section 31.C.2.c." rel="tooltip">c.</span>   The parties shall initiate negotiations required by Section 6, Title I of the Railway Labor Act, as amended, within 30 days of the delivery of a notice of early reopening in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_31C2a">Section 31.C.2.a.</a></p>
9743:    <p>2. The down/lateral bid restrictions set forth in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24F1">Section 24.F.1.</a> of the basic Agreement shall be waived with respect to pilots bidding for FDA crew positions.</p>
9763:      <p id="link_FDAB4d" class="link_highlight">d. The crew position of a pilot who was released from his FDA crew position award as described in Paragraph B.4.c. of this LOA shall be determined as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_13A6bii">Section 13.A.6.b.ii.</a> of the basic Agreement as if the pilot had been on a leave of absence when the System Bid on which he was awarded his FDA crew position closed. Such pilot’s assignment (as that term is defined in Section 24) to a new crew position and assignment (as that term is defined in Section 24) to an ITU training date/slot (if any such training is required) shall not generate an SDP or an inverse SDP for any pilot.</p>
9773:      <p>a. Relocation benefits as described in Section 6 of the basic Agreement, except that <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6E1e">Section 6.E.1.e.</a> (FDA Bonus) shall be inapplicable.</p>
9789:        <p>i. A pilot shall be entitled to expenses associated with the storage of his household goods in the location of his pre-FDA domestic residence (i.e., his permanent, primary residence immediately preceding his assignment to the FDA) or, if approved in advance by the Relocation Department, a different domestic location involving no greater cost to the Company (using the cost of storage in the pilot’s pre-FDA domestic location as the reference point). Reimbursement shall not exceed $4,000 per year and the storage must be at a commercial storage provider. In addition, the Company will assume the cost of packing such goods (subject to the standard limitations regarding the types of goods to be shipped/stored, which are catalogued in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6C1b">Section 6.C.1.b.</a>), and the cost of transporting them to and from the storage facility (local transportation only). Requests for reimbursement of storage fees must be submitted within 90 days of the date the expense was incurred, in accordance with the Company’s standard procedures concerning expense reporting.</p>
9858:          <p>(e)    Any air travel expenses in excess of the balance of the pilot’s FDA air travel expense bank shall be remitted to the Company by payroll deduction, as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_3E1avi">Section 3.E.1.a.vi.</a>, from the pay check on the 15th of the month following the pilot’s purchase of air travel tickets authorized by this paragraph.</p>
9870:        <p>In the event that an FDA pilot is furloughed or assigned (as that term is defined in Section 24) to a crew position in a different geographic location, he shall be entitled to the relocation benefits set forth in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6E2bii">Section 6.E.2.b.ii.</a> or <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6E2biii">iii.</a> of the basic Agreement (as appropriate).</p>
9885:        <p>iii. For all household goods shipments, this benefit shall include the cost of packing such goods, subject to the standard limitations regarding the types of goods to be shipped/stored, which are catalogued in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6C1b">Section 6.C.1.b.</a> of the basic Agreement, and the cost of transporting them as described above.</p>
9888:        <p>vi.  Delayed household goods shipments shall be handled in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6C1a">Section 6.C.1.a.</a> of the basic Agreement.</p>
9895:        <p>ii. In extraordinary circumstances, an additional day(s) may be approved by the Vice President, Flight Operations, or his designee. Any additional day(s) not approved by the Company shall be at the pilot’s expense. A pilot may use his Company credit card to pay for any additional day(s) and the amount of the expenditure will be recovered through payroll deduction as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_3E1aiv">Section 3.E.1.a.iv.</a> of the basic Agreement.</p>
9912:        <p>vi. The pilot/lessee shall manage his rental property in such a way as to minimize the amount, if any, withheld by the landlord/lessor. Absent extraordinary circumstances (e.g., failure to pay rent, photographically documented damage beyond normal wear and tear), the Company shall not seek reimbursement from the pilot with respect to deposit funds withheld by the pilot’s landlord/lessor. Any reimbursements due from the pilot to the Company owing to reduced deposit assistance refunds shall be treated as adjustments or reimbursements as provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_3E1avi">Section 3.E.1.a.vi.</a> of the basic Agreement. The Company shall not discipline or counsel the pilot with respect to deposit funds withheld by the pilot’s landlord/lessor.</p>
9921:        <p>iv.<a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6A8">Section 6.A.8.</a> of the basic Agreement shall apply to pilots who relocate prior to activation.</p>
9927:      <p>An FDA pilot whose employment with the Company is terminated due to retirement, voluntary resignation, or disciplinary discharge (for misconduct other than that described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6E2biv">Section 6.E.2.b.iv.</a> of the basic Agreement) shall be eligible for the same return relocation benefits that he would be eligible for if he was relocating from the FDA as a result of an award to a new crew position.</p>
9928:      <p>If an FDA pilot’s employment with the Company is terminated due to misconduct described in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6E2biv">Section 6.E.2.b.iv.</a> of the basic Agreement, the terms and conditions of that provision shall apply, regardless of whether the pilot elected the Enhanced Option or the Existing CBA Option at the beginning of his assignment to the FDA.</p>
9979:      <p>d. An FDA pilot transitioning to a non-FDA crew position who does not elect the “Early Exit Option” shall be entitled to “relocation days off” following his activation date in his new crew position in accordance with the provisions of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6F">Section 6.F.</a> of the basic Agreement.</p>
9993:    <p>4.   In order to facilitate tax compliance in the country where the pilot’s permanent, primary residence is located, and consistent with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_26N2">Section 26.N.2.</a> of the basic Agreement, FDA pilots shall update their permanent, primary residence address in the applicable Company computer system as necessary.</p>
10027:  <p>Provided he otherwise qualifies, a pilot formerly assigned to the SFS FDA may elect to take his FDA move back provided in <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_6E2b">Section 6.E.2.b.</a> of the basic Agreement, prior to his activation into the FDA. Once moved back to the United States, a pilot who selects the “Enhanced Option” may take advantage of the household goods storage provided in Paragraph C.2.c. of this LOA.</p>
10046:      <p>b. Trains may be used in FDAs pursuant to <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_8A3c">Section 8.A.3.c.</a> of the basic Agreement to the same extent as other modes of transportation mentioned therein, not to exceed 7 hours measured from scheduled departure time to scheduled arrival. Such train travel shall be booked in the highest class of service that is readily accessible to the public. If the train lacks the minimum two class configuration or a higher class is not available, train travel may be used only less than 4 hours, measured from scheduled departure time to scheduled arrival, unless waived by the pilot.</p>
10054:      <p>a. With respect to ground transportation between <a id="_idTextAnchor647"></a>HKG-CAN and CGN-FRA, <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_8B1b">Section 8.B.1.b.</a> of t<a id="_idTextAnchor648"></a>he basic Agreement is waived.</p>
10064:  <p>A pilot activated in an EMEA FDA crew position shall have the ability to expense up to $40/trip for ground transportation expenses (e.g., public train/subway/bus/taxi) to/from CGN in lieu of airport parking in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_5F">Section 5.F.</a> of the basic Agreement. Reimbursement shall be limited to the pilot’s actual cost (receipt(s) required) of ground transportation to/from the FDA base airport in conjunction with a trip.</p>
10069:    <p>3.   In accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25A2">Section 25.A.2.</a> of the basic Agreement, the CGN FDA local base day shall begin at 0215 LBT.</p>
10070:    <p>4.   Training conducted outside of 100 nm of the HKG Special Administrative Region (“HKG SAR”) shall be considered and treated as off-site training in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_11E1g">Section 11.E.1.g.</a> of the basic Agreement. If a pilot is assigned to a training event in Zhuhai, China, the pilot may expense the reasonable and customary cost of transportation between HKG and the training location in Zhuhai, as well as hotel accommodations at the contract hotel in Zhuhai. The number of nights shall be at least equal to the number of day(s) of training.</p>
10087:        <p>ii.  The pilot’s preferred exit date (i.e., the date upon which the pilot desires to start ITU training for or base transfer to his selected crew position), which shall be no earlier than 4 years and no later than 4 years and 11 months following the earlier of the pilot’s activation date in his FDA crew position or his registration with local immigration authorities. The Company shall assign the pilot to an ITU training start date or a base transfer activation date (subject to the applicable contractual provisions concerning the timing of base transfers, e.g., <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25C6">Section 25.C.6.</a>), which shall not be less than 90 days from the date of the pilot’s election.</p>
10090:      <p>b. If the pilot does not make this election, the Company shall assign the pilot to a crew position in a different geographic location in which he would not be the junior awarded/assigned pilot in that crew position. This shall occur at 4 years and 3 months following the earlier of the pilot’s activation date in his FDA crew position or his registration with local immigration authorities. A pilot assigned to another crew position pursuant to this subparagraph may be assigned an ITU training start date or a base transfer activation date (subject to the applicable contractual provisions concerning the timing of base transfers, e.g., <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_25C6">Section 25.C.6.</a>) consistent with Company staffing requirements. The Company shall provide the pilot with a minimum of 60 days’ notice prior to the ITU training start date or base transfer activation date<a id="_idTextAnchor665"></a>.</p>
10091:      <p id="link_FDAN2c" class="link_highlight">c. Referrals to the Company’s aeromedical advisor pursuant to this paragraph shall not be considered a violation of <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_15D1">Section 15.D.1.</a> of the basic Agreement.</p>

The phrase “FDA theatre of operations” does not refer to the “European theater” in Section <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_12D1cii">12.D.1.c.ii.</a> of the basic Agreement.</p>

10181:    <p>2.   for at least an additional 2 years beyond the pilot’s commitment period (for HKG FDA pilots), at which time his New Hire Junior Activation Compensation repayment obligations, if any, shall be determined in accordance with <a target="_blank" href="http://fdx.alpa.org/portals/26/docs/2015_Contract/2015FDXCBA_web.html#link_24F8">Section 24.F.8.</a> of the basic Agreement.</p>
